## []{#ch01.xhtml#page_10 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 1]{.f3} {#ch01.xhtml#ch01 .h2n}

## YOUR BIRTHDAY CODE {.h2t}

[O]{.dropcap}[N THE DAY YOU WERE BORN, YOU ACTIVATED A MAGNIFICENT BIRTH
CODE]{.f3}. This Birth Code is the blueprint to your soul, the
translation of your soul contract for this lifetime. Numerology, the
science of the meaning of numbers, is designed to translate the
Blueprint of your Soul to reveal your spiritual contract. This book will
give you the keys.

As you read, you will know when it resonates with you, because you'll
feel it at a soul level. You might sense a tingle down your spine or
experience delight and shivers of joy as you realize---your soul is
speaking to you through your own code!

Numbers are a gateway into developing your intuition. When you first
meet someone, you may have a gut feeling about him or her. Having access
to numbers gives you another perspective on their soul and permission to
confirm what you already []{#ch01.xhtml#page_11 .pagebreak}felt
intuitively. For example, look at the first letter of any person's first
name and you'll start understanding certain traits about who they are at
soul level (see [chapters 6](#ch06.xhtml#ch06) and
[11](#ch11.xhtml#ch11)).

Everything is energy. Everything carries a vibrational force. Every
number (and letter) is a unique vibration with a profound meaning. Just
as each musical note emits a unique frequency and sound (which can be
measured numerically), each number oscillates to a specific number of
cycles per second. Every sound, fragrance, color, and thought is a
vibration and can be measured as a number.

All the numbers aligned within one person (you), entity (business), or
family, create a code. Each sector of a code contributes to the whole
formula---a symphony of vibrant frequencies that make up all the
interconnections of your life.

This guide will reveal the mystery and magic in your codes, beginning
with the most important one, your Birth Code---the Blueprint of your
Soul. Just as importantly, this higher wisdom will give you a powerful
glimpse into other people's Soul Blueprints, thus helping you understand
them, forgive and love them unconditionally, and allow others the
freedom to find themselves in their own time and in their uniquely
designed way.

Numbers are the very essence of how life expresses itself. In
understanding your Birth Code you will discover who you truly are at
soul level, how to use your special gifts, and how you naturally
overcome obstacles to gain the wisdom and courage to fulfill your divine
mission.

Once you know and apply your Birth Code, you'll be freed from pursuing
expectations placed on you by others. What will set you free is getting
to know the True You through your Soul Blueprint. Knowing yourself
allows you to create your own reality---a reality based purely on your
alignment with spirit, rather than on unconscious motivations derived
from other people's advice and expectations.

Soul-code living begins at home---internally. You were indoctrinated to
believe certain things about yourself by external sources, and many, if
not most of those beliefs do not serve your highest good. Knowing your
Birth Code and how to apply it now and in the future will prepare and
strengthen you to manifest your true soul destiny.

When you are in alignment with your soul's Birth Code and current
cycles, you naturally align with abundance. Thus this book is designed
to elevate you to a place of joy, freedom, and a passionate
engagement---so you feel compelled to express your divine gifts at the
highest vibrational level! When you engage this way with the universe,
prosperity gravitates to you, abundance is attracted to you, and your
well-being translates into wealth of mind, body, and spirit.

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_13 .pagebreak}Numerology---the gateway to
demystifying your Soul's DNA Code---helps you start a profound
relationship with yourself that facilitates a deep connection with what
delights you. Your soul code gives you "permission" to live a life of
fulfillment, joy, and emotional integrity. A journey that is purely
empowered by the soul is a celebration of abundance.

Each person is wired differently. Just like every snowflake carries a
unique imprint, so does every human being, every soul. Our numerology
Birth Code attests to that. Your soul's Birth Code reveals the unique
ways you are designed to experience, explore, and manifest fulfillment
and abundance. Everyone has an independent way of expressing joy!

By taking ownership of the divine gifts in your Birth Code, you start
making *conscious choices* that elevate your vibration higher and
higher...

Awareness of the code comes first. Action corresponding to your code
follows. Then positive breakthroughs automatically appear, especially
when you consistently set clear intentions that are congruent with your
code.

::: group
### THE THREE IMPORTANT NUMBERS IN YOUR BIRTH CODE {.h3}

You have many numbers in your birthday and birth-certificate name.
(Every letter translates as a number too, which we will discover in
[chapter 2](#ch02.xhtml#ch02).) However, there are three numbers that
impact you the most. Throughout this manual, they will be referred to as
the Three Important Numbers in your Birth Code.
:::

The first two important numbers that define your Birth Code are both
derived from your birthday. The third important number is derived from
your birth certificate name.

Your unique Birth Code is made up of:

1\. **Your Day of Birth Number**---the day of the month you were born

2\. **Your Life Purpose Number**---the total sum of your full birth date

3\. **Your Destiny Number**---the total sum of letters in your
birth-certificate name (see [chapter 2](#ch02.xhtml#ch02))

Combined into a powerful triad, your Birth Code is a spiritual and
practical formula that is totally unique to you. (Even identical twins
do not share the same Birth Code, due to their different birth names.)

Your Birth Code unlocks the secrets of your birth promise---special
gifts, talents, your personality, the nature of your mission, and
corresponding lessons. Each of your three individual personal
frequencies describes how you think, feel, act, and experience life.
Your Three Important Birth Numbers form the basic building blocks that
make up your divine DNA code.

::: land100
[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_12
.pagebreak}![Image](./f0012-01.jpg){#f0012-01}
:::

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_15 .pagebreak}You'll refer to the Three Important
Numbers in your Birth Code in every part of your life. In fact, they are
having an impact on you right now, whether you are aware of them or not!

Later in this guide you'll discover how to use your Birth Code to create
a personal forecast map. However, in order to unlock the fortunate
Personal Days, Months and Years (intensifications of your Birth Code),
you will need to know your Three Important Birth Numbers first.

Now let's discover the first two important numbers in your Birth Code:
your Day of Birth number and Life Purpose (full birthday) numbers. Both
are derived from your birthday. Let's begin with your Day of Birth
number---the easiest to calculate!

::: group
### YOUR DAY OF BIRTH NUMBER {.h3}

Every person and entity (like a business, book or product launch, live
event, ceremony, first meeting) is born on a specific day of the month.
The Day of Birth is one of Three Important Numbers in a person's Birth
Code.
:::

The Day of Birth number gives you instant insights into someone's
natural disposition, their way of being and tendencies, w ho they are
day-to-day, moment-to-moment---even if you do not know their age. This
allows you to do a quick reading on anyone, as long as you know they
were born on the 5th, 22nd, 17th, etc.---so, regardless of whether you
know their year of birth or not, you can read this part of their Birth
Code.

::: group
#### **WHAT IS YOUR DAY OF BIRTH NUMBER?** {.h4}

If you were born on the 1st through the 9th of any month, your Day of
Birth corresponds to that number. If you are born between the 10th and
the 31st of any month, you will be impacted by one additional
double-digit number (sometimes two) along with the single-digit or "root
number." Find the root number by adding together the digits of your Day
of Birth (twice, if the result is another double-digit number). Read the
descriptions in [chapters 4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04) and [5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05)
for your Day of Birth number and your root number(s).
:::

::: group
### YOUR LIFE PURPOSE NUMBER {.h3}

Every person and entity has a birthday. Adding all the digits in a given
birthday results in the Life Purpose Number, one of the Three Important
Numbers in your Birth Code. No one has just one number in their Birth
Code, but a combination of many.
:::

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_16 .pagebreak}Your Life Purpose is a powerful
frequency revealing how you need to express your soul purpose. It
answers the following questions:

What is the main reason you are here? What is your main lesson? How are
you uniquely designed to feel happily engaged with your life? What
qualities will help you manifest the most success?

If you sense you're not on the right path, your Life Purpose number will
point you to your natural talents and abilities. You'll get a deep sense
of what makes you tick and understand why you are magnetically drawn to
certain activities, people, and goals.

Once you calculate your Life Purpose Number you'll hold the keys to your
unique purpose for being here on Earth in this lifetime. While there are
other people with whom you will share the same double-digit or
single-digit number, it is in combining all three birth numbers that
you'll get the overall big picture of who you are, what you're here to
do, and how you will best express your gifts.

::: group
#### **WHAT IS YOUR LIFE PURPOSE NUMBER?** {.h4}

The Life Purpose number is derived by adding each single-digit in a
person's full birthday. If that sum is two digits, it must then be
reduced (sometimes twice) to its single-digit "root" number. (Hint:
Anyone who is born in the 1900s will automatically have a two-digit Life
Purpose number). See [chapter 5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05) to discover the
meaning of all two-digit numbers (except "Master Numbers" 11, 22, 33,
and 44). See [chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03) to discover the meaning of
all nine single-digit numbers.
:::

This person has a **25/7** Life Purpose number.

If a person's Life Purpose number (full birthday) adds up to **19**,
**28**, **29**, **37**, **38**, **39**, **46**, **47**, or **48**, then
you must add two times before you arrive at the single-digit root
number. Read the descriptions of all three numbers for the full picture.

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_17 .pagebreak}Another example:

Let's look at six studies. Case Studies 5 and 6 are examples of
birthdays that require two calculations and result in a Life Purpose
made up of three separate numbers.

#### []{#ch01.xhtml#page_18 .pagebreak}CASE STUDY 4: OPRAH WINFREY {.h4}

::: group
### SHORT DESCRIPTIONS OF "ROOT NUMBERS" 1--9 {.h3}

Each single-digit number from 1 through 9 emits a unique vibration that
differentiates it from the other eight numbers, giving the person who
embodies it the strong characteristics and vital energy force of that
number. Knowing just the three important single-digit root numbers for
any person gives a powerful overall impression.
:::

Understanding the meaning of the single-digits in your Birth Code will
create a distinct picture, a pattern of energetic imprints that reflect
your personal instincts and general orientation towards your life,
career, health, and relationships.

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_19 .pagebreak}The following are brief descriptions
revealing the positive expression for each single-digit root number. Use
this as a quick reference guide for all Life Purpose and Day of Birth
Numbers.

To view the complete, in-depth definitions for all 31 Day of Birth
Numbers and all 48 Life Purpose Numbers, please refer to [chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03) (single-digit numbers 1--9), [chapter
4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04) (double-digit "Master Numbers" 11, 22, 33, and 44),
and [chapter 5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05) (double-digit "compound" numbers
10--48).

1

If you were born on the **1^st^** of any month--your Day of Birth Number
is 1.

**1** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of Birth
is on the **10^th^**, **19^th^**, or **28^th^** in any month.

**1** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Life Purpose
Number adds up to **10**, **19**, **28**, **37**, or **46**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are a natural and authentic
leader, an original thinker, accomplished, active, energetic, strong
willed, innovative, determined, courageous, and creative, you work best
independently, have unique ideas and approaches, have definite views,
and enjoy time alone and privacy*.

2

If you were born on the **2^nd^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **2**.

**2** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of Birth
is on the **11^th^**, **20^th^**, or **29^th^** of any month.

2 is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Life Purpose
Number adds up to **11**, **20**, **29**, **38**, or **47**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are a peace-maker, a diplomat,
imaginative, inventive, highly sensitive, healing, have a well-developed
intuition and an eye for detail are helpful, supportive, kind, romantic,
psychic (though you may keep that private), patient, cooperative, quiet,
and loving*.

3

If you were born on the 3rd of any month---your Day of Birth Number is
**3**.

**3** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of Birth
is on the **12^th^**, **21^st^**, or **30^th^** of any month.

3 is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Life Purpose
Number adds up to **12**, **21**, **30**, **39**, or **48**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are expressive, artistic,
independent, uplifting, fun, optimistic, enthusiastic, witty, and highly
creative. You want freedom in movement, speech and writing, enjoy
traveling, are a lover of Truth, can spot a lie easily, and your smile
lights up the room*.

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_20 .pagebreak}4

If you were born on the **4^th^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **4**.

**4** is also one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of
Birth is on the **13^th^**, **22^nd^**, or **31^st^** of any month or
your Life Purpose Number adds up to **13**, **22**, **31**, or **40**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are an enigma to others (and
even yourself), dependable, honest, practical, organized, disciplined,
grounded, productive, loyal, patient, devoted to family and home,
trustworthy, grounded, and not afraid of work. You make your own rules,
have unique ideas, are curious, don't believe anything is impossible,
have the gift of prophecy, and enjoy an unconventional life style*.

5

If you were born on the **5^th^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **5**.

**5** is also one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of
Birth is on the **14^th^** or **23^rd^** of any month or your Life
Purpose Number adds up to **14**, **23**, **32**, or **41**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are a seeker of freedom,
adaptable, charming, a multi-tasker, witty, adventurous, resilient,
fearless, and versatile. Have a great intellect, like change and
movement, enjoy travel, are a good salesperson, and have an active
mind*.

6

If you were born on the **6^th^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **6**.

**6** is also one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of
Birth is on the **15^th^** or **24^th^** of any month or your Life
Purpose Number adds up to **15**, **24**, **33**, or **42**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are a nurturer, artistic,
responsible, loving, creative, romantic, healing, dedicated to and loved
by your family and friends. You have a magical, magnetic presence; love
art and music, beauty, and tasteful surroundings; and crave
harmony---you are allergic to disagreements and conflict, exhibit good
manners and are fond of luxury, and must feel you are being of service
in some way*.

7

If you were born on the **7^th^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **7**.

**7** is also one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of
Birth is on the **16^th^** or **25^th^** of any month or your Life
Purpose Number adds up to **16**, **25**, **34**, or **43**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are spiritual or scientific,
sensitive, dignified, wise, quiet, private, analytical, have a refined
mind, are knowledge driven and wise, a truth-seeker, work best alone,
don't follow the beaten path, love to read, have unique beliefs about
religion and politics, are interested in mystical or rare subjects, need
to be in touch with nature on a regular basis, and delve into the
mysteries of the universe*.

[]{#ch01.xhtml#page_21 .pagebreak}8

If you were born on the **8^th^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **8**.

**8** is also one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of
Birth is on the **17^th^** or **26^th^** of any month or your Life
Purpose Number adds up to **17**, **26**, **35**, or **44**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are efficient, determined,
abundant, a leader, ambitious, athletic, healthy, powerful, influential,
a visionary, reserved, responsible, strong and disciplined. You have
good judgement, use time wisely, and excel at activities requiring
dedication, patience, and intelligent deduction*.

9

If you were born on the **9^th^** of any month---your Day of Birth
Number is **9**.

**9** is also one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Day of
Birth is on the **18^th^** or **27^th^** of any month or your Life
Purpose Number adds up to **18**, **27**, **36**, or **45**.

*When you are energetically aligned, you are compassionate, wise,
influential, artistic, magnetic, humanitarian, unconditionally loving,
courageous, trusting, generous, creative, charitable, idealistic, and
romantic. You can penetrate to the heart of a situation and want to make
a difference in the world*.

::: group
### THE REMAINING BIRTH CODE NUMBER {.h3}

You now know how to calculate two of your Three Important Birth Numbers,
powerful indicators of who you are at soul level. In fact, you can now
"get a read" on *anyone*---friends, family, and strangers---quickly once
they share their birthday with you. Just knowing a person's Day of Birth
gives you instant insights to help you tune in to their nature and
inclinations.
:::

While you can change your current name throughout your life, your
birthday and birth-certificate name are a permanent imprint of your soul
code that lasts for a lifetime. So, these Three Important Numbers in
your Birth Code never change.

Fortunately, as you will discover in [chapters
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)--[5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05), there is no such thing as a
positive or negative birth number. All Birth Code numbers are neutral,
all have a positive and shadow expression. It is up to you to choose the
positive expression of each number in your Birth Code. This is your key
to staying in alignment with your purpose and mission.

Now let's discover the magic in your Birth Name---the final of your
three important birth numbers!

[]{#ch02.xhtml}

## []{#ch02.xhtml#page_22 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 2]{.f3} {#ch02.xhtml#ch02 .h2n}

## YOUR BIRTH-NAME CODE {.h2t}

[W]{.dropcap}[HEN YOU WERE BORN, IN ADDITION TO THE CODE IN YOUR
BIRTHDAY, YOU WERE GIVEN ANOTHER UNIQUE CODE]{.f3}---it is your Destiny
Number, derived from the name on your birth certificate. This is the
third of your three core birth numbers. Your Destiny Number describes
the nature of your work environment, specifically *how* you naturally
use your gifts and activate your divine mission. Thus your Destiny
Number is aligned with your career.

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_23 .pagebreak}You are designed to express your Day
of Birth Number and Life Purpose Number in a certain way. This "way" is
your career environment, described by your Destiny Number.

For example, if your Day or Life Purpose Number resonates to the root
number 3, then you must share joy and uplift others in some capacity.
The key to *how* to turn this natural way of being into a thriving
career is described by your Destiny Number. If your Destiny Number
resonates to the root number 7, then your best career environment for
expressing joy and uplifting others happens when you are working alone,
in private, with plenty of time to think, read, and listen. Ideally you
have easy access to nature, since 7 is the number of serenity,
contemplation, analysis, and inspiration. Your breakthroughs come in
moments of silence. Your natural optimism and desire for self-expression
(3 Life Purpose or Day of Birth) are unlocked when you are in your own
private quiet space, where timelessness exists and your mind can enter a
kind of cathartics state of being. . .

On the other hand, if you have a **3** Day of Birth or Life Purpose and
a Destiny Number that reduces to **8**, then you are meant to step up as
a leader who inspires and motivates others from a joyful place, or you
embody the connection between happiness and financial abundance, or you
elevate others to lead from an internal place of joyful self expression,
often through entrepreneurship.

Do this exercise with both your Day of Birth Number and Life Purpose
Number---merge each of them with your Destiny Number to discover how you
to best express your gifts, personality and strengths in a career
environment.

Let's begin by calculating your birth certificate name first. It's best
to learn how to add all the letters in your name before using an online
calculator so you can write down and feel your numbers in action!

::: group
### HOW TO CALCULATE YOUR DESTINY NUMBER {.h3}

Every person and entity (business name, book title, or product name) has
a name. The "birth name" is the third of Three Important Numbers in your
Birth Code. To calculate your birth name, please use the name on your
birth certificate.
:::

If you were adopted, please use the birth-certificate name that was in
place before you turned six months old. So, if the new adopted name was
made official before you were six months of age, use that name. If it
was changed after you turned six months old, use the original
birth-certificate name as the primary Destiny Number. You can still look
at the new adopted name as a secondary influence, but it will not be
used as one of the Three Important Numbers in your Birth Code.

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_24 .pagebreak}Each letter resonates to a specific
number. When calculating which number is aligned with which letter, we
use the Pythagorean (Western) Numerology Alphabet system. It is a
straight forward system where the letter A corresponds to the number 1,
B to number 2, C to number 3 all the way to I to number 9. It and then
begins at letter J for number 1 and so on.

Use the following table to convert every individual letter in each of
the names that make up your full birth certificate name into a number:

[PYTHAGOREAN SYSTEM]{.f3}

::: land100
![Image](./f0024-01.jpg){#f0024-01}
:::

Add up your birth-certificate name to discover your Destiny Number:

1\. Write the birth name down on a piece of paper (or type the birth
name on your computer).

2\. Assign each letter to the corresponding number in the alphabet,
using the Pythagorean System above.

3\. Count all the numbers for one total.

Your total Destiny Number then must be reduced to a single-digit root
number. As you discovered in [chapter 1](#ch01.xhtml#ch01), sometimes
you need to reduce more than once to arrive at that single-digit.

Important tips on suffixes in birth names:

1\. Do not count the letters in "Jr" or "Sr." For example, "John Smith,
Jr." is written as "JOHN SMITH" without "Jr."

2\. Do not count I, II, or III. For example, "John Smith, III" is
calculated as "JOHN SMITH."

3\. Count any foreign letters as if they did not have symbols---so å is
a, ü is u, Æ is AE, œ is oe, and so on.

Let's look at the same six celebrity case studies from [chapter
1](#ch01.xhtml#ch01) to learn how to calculate any Destiny Number from
all the letters in a person's birth-certificate name.

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_25 .pagebreak}After calculating each Destiny Number,
you will see each case study's Three Important Birth Numbers---their Day
of Birth, Life Purpose and Destiny Numbers. Then you'll see a summary
showing how to merge the Day of Birth and Life Purpose number meaning
with the Destiny Number meaning. This summary gives you six examples on
*how* in combination the Three Important Birth Numbers point to the
career environment best suited for each celebrity example. You will see
how each one is expressing their gifts in alignment with the Three
Important Numbers in their Birth Code.

::: group
#### **CASE STUDY 1:** {.h4a}

Justin Timberlake's birth-certificate name is "Justin Randall
Timberlake."
:::

  [**J**]{.f3}   [**U**]{.f3}   [**S**]{.f3}   [**T**]{.f3}   [**I**]{.f3}   [**N**]{.f3}       [**R**]{.f3}   [**A**]{.f3}   [**N**]{.f3}   [**D**]{.f3}   [**A**]{.f3}   [**L**]{.f3}   [**L**]{.f3}
  -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- --- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- --------------
  1              3              1              2              9              5                  9              1              5              4              1              3              3

  [**T**]{.f3}   [**I**]{.f3}   [**M**]{.f3}   [**B**]{.f3}   [**E**]{.f3}   [**R**]{.f3}   [**L**]{.f3}   [**A**]{.f3}   [**K**]{.f3}   [**E**]{.f3}   [**DESTINY NUMBER**]{.f3}
  -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- -------------- ----------------------------
  2              9              4              2              5              9              3              1              2              5              89
                                                                                                                                                        8 + 9 = **17**
                                                                                                                                                        1 + 7 = **8** root destiny

Justin Timberlake's Destiny Number is **98/17/8**.

So, Justin Timberlake's Three Important Birth Numbers are:

Justin Timerblake's Birthday: **1.31.1981**

1\. Day of Birth: **31/4**

2\. Life Purpose Number: **24/6**

3\. Destiny Number **98/17/8**

First look up the meanings for single-digit **Day of Birth** and **Life
Purpose Numbers 4** and **6** in [chapter 1](#ch01.xhtml#ch01). Given
those meanings you'll notice that Justin is naturally very methodical
(4) and magnetic (6); disciplined, productive, grounded (4); creative,
responsible, compassionate (6); as well as not being afraid of work and
making his own rules (4) and craving harmony and being fond of luxury
(6).

How does he express these gifts in a career environment? Through his
**Destiny Number 8**---look up the meaning for number 8 in [chapter
1](#ch01.xhtml#ch01). He is a natural leader, a strong, determined
visionary, very efficient and ambitious, patient, courageous, abundant,
and influential.

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_26 .pagebreak}Now let's *combine* the meaning of
Justin Timberlake's 4 Day of Birth and 6 Life Purpose Numbers with his 8
**Destiny Number** to see the best career environment for him:

When Justin Timberlake is in a positive vibrational state, the career
environment that allows him to express his natural gifts with greatest
ease and joy is defined by Justin stepping up as an artistic,
compassionate Leader, a magnetic, creative Visionary, and a disciplined,
hard-working Influencer who uses his power and abundance in a positive,
unique and nurturing way, thereby being a source of courage to others.

Justin Timberlake's career as a singer-songwriter, actor, and record
producer ultimately defines his purpose and destiny.

::: group

Mariel Hemingway's birth-certificate name is "Mariel Hadley Hemingway."

Now let's discover Mariel Hemingway's Three Important Birth Numbers:

Mariel Hemingway's Birthday: **11.22.1961**

1\. Day of Birth: **22/4**

How does she express these gifts in a career environment? Through her

When Mariel Hemingway is in a positive vibrational state, the career
environment that allows her to express her natural gifts with greatest
ease and joy is defined by Mariel bringing energy into balance as a
caring Peacemaker who is dependable as well as flexible, a Prophet of
freedom, a trusting Confidante, and a disciplined, hard working diplomat
who uses her adventurous spirit in a fun, unique and kind way, thereby
being a source of calmness and inspiration to others.

Mariel Hemingway's acting career coupled with her passion for living a
balanced life--as a producer of videos on yoga and holistic
living---ultimately defines her dedication to express her purpose and
destiny for her highest good.

Julia Roberts' Destiny Number is **78/15/6**.

Julia Roberts' Birthday: **10.28.1967**

quiet way (7), is strong willed and determined (1) while having an air
of mystery and wisdom (7), has definite views and a strong independent
streak (1), is a natural truth seeker who []{#ch02.xhtml#page_28
.pagebreak}craves alone time, is extremely private, and needs to be in
touch with nature on a regular basis.

How does she express these gifts in a career environment? Through her
**Destiny Number 6---**look up the meaning for number 6 in [chapter
1](#ch01.xhtml#ch01). Julia Roberts is artistic, compassionate, very
magnetic, refined, and is creative; she needs natural harmondy, is a
natural nurturer, loves to be of service in some way, is dedicated to
her family and a beautiful home environment.

Now let's *combine* the meaning of Julia Roberts's 1 Day of Birth and 7
Life Purpose numbers with her 6 **Destiny Number** to see the best
career environment for her:

When Julia Roberts is in a positive vibrational state, the career
environment that allows her to express her natural gifts with greatest
ease and joy is defined by Julia using her magnetic presence as an
Artist or Healer to be of service from a place of Love and compassion,
dedicated to being a Creator of beauty from a place of honesty and
integrity. She has an independent perspective of her divine mission and
yearns for unique projects to work to satisfy her quest for wisdom and
knowledge and her dedication to be of Service.

Julia's leading lady status in Hollywood--her magnetic, beautiful, and
compassionate presence on the screen---is coupled with a deep personal
need to "get away from the hustle and bustle," devote quality time to
her family, and replenish her soul's core need for privacy in nature
ultimately defines her purpose and destiny.

#### **CASE STUDY 4:** {.h4a}

Oprah Winfrey's birth certificate name is "Orpah Gail Winfrey."
:::

  **[O]{.f3}**   **[R]{.f3}**   **[P]{.f3}**   **[A]{.f3}**   **[H]{.f3}**       **[G]{.f3}**   **[A]{.f3}**   **[I]{.f3}**   **[L]{.f3}**

                                                                                                                   1 + 6 = **7** root destiny

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_29 .pagebreak}*" It's best to learn how to add all
the letters in your name before using an online calculator, so you can
write down and feel your numbers in action!"*

Oprah Winfrey's Destiny Number is **97/16/7**.

Now let's discover Oprah Winfrey's Three Important Birth Numbers:

Oprah Winfrey's Birthday: **10.29.1954**

1\. Day of Birth: **29/11/2**

2\. Life Purpose Number: **31/4**

3\. Destiny Number **97/16/7**

(11) who is kind, sensitive and psychic (2), dependable, loyal (4) and a

(11/2).

How does she express these gifts in a career environment? Through her
**Destiny Number 7**---look up the meaning for number 7 in [chapter

to read), uncovering the nature of beliefs works best for herself,
doesn't follow the beaten path, needs time for contemplation to ponder
the deeper subjects, needs to be intellectually stimulated.

Now let's *combine* the meaning of Oprah Winfrey's 11/2 Day of Birth and
4 Life Purpose Numbers with her 7 **Destiny Number** to see the best
career environment for her:

When Oprah Winfrey is in a positive vibrational state, the career
environment that allows her to express her natural gifts with greatest
ease and joy is defined by Oprah seeking solutions through knowledge and
inspiration and stepping up as an Inspirational Leader, a Spiritual
Teacher, who also has the mastery to make each idea and inspiration
Practical, so everyone feels both grounded and inspired, using her 1 on
1 skills to Interview others, whose mastery she respects, sometimes on
rare and mystical subjects, and embodying the discipline and patience to
combine all these qualities in a cohesive, step-by-step way.

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_30 .pagebreak}Oprah Winfrey's impact as one of the
most influential people in the world, her ability to sit down and
interview her guests at soul level, and her OWN network flagship program
"Super Soul Sunday" are the epitome of Oprah's ultimately destiny as a
spiritual teacher.

### SHORT DESTINY NUMBER DESCRIPTIONS FOR "ROOT NUMBERS" 1 - 9 {.h3}

The following are brief descriptions revealing the positive expression
for each s*ingle-digit root number* as regards the nature of your career
environment. Use this as a quick-reference guide anyone's Destiny
Number.
:::

To view the complete, in-depth definitions for your Destiny Number,
please refer to [chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03) (single-digit numbers
1--9), [chapter 4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04) (double-digit "Master Numbers" 11,
22, 33, 44) and [chapter 5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05) (double-digit "compound"
numbers 10--99).

1

**1** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **10**, **19**, **28**, **37**, **46**, **55**, **64**,
**73**, **82**, **91---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **1** (such as 100, 109, 118, etc).

*When you as a* ***1 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to an* ***Innovative Leader***. *You do so
through self-realization---having the courage and initiative to apply
your own original ideas, and trusting in your innate creativity. Take
charge of your gifts as an independent thinker. You must stand alone, so
you can explore new ideas and skills without interference. You work best
independently and in privacy. Be your own boss*.

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_33 .pagebreak}*" Once you know and apply your Birth
Code you'll be freed from pursuing expectations placed on you by
others."*

2

**2** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **11**, **20**, **29**, **38**, **47**, **56**, **65**,
**74**, **83**, **92**--or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **2** or **Master Number 11** (such as
101, 110, 119, 128, etc.). \*\*If your Destiny Number reduces to 11 and
2, please be sure to read the detailed description for both numbers
([chapters 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03) and [4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04)).

*When you as a* ***2 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to create harmony and balance as a*
***Mediator of Peace***. *You are able to navigate two worlds at
once---the seen and unseen, the spiritual and practical---thereby
combining the beauty and value of both. By being open and receptive to
your amazing intuitive gifts you gain the persuasion powers to be
helpful to others through love and kindness. You are a natural healer,
here on Earth to inspire and give hope. Due to your high sensitivity,
you must feel in harmony in your work environment*.

3

**3** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **12**, **21**, **30**, **39**, **48**, **57**, **66**,
**75**, **84**, **93**---or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **3** (such as 102, 111, 120, 129, etc.).

*When you as a* ***3 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to express your creativity and be a*
***Messenger of Joy***. *You are designed to inspire others through your
artistry and communication skills---using writing, music, painting,
poetry, speaking, and/or dance---to ignite your imagination and share an
uplifting message. Your smile lights up the room---and so must the
fruits of your career. Feeling totally positive about your work projects
is crucial in order for your natural optimism and enthusiasm to fire up.
That's when your inspirational creativity deeply impacts others at soul
level*.

4

**4** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **13**, **22**, **31**, **40**, **49**, **58**, **67**,
**76**, **85**, **94---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **4** (such as 103, 112, 121, 130, etc.).

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_34 .pagebreak}*When you as a* ***4 Destiny*** *are
energetically aligned, your divine mission in this lifetime is to build
something of value and be the* ***Practical Manifester*.** *You must
feel like your gifts are being used to create something practical,
secure, and stable. You are a natural facilitator and manager who knows
how to get results and delegate others to follow a certain protocol,
bringing out the best in them. You thrive when you have work to
accomplish and must feel that what you put out there is valuable and
serves a practical purpose. Your work environment should feel orderly,
stable, and secure (everything in its place) so you can use your natural
dedication and integrity to fulfill your responsibilities*.

5

**5** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **14**, **23**, **32**, **41**, **50**, **59**, **68**,
**77**, **86**, **95---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **5** (such as 104, 113, 122, 131, etc.).

*When you as a* ***5 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to be a* ***Messenger of Freedom***. *You
feel the most happy in your career when you can explore freely,
independent of any constraints, and make the most of any experience. You
want to experience life fully, are naturally curious, want to explore
every possible angle, and use your gift of communication to share
messages that excite and liberate. You are a natural networker and
salesperson---if you are passionate about a subject, you can "sell" it
to anyone. In order to feel at ease, you cannot feel bored or locked
into a 9 to 5 job. Freedom of movement is key*.

6

**6** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **15**, **24**, **33**, **42**, **51**, **60**, **69**,
**78**, **87**, **96---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **6** (such as 105, 114, 123, 132, etc.).

*When you as a* ***6 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to nurture others through compassion as a*
***Healer of Love***. *You are stimulated by beauty, love, and family to
create harmony in everything you do. Being of service through mentoring,
guiding, advising, teaching, inspiring, and healing others is the key to
unlocking your Destiny. You are designed to create something beautiful
and deeply meaningful. In doing so, you inspire others to do the same.
Your gifts to heal are profound---use them to fulfill your destiny*.

7

**7** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **16**, **25**, **34**, **43**, **52**, **61**, **70**,
**79**, **88**, **97---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **7** (such as 106, 115, 124, 133, etc.).

[]{#ch02.xhtml#page_35 .pagebreak}*When you as a* ***7 Destiny*** *are
energetically aligned, your divine mission in this lifetime is to
contemplate, search for answers, and be a* ***Seeker of Truth***. *You
love to learn and seek wisdom, so your best career environment allows
you to discover secrets and mysteries in science or spiritual subjects
and answer life's big questions. Your mind and intuition are very
active, so you need to be engaged in some kind of research, analysis, or
meditative field. Using your acute observation skills by digging deeply
allows you to feel fulfilled on every level. By merging your amazing
intuitive skills with learning and reading you can specialize in a
subject and teach your wise discoveries*.

8

**8** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **17**, **26**, **35**, **44**, **53**, **62**, **71**,
**80**, **89**, **98---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **8** (such as 107, 116, 125, 134, etc.).

*When you as an* ***8 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to consistently expand your feelings towards
prosperity, and power and use your limitless energy reserves to step up
as a* ***Visionary Leader***. *Hold space for your own visions by
utilizing your natural courage, influence, and quest for achievement.
Trust in the infinite abundance of the universe to manifest your
creative dreams. By doing so you empower others to succeed as well. You
must feel like you can achieve anything, that with discipline and
excellence you will reach all your dreams and goals. Being your own boss
or running your own business serves you well*.

9

**9** is one of your important Birth Code numbers if your Destiny Number
adds up to **18**, **27**, **36**, **45**, **54**, **63**, **72**,
**81**, **90**, **99---**or **any three-digit number** that reduces to a
single-digit "root number" of **8** (such as 108, 117, 126, 135, etc.).

*When you as a* ***9 Destiny*** *are energetically aligned, your divine
mission in this lifetime is to make the world a better place by being a*
***Compassionate Humanitarian***. *Your mission is to love
unconditionally and share that love in everything you do. Others look to
you as an example (whether you realize it or not!) and see you as a wise
leader. You need to have your heart and soul engaged in your career and
allow yourself free rein to explore many cultures and people from all
walks of life. This diversity will unleash the underlying truth that
opportunities are to be found everywhere. You are sensitive, forgiving,
creative, intuitive and have healing abilities, so when you know that
you are elevating and transforming people's lives you feel fulfilled*.

## []{#ch03.xhtml#page_36 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 3]{.f3} {#ch03.xhtml#ch03 .h2n}

## SINGLE-DIGITS 1--9 AND THE THREE TRIADS {.h2t}

[N]{.dropcap}[OW IT'S TIME TO DELVE INTO THE POSITIVE GIFTS AND SHADOW
SIDE FOR ALL NINE SINGLE-DIGIT ROOT NUMBERS.]{.f3} You are both
supported and enlightened by your beautiful soul code. Each of our Three
Important Birth Numbers will illuminate moments that shift us (both
challenging and exciting!) so that we can acclimate and make the most
out of them!

Root numbers by their very name define the underlying energy of any
number when it is reduced to its origin---a single-digit. Please refer
to [chapter 4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04) for all double-digit "Master Numbers"
11, 22, 33, 44, etc. and [chapter 5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05) for all
double-digit "compound" numbers (10--99).

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_37 .pagebreak}Each single-digit number can be
compared to the key of a piece of music, such as A minor or D major,
from which the building blocks of melody and harmony are formed. Numbers
are aligned to music and to the stars---they form a code that is both
visible and invisible. This chapter will unveil the deep mysteries of
each single-digit and forms the basis of the whole book itself.

It's important to note that most people have at least two different root
numbers in their Three Important Birth Numbers' code. Only on rare
occasions will you meet someone who has the same three root numbers as
their Day of Birth, Life Purpose, and Destiny Number.

If one of your three numbers appears twice (for example, you have a 7
Day of Birth and a 124 Destiny which reduces to 7) then you have an
"Intensification." Refer to [chapter 11](#ch11.xhtml#ch11) for more on
intensifications, both in your Birth Code and other areas of your life.

We begin with the three numerology triads, since they reveal how each
single-digit belongs to a unique number "family."

::: group
### THE 1-5-7 "MIND" TRIAD {.h3}

The three numbers that compose the Mind Triad are 1, 5, and 7. Those who
have one or more of these three Mind numbers are analytical,
intellectual, intuitive, ambitious, independent, witty, and psychic.
This Mind Triad is comfortable with information, both analyzing and
gathering facts and figures and using the mind to solve problems and
make decisions. They enjoy learning and exploring new territory.
:::

Mind Triad people may have a tendency to worry or overanalyze---getting
caught up in the net of information overload. Encouraging a Mind person
to feel the outcome of their solutions in advance instead of thinking
through them may make them feel a tad uncomfortable---but is truly the
way into experiencing that missing link---the blissful factor.
Fortunately, Mind people have a natural intuitive side that is always
ready to listen once they switch off (or at least turn down) their
"inner analyst!"

::: group
### THE 2-4-8 "MANIFESTATION" TRIAD {.h3}

The three numbers that comprise the Manifestation Triad are 2, 4, and 6.
Those who have one or more of these three Manifestation numbers are by
nature more patient, have a peaceful, grounding energy, use order and
discipline to manifest results into physical reality, and are a stable
influence. Manifestation Triad people know how to get things done and
overcome obstacles to do so. Thus having a 2, 4 or 8 in your Three
Important Birth []{#ch03.xhtml#page_38 .pagebreak}Numbers is an
invitation to implement result after result, building a solid foundation
for now and the future.
:::

Manifestation people may have a tendency to implement before intuiting
or feeling out the efficacy of their plans. So they may be perplexed
when they don't achieve their intended result. This happens because
their intentions were not fully aligned with how they feel before they
go into manifestation mode. Taking the "heart" and "fun" out of the
intention process can lead to frustration. With their natural thirst to
manifest, they just need to carve out some quality time to enjoy the
process, introduce a sense of *play*, and check into their feelings.
Then, the outcomes of their steady implementation process will be
extraordinary and lasting.

::: group
### THE 3-6-9 "CREATION" TRIAD {.h3}

Numbers 3, 6, and 9 form the Triad of Creation. Those people who have
one or more of these three Creation numbers are by nature compassionate,
loving, emotionally engaged, highly creative, nurturing, enthusiastic,
and social and have a great need to be of service in order to uplift
others. Creation Triad people must have their heart engaged in every
part of their life experience. Feeling good and expressing their good
vibes in some way is their key to happiness. Thus they must have an
outlet to talk, write, dance---create in any format of their choosing.
:::

When expressing the shadow side of this triad, the person can get moody,
dissipate energy through distractions, stop manifesting altogether and
abdicate responsibilities. They can feel sorry for themselves and blame
the world for what they perceive as unfair treatment. The best "cure"
for distractions and doldrums is---to go play and create. Laughter and
humor are wonderful healing balms for the 3-6-9 triad to create a
"pattern interrupt" and press the mood reset button! Their feelings are
their soul-food, and so getting into a positive state allows them to
feel valued, appreciated, and loved again. Then they can share the love,
uplift others, and thrive. After all, to *love* is their ultimate
motivation.

A special note about this triad. The 3-6-9 triad governs the creation
process. Thus the building blocks of the universe reduce down to these
three numbers. In astrology, for example, all the different "aspects"
(connections between planets or angles) add up to numbers that reduce to
either 3, 6, or 9, such as the 120-degree "Trine," which adds up to 3;
the 90-degree "Square," which adds up to 9 and the 60-degree "Sextile,"
which adds up to 6 (Any aspect will reduce to 3, 6, or 9.) The 24 hours
in a day add up to 6, and 12 hours add up to 3. 60 minutes is 6.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_39 .pagebreak}Multiples of 3, 6, and 9 are repeated
over and over again no matter which number is multiplied.

Use the three triads---Mind, Manifestation and Creation---to get a quick
read on anyone. For example, if you know a person with a 10/**1** Day of
Birth (which is in the Mind Triad) and a 33/**6** Life Purpose (which is
in the Creation Triad), you can deduce that this person likes to analyze
and think things through, craves independence, is motivated (Mind), has
a great capacity for compassion, enjoys helping and advising others, has
good people skills, and must express their feelings (Creation).

These three numerology triads alone are a great starting point to gain
instant understanding of a person's outlook and natural ways.

::: group
### NUMBER "0" {.h3}

The number 0 hovers between worlds---between numbers of positive value
and numbers of negative value, between the seen and the unseen. It
therefore represents a unique power. In fact, if you add 0 to any number
*it expands and empowers that number*---3 becomes 30, 7 magnifies to
70---and the more zeros you add, the bigger the value becomes---2,000
and 8,000,000---carry far more impact and influence than 2 and 8.
:::

Thus the number 0 represents the "God Number," symbolizing the greatest
power and multidimensional reality---the supreme balance between light
and dark. 0 is the full circle, representing all the universes,
galaxies, multiverses---all there was, is, and will be to experience.
When you loose track of time, you experience the power of hovering
between worlds in a space where life just is---and each moment expands
into timelessness.

0 takes you to your Origins---Original Source, where there is and always
will be Only light, total Omnipotence. Even the word "zero" ends with
the letter O, representing 0. The full circle in O is both everything
and nothing, full and empty. It is both a container and an entry into
another dimension. It can hold all energy, while allowing all energy to
pass through it. There is no time, just eternity.

Look at zero as the ultimate existential experience. Zero puts a divine
sparkle into everything it touches. Zero holds divine light.

::: group
### MEANING OF SINGLE-DIGIT "ROOT" NUMBERS {.h3}

Let's go now on a wonderful, life-changing journey and discover the
secret drivers, divine gifts, and direction for all nine single-digit
numbers from 1 through 9.
:::

::: land100
[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_40
.pagebreak}![Image](./f0040-01.jpg){#f0040-01}
:::

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_41 .pagebreak}Use the following descriptions for
your Day of Birth Number, Life Purpose Number, and Destiny Number.

Make a note of intensifications---when the same number repeats. (See
[chapter 11](#ch11.xhtml#ch11))

Pay attention to which numerology triad your Three Important Birth
Numbers belong to:

Are they **all grouped into one triad family?** For example, all three
of your Important Birth Code numbers are either 2, 4, or 8 thus
representing the Manifestion Triad exclusively. Or do they represent
**two** of three triads? For example, your Birth Code comprises a 3 and
a 9 (Creation) plus 5 (Mind). Or do your Three Important Birth Code
Numbers **all belong to different triads?** For example, a 3 Day of
Birth (Creation Triad), a 2 Life Purpose (Manifestation Triad), and a 7
Destiny (Mind Triad).

::: group
#### **ROOT NUMBER 1** {.h4}

1 is the number of new beginnings and originality. It is the vibration
of free will, individual pursuit, innovation, and daring---the original
spark of creation. 1 represents courage, and enthusiasm. 1 people
following their primary impulse. They are natural born leaders who want
to leave a unique legacy. They resist taking the beaten path, instead
follow their instinct to create new experiences for others---introducing
innovative new ways---by following their own, individual path. When in
positive alignment, a 1 person animates energy, stays in motion, always
creating something new, and guides others to break through into new
territory by the very nature of who they are at soul level. They rebel
against being asked to follow others, since it is their role to take
command.
:::

1 is the first number in the Mind Triad, and so this vibration means the
mind is always on fire with ideas springing up freely and uninhibited,
always with the intent to create something new. Putting the ideas into
practice takes its form in unique ways. 1 feels like they are "number
one," seeking to stand out in some way and direct others, or be the
"star." They usually become important and influential in some area of
life.

Mediocrity frustrates a 1 person---they need to feel value and the
original, intelligent spark of creation in everything and everyone.
Confidence and fearlessness are their natural gifts (a lack of these
qualities means they are out of alignment energetically).

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_42 .pagebreak}1

The image of the one is of a straight line coming from heaven to earth
and back. It is dignified and straightforward, and has a penetrating
sense of direction. 1 is a vibration that represents the masculine
aspect of our human experience.

All number 1 people carry dignity. 1 likes to stand out, is proud,
achievement oriented, represents the primal impulse, and has a strong
self-worth. 1 always will demand respect and feels set apart from
others. 1 has strong views and definite beliefs, and protects those that
are vulnerable. They are private, value their solitude, and enjoy
spending time alone.

1s are very affectionate with those whom they love and trust but not
keen on having an immediate familiarity with people they have just met.
1 is comfortable around younger people and children, though they may at
times feel a sadness arise from childhood memories. 1 enjoys exquisite
clothes and jewelry and tends to have impeccable taste with a penchant
for the finer things in life.

Since 1s are naturally self-centric and here to learn to be
self-sufficient and self-reliant, they also have a great desire to be in
love and be loved by a partner. This paradox exists perhaps because they
need to explore first being independent and then reach out and learn to
be *interdependent*. Of all the nine numbers, 1 people may know best how
to bypass codependency due to their underlying need for self-reliance.

1 is in the Mind Triad, thus blessing 1 people with mental resources and
an active imagination. Appealing to a 1 person's intelligence leads to
the best results. This is true for children and adolescents as well. 1s
do not do well with authority and control, and they will eventually
rebel and even turn aggressive. 1s need to guard against overanalyzing
and worrying about a future that is totally hypothetical. Staying
focused on the present in a flowing, creative state of being allows 1
people to thrive and reach their highest goals, often with astounding
speed.

1 must feel like they are an authority in something. They are natural
leaders and use their original ideas to move energy with dynamic power.

::: group
#### **CHALLENGING EXPRESSIONS:** {.h4}

1 people are very good at starting but have a more difficult time
completing projects and goals. Their pride can get the best of
them---they can even go against their true values when their pride is
wounded. 1 does not respond well to criticism, though they can dish it
out. 1 in its shadow expression is stubborn, will complain when
ambitions are thwarted and can be quite self-centered. 1 can suffer from
"bruised ego" syndrome and will only help others if they do exactly as
the 1 person expects of them. When a 1 is ignored, they can lash out
with anger.
:::

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_43 .pagebreak}When out of alignment, a 1 person can
be boastful, aggressive, cynical, and egotistical, and even can turn to
bullying others to create a false sense of power. Their repressed
feelings can turn to anger, and they are unwilling to join forces with
others or cooperate with people easily, preferring their own way or the
highway. They won't want to be told what to do and may even lash out
aggressively to stop anyone whom they view as an unwelcome parental
figure.

Other out-of-alignment expressions for number 1 are lacking iniative or
being indecisive, lazy, low in confidence, or easily influenced and
swayed by others.

If you have hurt a 1 person in some way and want to come back into
harmony with them, share your sentiments with great humility---a 1 won't
necessarily wrap their arms around you, but will accept your apology
with grace and gratitude.

1 people believe they are superior to others and can attract resentment
for these airs of superiority, since they can come off as pedantic,
arrogant, and conceited. Thus they can be obstinate and do not accept
opposition in any way, shape, or form. Or they can be inconsiderate of
other people's feelings even while they themselves are very sensitive.

The way to harmony and peace is to be carefree and spontaneous, loosen
the reins of control, use their good humor, and tap into their love of
new discoveries, as this positive mindset instantly presses the reset
button, aligns 1s to their heart-center, and lets bygones be bygones.

Affirmation: *I am at one with my mind, heart and soul. I magically
create miraculous opportunities for me to accomplish anything!*

::: group
#### **ROOT NUMBER 2** {.h4}

2 is the number of peace, balance, and unity---the union of opposites.
With a strong emphasis on balance, 2 is designed to merge realities,
bringing opposites together. 2s are the peacemakers, mediators, and
diplomats---wanting harmony to prevail even under the most trying
conditions. Thus their patience and listening abilities are highly
prized.
:::

2 carries ancient wisdom, and a sense of mysticism and secrets and has
wonderful artistic gifts. It represents duality, pairs, couples, the
feminine vibration, receptivity, and one-on-one engagement. 2 people are
very sensitive, so be extra gentle with them. 2 is connected to
imagination and dreams. They love to connect to and correspond with
others.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_44 .pagebreak}As the most diplomatic of all nine
numbers, 2 people get along with pretty much anyone. This is especially
true since 2s don't seek to measure up against others at the cost of
harmony and maintaining equilibrium. They don't feel the need to impose
their views or beliefs on others. They are also peaceful people to be
around, since they exude a calmness when making decisions.

2

The visible representation of number 2 looks like a person bowing to the
left, in the direction of the number 1. This innate desire to merge with
another, join with them, and create peace is integral to all 2s.

2s have a need to look for advice, support, and approval from
others---making sure all bases are covered before they break new ground.
This cautious approach requires a need to understand and know as much as
they can before making a decision and then proceeding with care. This
moderate approach is appreciated and respected by others, giving 2s the
gift of good judgment.

This, coupled with their kind disposition, warmth, and understanding
makes them easy to be with and welcome in any situation. 2s are
excellent managers, as they have a miraculous touch of persuasion which
opens doors for everyone to see eye to eye---often discreetly getting
others to view things their way. This tact, mediation, and diplomacy
enables the 2 person to make major inroads in securing consensus between
different parties, allowing them to open doors and succeed where others
could not.

2 is the first vibration in the 2-4-8 Manifestation Triad. Thus 2s are
naturally responsible, conscientious, and efficient. 2s are usually
humble, but can initially lack self-confidence.

2 people are very psychic, though they may keep that side of themselves
secret. They are extremely sensitive to other people's feelings, sensing
them instantly, and so they are very concerned for their close loved
ones' well-being. Their highly developed intuition serves them well when
they meet people, since their natural shyness can lead them to not trust
others easily. 2s are generous friends and make great companions. They
have a natural interest in the psychology of human nature due to their
acute observation skills and ability to intuit body language, sounds,
and facial expressions. This makes them excellent observers.

2s are naturally very romantic, stemming from the number's connection to
two people in partnership. One of their main lessons is to be in
partnership with lovers, friends, and associates without losing their
independence and sense of self. Not falling into codependent
relationship patterns is a major lesson for any 2 person. 2s are very
affectionate and tender. They have a primal urge to please others.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_45 .pagebreak}Due to their sensitive nature 2 people
are secretive and don't readily share their intimate thoughts, their
plans, or even what their next move will be. At the same time they are
wonderful conversationalists and can naturally get others to reveal
parts of themselves. When they approach their goals, they are the
opposite of 1 people, who just go for it---2s will move forward, then
course-correct and then might head right, left, and even backwards
before lunging forward again, often with great force. This zigzag
pattern towards their goals gives them a sense of balance, which they so
crave. A 2 person will usually attract financial well-being---if
anything, it is rare to see them struggling in conditions of poverty.
However, if trained to have a "poverty-conscious" mindset, 2s must
consciously extricate themselves from this paradigm first before
experiencing their natural gift to attract prosperity. 2s are very
giving with their resources. They find it more difficult to accept
gifts, having an innate tendency to feel inadequate if they accept
support, especially financial.

2s trust others implicitly. They can't imagine anyone having a "bad"
intention or being anything but kind and noble. This means they believe
what others tell them. So they must learn to discern between what feels
right and what feels just a little "off"---use their intuitive gifts to
separate the manipulators from those who will not take advantage of
their kind hearts and good faith.

A 2 person loves to dream and live in their imaginary, idealistic world.
These sensitive, kind souls are highly adaptable and intuitive, giving
them all the qualities they need to fulfill their beautiful dream of
bringing peace, love, and harmony to the world. In their most positive
state, 2s are a true blessing to everyone around them.

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

A 2 person living in the shadow expression of their number may have a
tendency to fear the unknown and be unusually cautious. They need highly
sensitive support to come to terms with the unfamiliar. In fact, 2s can
fear every kind of pain or loss, allowing their very active imagination
to fuel their fears and worries. They may appear calm and balanced, but
this can also hide a neurotic, touchy, nervous disposition. If they feel
hurt by someone, they don't tend to react aggressively; rather they will
retreat into silence and even shut down.
:::

Due to their natural humility, 2s, when out of alignment, can sometimes
slip into feeling inadequate and suffer from low self-esteem. This sets
up a situation where they can easily get depressed and in turn will
create problems for themselves to almost "prove" their perceived state
of lack. []{#ch03.xhtml#page_46 .pagebreak}The 2-4-8 Manifestation Triad
that number 2 belongs to is very meticulous and demands thorough
attention to detail---but the sensitive 2 person can go overboard and
demand too much of themselves. Expectations that are set too high can
spiral into complexes and inhibited behavior, as they doubt their own
abilities and react fearfully when the unexpected shows up at their
doorstep. This self-criticism is a big lesson for the 2 to overcome, so
they stay centered and live their life free of inner conflict.

Being in a secure, loving home base is integral for their equilibrium
across all of the spectrums in their life. If they feel obligated to
live in a disharmonious and tense environment, or with people who are
argumentative and aggressive, they will loose their sense of
equilibrium. This is when 2s can become bitter and broken. Since
conflict and a disharmonious environment have a very detrimental effect
on 2s, they must always have a "safe place" to go to in order to feel
loved and nurtured; otherwise they will lash out and be temperamental.
Loud noise, aggressive, violent movies and blasting music will also harm
the energetic field around a 2 person and can easily throw them off
balance.

At the same time, 2s will sacrifice much to get their life back into
harmony. It is very important for all 2s to accept that life is filled
with both positive and negative situations so that they don't react to
the challenging moments with tension, depression, and inner turmoil.
This is why having a harmonious home environment is so integral to their
spiritual, mental, and emotional health.

Their shyness may make them "freeze" around strangers. Once they feel
their heart engaged in a conversation (and sense that there is no danger
of being hurt), they open up the soft petals of their sweet, tender
heart to others. They are deeply affected by inconsiderate or rude
behavior. However, once they regain their balance they will figure out
how to justify such actions by others and forgive them.

2s can be very cautious and may not easily take a chance. They also can
become possessive of things and people. Indecision can lead to feeling
separate and divided.

To remain balanced and strengthen their inner confidence, 2s must
release their desire to please and be "perfect;" otherwise doubt and
indecision will run their lives in circles. Their need to please can
lead them to sacrifice their own unique ideas for someone else's
cause---thus 2s need to be diligent and maintain boundaries.

They must not get preoccupied with unimportant matters---like surfing
the internet and obsessive attention to social media---which create a
false sense of connection the 2 craves *without yielding meaningful
results*, and the end result is that the wasted time reinforces a sense
of inadequacy and []{#ch03.xhtml#page_47 .pagebreak}incompletion. 2s
must always discern between what actually matters and what does not. . .
what is for their highest good, and what is not.

Getting to this place of peace means learning first and foremost how to
Relax. Relaxation is the key for a 2 to regain and maintain inner
harmony and peace. In this place of serenity their moods and emotions
won't get repressed or overwhelm them---both sure signs that they are
imbalanced and just need to take a moment to regroup. Deep breathing,
exercise, and meditation are wonderful and necessary on a daily basis
for all 2s. Bypass division, separation, or indecision through
listening, deep breathing, and gratitude.

Affirmation: *I am indivisible. I breathe deeply and feel connected to
the divine at all times. I am grateful for every experience that comes
my way and see hidden benefits to each encounter in my life*.

::: group
#### **ROOT NUMBER 3** {.h4}

A 3 person is highly creative, action oriented, and truthful and
radiates with joy. They are fluid in how they move through their life
experiences, and love to explore everything from their heart-center. 3
is connected to truth, fertility and creation. It is the number
representing the trinity of Mother-Father-Child. This trinity governs
creation---which is the numbers 1 (primal impulse) and 2 (desire for
peace) propelled into action. 3 people are usually very talented, very
vivacious, interested in many things, ingenious and brilliant. They are
curious and love to learn---asking questions all the time.
:::

3 is the first number in the Creation Triad and thus is fiercely
independent, seeking total freedom of movement. 3s have the artistic
touch even if they are not in the arts. This number requires that they
express themselves in some capacity, either through writing, speaking,
performing as a musician, dancer, or actor, being the star of a radio or
TV show or having a platform of some kind to share their message. 3s,
above anything, must communicate. They always have something to say!
They are fierce advocates of freedom of speech and expression. Their
natural yearning for renewal and birth gives them tremendous powers of
creation.

The 3-6-9 Creation Triad that number 3 belongs to infuses them with
compassion, tenderness, and a loving, affectionate disposition. They are
magnetic, and their smile lights up any room. 3s are impressionable and
can be easily influenced. This is especially true if others appeal to
their giving []{#ch03.xhtml#page_48 .pagebreak}and generous nature---or
show them appreciation so they feel valued and appreciated.

3 people have a great sense of humor and a cheerful disposition. Their
optimism is contagious, and they tend to see the world with the glass
half full---searching for the bright side of everything and in everyone.
When energetically aligned with their gifts, 3s are the most positive,
uplifting people to be around. No other vibration gives such light,
grace and is as enchanting!

3s can take any challenging situation and move quickly through
bitterness (or bypass it altogether) into a place of acceptance and
seeing it in a positive light. Their ability to "see" future positive
impact and outcomes for any current or past challenge stems from an
uncanny "bird's-eye" view 3s have, which allows them to fully move
through pain and trauma and come out the other side seemingly whole and
reborn. Thus their ability to reboot---literally *create* their
reality---as well as acknowledge the bright side in everything and
everyone, is one of their most powerful gifts. These talents, coupled
with their natural gifts of expression and outgoing personalities, make
3s adept at helping anyone feel good, whether it is an intimate friend
needing their support, or in brand new social situations. They are
experts at comfortably mixing with any group and have a knack for
adjusting quickly to different personalities or changing situations.

3

The image of the 3 is two wide-open half circles facing to the left,
gathering inspiration form the past and remolding it to manifest a new
creation. It has a welcoming feeling to it, and thus the embracing,
congenial nature of the 3 person---wrapping their two arms around
everyone they meet---is represented by the figure 3.

3s are born to inspire. They cast a spell by just being delightful,
motivating others to act through their passionate enthusiasm, happiness,
positive mindset, and optimistic attitude. Their spontaneity blends with
an effortless capacity to connect with anyone---be it in an elevator for
10 seconds or in any other social setting. Their natural charm, coupled
with their brilliant and personable magnetism, relaxes and "disarms"
anyone with whom they make contact.

For 3s everything comes down to furthering a deep ideal, something they
are so passionate about that they can't imagine anyone else not sharing
the same ideal with them. This ideal is their truth, and 3s, adherence
to what is true is one of their major drivers. They will leave no stone
unturned to find the truth. Thus they make great detectives. If you
answer a 3 in an evasive way, they'll not let you get away with it! 3s
can spot a lie []{#ch03.xhtml#page_49 .pagebreak}in a second. Even if
they are somehow heading down a misleading path, they will never stop
trying to search for the truth.

3s are not as driven to be successful in order to achieve a high
position or power in as much as they appreciate success due to the
pleasures and good life that achievement brings. 3s love a deliciously
prepared meal as much as beautiful surroundings and adornments. They
like to spoil themselves and their loved ones (and need to watch their
wallets).

3s thrive when they can travel. . . being with others, seeing the world,
and going on journeys wakes up their innate creativity and yearning for
independence. Plus they love to explore other countries, cultures,
music, and people---getting to know other ideas, religions, lifestyles,
and cultural paradigms. 3s are also deeply spiritual because 3 aligns
with their quest for truth.

3s love defending the underdog and are advocates for animals. They will
take risks---and when they couple their natural passion with their
willingness to take a chance, their impact is beautiful and great. Their
delightful, charming, magnetic personalities are a breath of fresh air
invoking a lightness of being.

Having a higher education is important for 3s and makes them feel part
of the higher ideals and philosophies they so cherish. They must have a
total sense of independence in any marriage union in order to feel the
freedom that is integral to their happiness. 3s appreciate and enjoy
luxury, which reflects the beauty and vibrant nature of their soul.

A balanced 3 will not succumb to moodiness or depression and will easily
forgive themselves as well as forgiving others. Having a good circle of
friends can help 3s to express their ideas and feelings, though the key
to their happiness is to engage in creative activities that totally
absorb them.

The key to a happy, meaningful life is for a 3 to *focus and
specialize*.

3 people must *persevere in their chosen specialty* and not get offtrack
and distracted by frivolous activities. They must only promise what they
can deliver and intend to accomplish.

When 3s know they are uplifting people, nothing will stop them. In their
natural, connected state, 3 people are luminous, vibrant beings of joy.

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

3s can and will multitask; however, their tendency to scatter and go
offtrack results in wasted energies when they are tired or out of
alignment. They can delay or dilute the impact of their divine mission
if they don't learn to how to focus and specialize in one direction at a
time. Vacillation can lead to indecision or going on tangents for hours,
days, or weeks at a time. 3s []{#ch03.xhtml#page_50 .pagebreak}like to
begin projects, but may have a more difficult time completing them,
since they can get distracted, and that is when they go off course.
:::

A 3 person also gets bored if not intellectually or creatively engaged
and may slack off if they lack self-motivation. 3s need to play and have
fun but can go too far and forget about their responsibilities
(disliking the whole idea of responsibility to themselves and others).
This happens especially when they don't have the organization to help
them stay focused on priorities. Thus they can get lazy about practicing
and developing their gifts. Dedication to their often outstanding
talents is supported by a systematic approach of their priorities. 3s
believe anything is permitted because it is so easy for them to attain
success as it is, so they use their natural happy and congenial nature
as an "escape" to chill more than is necessary.

When 3s stop consistently pursuing goals, during both easy and difficult
times, they may attribute their lack of practice to other factors. But
in the end, most inaction and lack of commitment is due to their lazy
attitude. This confusion about the **origin** of their lack of
initiative can throw them for a loop. It occurs especially when 3s
encounter mental blocks or tiredness and won't work through their
resistance with a conscious decision to act.

3s can be wise and philosophical, then witty and funny the next moment,
while abdicating discipline. This results in a lack of steady growth.
One of 3's lessons is to persevere steadfastly with their goals.

A 3 person also may have the tendency to be too talkative, sometimes
compulsively, so they need to guard against speaking when they don't
have something valuable or new to say.

There can always be too much of a good thing, and 3s can exaggerate and
even be superficial and "fake" or may make promises they can't keep.

The quickest cure for a negative emotional state or depression is to
"just do it"---to be creative. Express yourself in whichever way you
want to. Then, eventually, and usually quickly, you reconnect with the
beauty and joy in your soul and are happily on track and back in the
flow again---eager to share your gifts on some kind of stage.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_51 .pagebreak}Affirmation: *"I am happily engaged
with what I love to do. I lavish my focus and full attention on
activities that uplift me. I spend time with those who allow me to feel
light and free."*

::: group
#### **ROOT NUMBER 4** {.h4}

4 both is a grounding frequency (symbolizing the Earth) and carries a
mysterious quality connected to the divine. As a 4 you are practical,
trustworthy and have a hands-on approach to your life. When you commit
to something, you can be counted on to complete it. This is epitomized
by the square: four equal sides that symbolize architecture, home,
balance, and building something that lasts. So, on the one hand your
reliability, organizational skills, stable and calm demeanor,
self-discipline, meticulous attention to details, and responsible
character make you sought after as a family member, colleague, and
friend. But 4 is also an enigma, and you like it that way! (Even though
it results in others being perplexed by you.)
:::

The paradox of the 4 is that you always have one foot in the
