future---this is the inventor in you wanting to go the unconventional
route and thwarting all expectations. Your ideas and values are ahead of
their time, unconventional and even prophetic. You often just have a
"knowing" about what will transpire ahead of time long before it
happens. This other side of you favors individualism, a marked
originality, and sudden, unexpected events. As a living, walking paradox
(organized and unpredictable) you are seldom fully understood, but it is
what makes you so unique. You like being unconventional!

There is a "genius" quality to your 4 vibration allows your natural
curiosity to go off the beaten path. You naturally have the focus and
discipline to explore your hunches and intuitive downloads. After all,
you love a good quest to sink your teeth into! You are rarely deterred
once you've started on such a mission.

Though you are eager to explore all possibilities that exist beyond your
own personal life, when it comes down to making internal
adjustments---shifting your personal habits---you are very stubborn.
This four-square "box" can be your hiding place to avoid taking
responsibility for your own growth and transformation.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_52 .pagebreak}4

If you look at the visual image of the number 4, it stands on one leg
and points a big triangle to the heavens. Thus 4s are taking the
powerful 3-6-9 Triad of Creation and grounding it, bringing it down to
Earth---making it real and practical. The lesson for a 4 person is to
stay connected to Earth while exploring the wonderful gifts in the Triad
of Creation---at the same time. Then the discoveries and shifts are
*mirrored* in their personal lives as well, as reluctance to make
personal changes dissipates.

The balance between heaven and Earth is reflected in the merging of
intuition and intelligence---**applied equally across all four areas of
human life---physical, mental, emotional and spiritual**.

Thus 4 symbolizes the real reason for our life on Earth: *We are divine
beings of light having a human experience*. We are always connected
through the Triad of Creation to Source, to the Creator, and are here to
internalize the light into practical, real-time results. We are
reflectors of the love of God---and the number 4 invites us to remember
we are members of one big galactic family.

Living in a clean, organized environment is very important for you to
stay balanced and healthy. 4 governs feng shui---the art of keeping your
physical environment energetically clear and positive---so be sure to
"feng-shui" your home and work place often. Clarity of mind thrives when
you clear your life.

4 lies in the middle of the Manifestation Triad (2-4-8), thus taking the
intuitive insights of the number 2 and manifesting them into physical
form as real, practical results.

As a 4 you love being part of a family and cherish your friends. You are
tolerant and compassionate. Money and status is not of great interest to
you (though the other numbers in your Birth Code may show otherwise).
You mix with people of all means, not caring about rank or class. It's
the "inner genius" in you---your surroundings might go unnoticed in
favor of your imagination! You live for this moment. And your tolerance
for others is exhibited in "to each their own"---something you expect in
return!

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

When you are energetically out of alignment a rigid approach to life
will appear. This fixed nature can get you stuck in a rut, as you hang
on to your opinions as if they mean more than the people you are with.
Being headstrong can also lead to arguments. A tendency to work long
hours (which naturally suits you) may turn into overwork, so be careful
about crossing the line when it comes to fulfilling tasks. If you notice
it gets to the point where you get too busy and don't ever stop to smell
the roses, take the queue and make time to simply relax and enjoy life.
Emotionally you can close down, not demonstrate affection.
:::

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_53 .pagebreak}You may also get too serious at times,
forgetting to lighten up and go with the flow. When you find yourself
not responding to humor---and leading a humorless life---it's a sign for
you to loosen up! Hanging on to old habits and mind patterns or living
in a disorganized space will exacerbate being stuck.

Guard against being careless and not fulfilling your responsibilities. A
real disconnection from the positive expression of your number 4 results
in dishonesty and a completely undisciplined lifestyle. In this
disoriented emotional state you can inflict needless pain on yourself
through envy, jealousy, self-pity, and resentment of others. You will
waste your most precious commodity---time---as well as other resources
while fixating on comparing yourself to others or feeling self-blame and
guilt, rather than lifting yourself out of the situation (no matter how
challenging it seems at the time) by taking a step of faith, owning your
experience of it, and being accountable. For you, just doing something
valuable, no matter how big or small the gesture is, sets you back on
track!

Affirmation: *I am whole, I am complete, I am more than enough, I am who
I am---I live and let live*.

::: group
#### **ROOT NUMBER 5** {.h4}

We have arrived at the midpoint. 5 is the number right in the middle of
1 and 9.
:::

5

If you look at the image of the number 5 you can see that it faces left
(the past) at the bottom and right (the future) at the top. 5 has two
straight lines and a curved line. Thus 5 is a visual representation of
the **pivot point,** representing versatility, movement, decisions,
risk, and a new beginning of some kind.

5 also lies in the midpoint of all three triads, as well as being in the
middle of the Mind Triad (1-5-7). In this position, 5 expands your
original creative ideas through a keen intellect and intelligence. You
are adept at capturing all the various angles of a question with your
uncommon perception. You are naturally connected to higher consciousness
by virtue of your keen sense of freedom and adventure.

Exploring the unknown is your forte---whether through physical travel,
or in your mind. You are inspired by your insatiable curiosity to
experience all there is to experience! 5 governs the senses, so you want
to taste, see, smell, touch, and hear as much as you can. Though this
can result in distractions (something to watch!) you are also the
ultimate multitasker []{#ch03.xhtml#page_54 .pagebreak}and so are
designed to handle multiple tasks at one time, depending on the nature
each task requires your full attention or not. The 5 vibration is by
nature very sensual and spiritual.

You have a great magnetism and charm, which make you very attractive.
When you feel fulfilled and happy your enthusiasm makes you
irresistible, and you naturally become the center of attention in any
gathering or group.

Connection is one of your key themes. . . connecting via voice, the
internet, writing, publishing, video, radio, television, film, the arts.
You use some kind of media to meet others, gather information, share
your message---all with the goal of bringing people together. 5 governs
groups or crowds of people, making you an adept social networker as well
as performer, writer, or speaker. You enjoy big crowds! This gift of
connection also makes you a wonderful salesperson---you can sell ice to
Eskimos as long as you passionately believe it to be of value. This
persuasion power and your natural charm aligns you magically with anyone
who experiences your words, music, art, or message.

The 5 vibration is very alert and bright---not much escapes your notice.
You have an innate connection to your surroundings that makes you
extremely fine-tuned, noticing everything in great detail.

Other keywords for a 5 person are change and freedom. You are very
adaptable and thrive when there is movement---stagnation and boredom are
your greatest fears. You are the intrepid adventurer and enjoy travel or
anything that opens your heart and mind to new things, ideas, and
cultures. Being fearless is something you naturally teach others just by
the virtue of who you are. Being so engaged in the moment makes you
flexible and versatile, which delights not only you but others who come
into contact with you. You win people over with your irresistible charm
and wit, making you popular in general and helping you personally to
create momentum to bring your divine gifts to a greater audience.

Thus freedom of movement is integral to your life. You may change where
you live, travel, or wander all over the world looking for inspiration
and excitement. You also can change your mind, sometimes abruptly from
one moment to the next. Oscillation is the nature of the 5, also due to
your restless, adventurous nature. You need to feel your imagination
engaged. Stimulation of all your senses is an important factor in your
well-being.

This excitement factor shows your ability to dazzle with your
brilliance. Applause and accolades are natural by-products for you when
you live at your highest vibrational frequency. Your personality is
vivacious. Due to your alignment to subtle energetics, you have a great
sensitivity for beautiful things---both artistic and intellectual. Just
be aware that you tend to keep from emotionally engaging with ideas or
people, and this can lead to an indifference about relationships.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_55 .pagebreak}As a 5 person you are an agent of
change for others. Your enthusiasm and daring exhibit a wonderful zest
for life. It's as if you never grew up and have the radiant mind of a
child in your heart throughout your life. Your willingness to experience
all that the world has to offer and every facet of our human experience
is both inspiring and motivational. Due to your natural versatility and
openness, setbacks don't affect you for long---you are able to rebound
quickly and move on living so beautifully in the present moment.

5 encompasses the whole human experience, all five senses, and all
contradictions as well. Wherever you are, something is "happening,"
something is moving. You love life, adventure, and liberty. You thrive
to experience, vibrate, and live to your fullest capacity. The pivot
point aspect of your number also indicates that you may fluctuate from
feeling totally exalted to profoundly down for seemingly no
reason---except that others just don't understand how intensely you
**experience** life and that you thus need time to adjust. Your approach
is one of total immersion---taking in the obvious and all the subtleties
at once. Others around you may not be as tuned into the subtle energies
that you pick up, but it is this full-immersion experience that delights
and inspires you the most.

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

You may be very critical when you are not energetically aligned with the
positive expression of number 5, and this will lead to an urge to spot
mistakes and flaws and point them out (others, and your own). Try not to
be impatient when doing so, or refrain altogether.
:::

You may be quick to use your mind instead of your heart to over-analyze
people and situations, using the intellect instead of your feelings to
find answers. Logic appeals to you however, you must be vulnerable and
open up the tenderness in your heart. Getting analytical at the expense
of heart-to-heart connections, especially in your intimate
relationships, can lead to endings and breakups. Yes, love runs deep,
but under too much incessant scrutiny, it has no breathing room to live
and thrive. Using your instincts to navigate love, instead of talking
through it or intellectualizing the experience (thereby not allowing the
space to assimilate feelings), is important if you are to maintain deep,
loving relationships.

You can be high-strung, have a nervous disposition, and crave change for
the sake of change. Guard against impulsive actions---and reactions. Any
restlessness you have can be channeled into doing something new!

Addiction is another shadow side of this number, since you want to try
everything. If you go too far, then you forget to use discernment and to
choose only what is for your highest good. Since you crave change and
[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_56 .pagebreak}are so versatile, you may enter and
exit relationships quickly, rather than allowing them to evolve and
grow.

If you find yourself criticizing others while at the same time not being
responsible for your own life, you will vacillate through life blindly,
not seeing a need to course-correct, not recognizing the valuable
feedback coming your way, and not benefitting from the experiences that
would enable you to mature emotionally.

Your attention is captured by many things at once, and so you may not
stay true to your *initial* impulses. Patience and learning how to
center your brilliant, magnificent gifts are the key for you to maintain
calm and peace and your delightful enthusiasm for life.

Affirmation: *I sing a song of delight. I take pleasure in everything I
encounter. I surrender. I feel blessed!*

::: group
#### **ROOT NUMBER 6** {.h4}

As a 6 person you are deeply compassionate, loving, and responsible
toward your family and friends. You have a calming influence on others.
6 is aligned with beauty and is the middle number in the 3-6-9 Creation
Triad giving birth to the creative seeds and impulses received from the
number 3.
:::

6

If you look at the image of the 6, it is shaped in the form of a woman
who is with child---pregnant with a large belly, about to give birth and
take on the responsibility of a parent. This is the key to the number
6---nurturing others, being of loving service to others, being
supportive and utterly devoted. You naturally want to "mother" and share
your advice. Inevitably people, friends, even strangers, will come to
you and tell you their deepest secrets, share private and personal
information with you that they wouldn't with others. You exude a warmth,
compassion, and wisdom that holds the space for love. It's like you hold
an invisible invitation for others to seek you out as an advisor,
healer, mentor. . . without you actually having put out any conscious
signals. Thus make sure you consciously create boundaries, otherwise you
will feel energetically depleted. Also, make sure you make room in your
life to nurture **yourself**---with massage, reflexology, energy
healing---to recharge your vibrational field. You love to give, and you
must learn to receive the bounty of love and luxuries life has to offer!

You love to give affection and hugs and are very generous with your
resources and time. Your natural poise and charisma make you highly
magnetic. . . when you walk into a room, people take note!

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_57 .pagebreak}6 governs human love and romance as
well as money and abundance. In your intimate relationships, once you
commit to a partnership you are devoted. This devotion extends to your
loved ones and friends---who genuinely love you. You can get sentimental
(and may try to hide this) and very idealistic. You are attuned to
exhibiting good manners and are tasteful, yet will not shy away from
expressing yourself strongly when you feel passionate about something.

Harmony and beauty are so important to your well-being, and to attract
abundance you must surround yourself with high aesthetics. Jarring
noises, conflict, arguments, discord, jealousy, and unresolved issues
are best eliminated or dealt with as quickly as possible in order for
you to pursue the rest of your day at peace.

Your natural artistic side needs to be expressed. You naturally enjoy
beautiful music, exquisite art, furniture, and clothing, so adorn and
surround yourself with beauty to feel good and whole. When at home,
though, you like to dress comfortably. As a 6 it is important for you to
live in a sensually pleasing environment. Anything that feels "ugly"
needs to be removed---you are so sensitive to vibration, sound, and
visuals. You love having your favorite colors and artwork in your home.
Living in a place of serenity and beauty pleases you to no end.

Money is attracted to you when you are positively aligned with your
Birth Code. Sometimes it can appear without much effort through
inheritances, wealthy friends, or sponsors, but just as often it is
through your talents and abilities that magnetically attract abundance.

You are highly creative and must find an outlet at work or elsewhere to
express your innate artistic gifts. Use your voice whenever you can, the
sound of your voice carries healing vibrations. You can use it in your
career to speak, teach, counsel others, share information, or sing, in
the healing arts or in politics. Like the number 3, you have a smile
that is irresistible!

You also are very attuned to justice, seeking to find the underlying
fair response to any situation. This means you want the law to be upheld
and understand the need the rules of law has to honor the basic needs
and sanctity for any person.

As a 6 you are good at finishing projects once you can get yourself
started.

::: group
#### []{#ch03.xhtml#page_58 .pagebreak}**Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

6 out of alignment can lead to a controlling and interfering nature,
where you meddle in other people's business. This can be reflected in
your family relationships, partnerships or friendships. Then you'll
argue your point to stay in power and cause a lot of disruption. This
bossy side will replace your natural nurturing instincts with a
domineering attitude towards others.
:::

You can be a perfectionist and this can lead to criticism of others,
since you will expect them to perform to your high standards. Sometimes
you can resort to self-righteous behavior. Another shadow side of the 6
expression is total self-absorption.

When not aligned, money matters can range along a spectrum from where
you overspend and are too extravagant or extremely stingy. Regarding
overindulgence, you need to watch your sweet tooth!

Another challenging aspect of this 6 vibration is that you may want to
follow the path of least resistance (and keep a false sense of harmony).
You can be careless concerning your responsibilities, especially
regarding the obligation you have to yourself to fulfill your divine
mission. This will create a quality of being a "drifter," someone who
does not make commitments to themselves and would rather "go with the
flow," drifting from here to there to nowhere, since there was no
conscious dedication to a specific mission or project or goal. Your
indecision, laziness, and feeling like you are being inconvenienced by
choosing to commit to something will make you the root cause of your
failed half-hearted attempts. It also creates a spiraling tendency to
magnify difficulties and obsess on problems, which are quite often not
even real.

**Everyone** is confronted with adversity, lackluster days, and
challenges; thus it is vital for a 6 person to overcome the inertia that
can recur a daily basis or every so often.

In order for you as a 6 to accomplish something meaningful and joyful,
something that has *real impact* on your life, you must be motivated
internally and externally to do anything---preferably through a goal or
deadline---so as to overcome your occasional passive nature. Then you
will shower the world with your loving radiance and brilliance!

Affirmation: *I share my love freely and generously. I practice using my
gifts every day. I nurture myself. I care deeply about my divine mission
to uplift others through love and joy*.

::: group
#### []{#ch03.xhtml#page_59 .pagebreak}**ROOT NUMBER 7** {.h4}

7 is a number of the spiritual seeker, the sensitive, mindful
philosopher, and, brilliant analyzer. As a 7 you are driven to
understand the mysteries of life, to grasp the unknown. You are
comfortable with secret subjects, the healing modalities, and usually
have vivid dreams. Even if you are not attracted to spiritual subjects,
as a 7 you love to learn, read books (you may have books in every room
of your home), and educate yourself---exhibiting a quest for gathering
knowledge and gaining understanding.
:::

Ultimately 7 is the number of spiritual completion. Inner peace and calm
are brought about through bridging the higher world with the world
below---heaven and Earth---as the inner and outer realms are understood
to be one and the same.

7

The image of the number 7 has a horizontal line at the top, symbolizing
the world above, or heaven, with a diagonal line reaching below,
signifying a bridging to the lower world. 7 also looks like a lightning
bolt and symbolizes lightning insights, intuitive downloads that come
out of the blue and light up your mind. So 7 can bridge anything, making
connections between ideas and subjects that seemingly have no common
ground, such as good and evil, light and dark. As a symbol of lightning,
7s can experience sudden profound shifts in their lives that take them
by total surprise. The effect of the lightning bolt also makes 7 a
"change agent." Often their presence alone can soothe and heal.

Notice, too, that the 7 "opens up" to the left---the past. Thus 7 has a
good memory, and enjoys looking back at history to gather wisdom and
understanding of the present. 7 "points" diagonally to the upper left,
which signifies its interest in developing new ways of being, future
technological or scientific breakthroughs, psychic premonitions of the
future, and an intuitive understanding of reaching into other
dimensions. Thus a 7 person often has unorthodox, unique beliefs and
values.

Due to their quest for knowledge, 7 people need to travel extensively at
some point in their lifetime or read many books about other lands, other
cultures, and even beyond Earth, space, and time.

Financially it is important for 7s to have a nest egg. Otherwise they
get nervous about the future. This anxious tendency can interfere with
their ultimate mission to be a channel for new wisdom.

7 symbolizes the original seven Wonders of the World, great mystery,
magic, and ceremony. Thus as a 7 person you have a tendency to look
deeply at everything. You are an observer of the mysteries of life, a
seeker of wisdom, and a natural researcher. You do best when you have
extended periods of time alone---sometimes even going through periods
where you []{#ch03.xhtml#page_60 .pagebreak}are a hermit. In fact, it's
best for you to work alone. As Pythagoras said, "Those who desire wisdom
should look for it in solitude."

Your views and values can at times be mysterious to others, as your
quest for wisdom possibly changed the beliefs of your early life and
helped you connect your divine nature.

7 is the final number in the 1-5-7 Mind Triad. Thus it carries
tremendous intelligence. You can be taken aback at times by the lack of
understanding and intellectual capacities in others. For you the
questions of "Why?" are truly integral to your thirst for knowledge. You
like to approach life from a logical perspective, yet eventually must
merge intuition with logic to get to the deeper mysteries you yearn to
solve. Specializing in any field suits you well, as you can then put all
your eggs in one basket and delve into the infinite depths, exploring
knowledge and wisdom indefinitely. If you ever feel the well has dried
up or been explored completely, it is important for you to find another
source of life to satisfy your natural curiosity and to expand your
knowledge and inner capacity to cradle great wisdom. You're naturally
not a fan of anything frivolous or superficial.

You do not like to be under anyone's watchful eye! That includes an
abhorrence of "Big Brother." Any person or entity that invades your
privacy, which you guard like a lioness guards her cubs, is not welcome.
You keep your private life secret and at the same time have "eyes in
back of your head," taking in everything around you. When you enter a
space you feel what's going on, even though you'd never let on about
it. . . this is what makes 7 a number of holding secrets. It is no
coincidence the most famous fictional spy, James Bond, is "007"!

If a 7 person goes into the creative arts, their ability to both learn
and intuitively channel makes them quite a magnetic and unique
performer, writer or artist in any field.

In your intimate relationships you need privacy and a "cave" to escape
to for solitude. You can be very loving and devoted, as long as you
don't expect your partner to live up to your long list of ideals. Since
you can intuitively sense the true from the untrue, you can jump ahead
and not create the space for your partner to discover the wisdom and
truth in their own way and on their own time. Others need to earn their
trust with you, but once they have it you embrace them with complete
non-judgment and openness---and in turn expect the same from them!

You thrive when you are in nature---especially near the ocean. Take many
getaways---7 rules rest, rejuvenation, meditation, and sabbaticals.
Refresh your heart, mind, and soul with long stays in places that feel
like spiritual sanctuaries.

The bridge that 7 symbolizes will be a metaphor for growth all your
life. Bring the sacredness of bridging light and dark, seen and unseen,
into []{#ch03.xhtml#page_61 .pagebreak}your daily life. Make your life a
ceremony, a devoted song to Spirit, Source, or God. You understand the
reason for darkness, and you, as the lightning bolt of truth, radiate
brilliance. You are a beacon of light in the world. Shining your light
in darkness in whatever way, shape, or form that takes, is your divine
gift. Opening up the sacred halls of wisdom within you will give you
direct access to the truth---as revealed in the records of time and
timelessness.

Always remember, your divine mission can benefit a big community of
like-minded souls---and then reach out to inspire the world.

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

Due to your wisdom and natural quest for knowledge, you can get
impatient with those who in your mind cannot "catch on" fast enough.
Also, since you can easily spot when something is wrong, your
perfectionism may turn you into a critic with a need for perfect
results---rather than being open to what is for the highest good of the
situation. Guard against being cynical about life, either because others
have disappointed you, or due to unresolved emotions arising from
previous life experiences.
:::

You have a strong personality, so it's important for you to balance your
strong energy with time for playfulness. Otherwise you will focus on the
powerful, accomplishment qualities of the 7 at the expense of joy and
love.

You can be very secretive, not revealing much about your true
motivations. It's natural for you to keep your own issues private, yet
not at the expense of being distrustful or not trusting of others. In
intimate relationships it is important for you to be vulnerable
*emotionally*, not just *intellectually* (sometimes you mistake the
intellectual openness for emotional vulnerability).

When out of alignment you get pessimistic and frustrated. Know, this is
when you try to direct your aha moments in an obsessive way, rather than
being a channel for light and love, without conditions on how or in what
area that wisdom is to stream through you. A change of place or time in
nature will usually help you reconnect very quickly!

Affirmation: *I am truth embodied. My soul is my true home. I live to
share the light of wisdom*.

::: group
#### []{#ch03.xhtml#page_62 .pagebreak}**ROOT NUMBER 8** {.h4}

8 is the vibration of leadership and strength, abundance, financial
security, and power. 8 people have a vision that must be made practical.
Thus 8 governs entrepreneurship and the executive. 8s are responsible
and patient by nature, allowing them to take an idea from its inception
to a successful outcome. It is natural for an 8 person to at some point
in their life to experience obstacles and ups and downs---however, these
are designed to be overcome in order to gain confidence and strength. As
an 8 person you use any challenges as stepping-stones to success.
:::

You are shy and reserved by nature. It is not immediately obvious that
you have the fortitude to push forward, but you persist every step of
the way, and eventually reach your goal. Nothing and no-one will stop
you from achieving your mission. Your quiet nature is a protection of
your intensely driven nature to reach the pinnacle of your profession.
Your strength, fortitude, and internal power to succeed are exhibited in
the visual image of the number 8.

8 is the final of three numbers in the 2-4-8 Manifestation Triad.

8

8 looks like a vertical infinity symbol---and it does represent eternal
life. This is the only number besides 0 which you can draw repeatedly
without lifting your pen. 8 is also visual representation of two
windows, with the window above giving a vision of the spiritual and the
one below relating to the material. Thus 8 represents making visions
(messages from spirit) real, bringing them to Earth, and materializing
them into goods that can be exchanged for money.

8 represents the energy exchange of money.

8 is aligned with business, in that this vibration takes a vision
(spirit), creates a product or service (matter), puts it out into the
world (enterprise), and in return receives payment for that product or
service. This is one of the core spiritual and human energy exchanges to
life. Whereas the number 4 symbolizes the manifestation of creative
ideas, 8 takes it one step further by adding the financial energy
exchange. Both the spiritual and material realms represented by the
number 8 are necessary to experience fulfillment and abundance. In some
way or another an 8 person will be focused on money
manifestation---whether they have it or not. Usually they will have
experiences of both. Either way, it is only once their soul is
completely free to manifest those messages from spirit that 8 people
realize their dreams of lasting abundance and fulfillment. Often, they
end up as an example or teacher of spiritual, manifestation, and/or
financial laws.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_63 .pagebreak}An 8 person is meant to lead in some
capacity. They need not be a success in the financial or business world,
as long as they have access to an environment where they can inspire
others to greater heights with their vision. The infinity symbol also
implies that 8 people are like a battery that keeps going and going,
never giving up.

At the same time, you as an 8 are very realistic and have great
organizational skills. Your innate patience and intelligence allow you
to excel at anything. You are born with a desire to take on
responsibilities, so it is rare to find an 8 who is careless, since they
pride themselves on living up to the highest expectations. Their
reliability is legendary, and so is their warmth.

8s like to keep a certain image of themselves that is strong as befits
the leaders they are. However they do care about what others feel about
them, especially when it comes to their accomplishments, and do
(privately) enjoy compliments.

The symbol of infinity is also reflected in the balance of justice and
honor that 8 people represent. They have a very advanced sense of what
is ethical and true, representing honor, impartiality, and dignity in
everything they say and do. Thus they also like to mix with dignitaries,
seeking the company of important, influential people---a group that they
naturally know they "belong" to.

It is important for you as an 8 person to share your resources with
others in a philanthropic way. When positively aligned, 8s can
materialize anything---they are magical at turning their visions into
reality. Their penchant for persistence and courage as well as their
cooperative nature, allows 8s to accomplish anything they set their mind
to when it comes to working with others. 8 people are ambitious, enjoy
challenges, and strive to be the best they can be. They have both
originality and inspiration, so as long as they create something that
fulfills them at soul-level, combining their multiple talents in a
practical way, they will be successful. They can act as instruments of
positive shifts in other people's lives.

As friends they are loyal, dedicated, and so sweet with those whom they
trust and care for deeply. However, due to their need to appear strong
with no need in the world, 8s can feel lonely, with a great need to be
loved and cherished. If a dear friend or family member needs them for
any purpose, the 8 person will make sacrifices for them---no questions
asked. They will do the same for an ideal.

You as an 8 person are only attracted to quality and will not be seen
shopping for secondhand clothes. You value the best and will wait to
secure the highest quality in favor of a cheaper version. This is
because you are aligned with the vibration of longevity.

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_64 .pagebreak}As an 8 your dreams are never small!
Everything you do has to exhibit your highest expectations of what is
"the best." 8s have the inner courage, the natural leadership, and the
vision to achieve greatness in any field. Their enjoyment of challenges
and creating the best possible outcome for the highest good of all makes
them unstoppable and wonderful contributors and influencers.

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

An 8 out of alignment is egotistical, materialistic, and forceful---or
succumbs to passive and powerless behavior. Their longing for success
can outweigh their desire for happiness. Thus 8s must pay attention to
their heart. . . if there is a feeling of loneliness, if there is a
sense of longing for something that is missing, an 8 must not be afraid
to pursue happiness with the same wisdom, maturity, and discipline that
they devote to their divine mission.
:::

8s are demanding of themselves and transfer that quest for excellence
and success onto others, which is not necessarily a negative unless it
is expected and those who do not measure up are judged. You may take
your ambitious drive too far if you are out of alignment energetically.
You will work without reservation for many hours to achieve your goal
but can forget to stop and smell the roses, not allowing yourself to
enjoy anything else on the journey you are taking. This means you may
not be able to fully enjoy the actual goal once you attain it. . . you
have put so much focus on the getting the result that when it happens,
you refocus on the next goal without taking some time to appreciate the
beauty you've created. Eventually this lack of appreciation along the
way can lead to frustration and dissatisfaction.

Your are dedication to being actively engaged in the pursuit of your
vision is commendable as long as you pay attention when you feel
restless, or that there is something "missing" along the way. If not,
you might eventually react with tremendous anger when provoked or
exhibit a suctioning of strength in your physical body that translates
into health conditions or a need for rest.

Guard against being egotistical and vindictive, obstinate, intolerant,
and stubborn.

Affirmation: *I give everything to inspire others to be the best they
can be. My deeds are my expressions of wealth and well-being. I am
enriched by helping to enrich others*.

::: group
#### []{#ch03.xhtml#page_65 .pagebreak}**ROOT NUMBER 9** {.h4}

9 is the number of transformation---something needs to end to begin
again. Thus 9 can regenerate itself over and over again and exhibits a
great determination. This number symbolizes evolution and an enhancement
of psychic abilities and clairvoyance. You'll see shortly how the
regeneration quality of the number 9 is confirmed in mathematics and the
whole human experience on Earth---9 is the King of Numbers and will
reign forever. A 9 person is warm, outgoing, and loving with a dramatic
flair, exuding a magnetic personality that allows him or her to get
along with pretty much anyone. 9s are compassionate, romantic, filled
with unconditional love, kind, empathetic, patient, tolerant, and wise.
You as a 9 are an inspirational and compassionate humanitarian with
great idealism and strong willpower. Your imagination knows no bounds!
And you absolutely love to give.
:::

As a 9 you have a powerful personality, and you can use it to fulfill
your greatest desire---to be useful to others by manifesting
inspirational accomplishments and/or beneficial products or results. You
represent *leadership by example*---others will look to you as an
example to be followed, whether you are aware of it or not. Your
charisma exudes loving confidence, so you need to accept the example you
set and allow the quality of life you lead to speak for itself, since it
will be emulated by others. You *live* your talk. You want your high
ideals to inspire others so they too experience their highest potential.

Your sweet-natured soul does not like seeing anyone in pain. When you
see someone who is suffering, you reach out to them since you truly care
about how others feel. And if you have healing balm or
stress-alleviation tool, you will share it. You are a natural at
teaching, healing, and giving counsel through the highest values of love
and beauty. Your ultimate goal is to raise the vibrational awareness of
humanity.

You are naturally very direct and expect the same from others---what you
say is exactly how you feel. So you don't tend to play games to get what
you want; you just ask for what you want!

9

9 has a circle at the top, representing a big head filled with wisdom
(or ego) learned from the numbers 1 through 8 that preceded it. The
"head" is connected to Earth by a line on the right side, representing
the artistic, creative side of the human experience. The wisdom and
leadership of 9 make it very evolved. You are here to help people, often
through major transitions, since 9 also represents endings. In order to
have the capacity to love deeply, without judgment or expectation, you
yourself experienced hardship and tests. Those who are born to help
others experience the pain []{#ch03.xhtml#page_66 .pagebreak}and loss
themselves in order to forgive and have compassion at the deepest level
of the human experience.

Another result of your emotional connection is that you understand
people from all walks of life. You respect all their various qualities
and missions. You also love giving back---having a charitable and
philanthropic nature. Your sensitive, artistic nature blends with your
quest for perfection. As a leader you demand only the best from
yourself.

9 is the final number in the 3-6-9 Creation Triad and thus represents a
culmination and celebration of a mission accomplished. Your main lesson
is to elevate what is seemingly everyday and ordinary into something
that is extraordinary and meaningful.

You are naturally honest and direct---getting straight to the point and
penetrating directly to the heart of the matter. When others are not
direct with you, it takes you by surprise. Other people's dishonesty,
manipulation, or indirectness can catch you off-guard, so you need to
learn to be more cautious with others, but not when you are teaching.
Another quality to guard against is your impatience with those who think
more slowly than you do or others who don't recognize the thought
patterns and actions that lead up to a mistake. You like to be in
control on some level, so this can be a challenging area for you.

No detail escapes your keen observation---as you have a clear, sharp
mind that penetrates quickly to the root of the matter while grasping
the overall picture. So you are conscious of all energy, subtle and
visible, happening around you.

In relationships you may strive to be in control. With your independent
streak, you may keep your distance, which results in a lack of true
intimacy. You can be an enigma in this way, due to your warm, generous
nature and your lack of commitment to a serious relationship. This is
also connected 9's symbol of endings, so you somehow know that
everything will come to an end, and this may keep you from fully
engaging with another heart-to-heart.

You approach life with total passion and a profound intensity. Your
vibrant and noble nature, enthusiasm, and generosity are noted by
everyone who is blessed to be in your presence.

::: group
#### **Challenging expressions:** {.h4}

When you are energetically out of alignment you hold onto resentments or
memories, not letting them go. You become resentful of life and can shut
down emotionally. Guard against being arrogant, tyrannical, or
dishonest. An abdication of leadership can result in you closing your
mind to wisdom and drifting through life aimlessly---dissipating your
gifts. Frustration is a sign that you must reconnect with your
heart-center and surrender to love.
:::

[]{#ch03.xhtml#page_67 .pagebreak}Guard against focusing on limitations.
This will push you to want to control others, since you are not healing
your own sense of lack within first. Rather than feeling the need to
control, shift your focus onto creating beauty, love, and excellence.
Your role is to exude the joy of living a life to its highest potential.
When you focus on what is for your highest good, your emotional
touchiness will naturally disappear.

When out of alignment you can be stubborn, reacting with aggressive
action and creating conflict as a result. Though your temper can rise to
a boil quickly, you can just as quickly move on, ready to forgive and
forget.

Your natural inclination to be direct can turn into a frankness that is
too confrontational or aggressive. Speaking your mind without caring
about how this might affect the other person(s) results in consequences
that are not healing or beneficial. Refrain from reacting
instantaneously, especially when the result is biting in nature.

Deep down you can have a fear of rejection and then will feel a lack of
confidence. Then, reassurance that you are appreciated, understood,
respected, and loved is something you need and crave.

Affirmation: *I serve others with love and wisdom. I stay true to my
heart, leading always with love and for the highest good of all*.

[]{#ch04.xhtml}

## []{#ch04.xhtml#page_68 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 4]{.f3} {#ch04.xhtml#ch04 .h2n}

## MASTER NUMBERS 11--99 {.h2t}

[N]{.dropcap}[OW WE WILL ENTER THE MYSTERIOUS REALM OF DOUBLE-DIGIT
NUMBERS]{.f3} 11, 22, 33, 44, 55, 66, 77, 88, [AND]{.f3} 99, [ALSO
REFERRED TO AS "MASTER NUMBERS]{.f3}." A Master Numbers is an
intensification of a single-digit number, so the core meaning of the
single-digit before it is doubled, is incorporated in a new experience,
which takes on messages of the single and double digit and *blends* them
into a *new* vision.

Master Numbers by nature carry a greater responsibility than
single-digit vibrations. In order to elevate yourself to the higher
calling of a Master Number you must listen intently to your inner
calling, which always will reveal your soul's chosen path.

::: group
### []{#ch04.xhtml#page_69 .pagebreak}MASTER NUMBER 11 {.h3}

If your Day of Birth is 11 or 29 or your Life Purpose or Destiny reduces
to 11 (such as 38, 47, 56, etc. and 119, 128, 137, etc.), then Master
Number 11 is one of your Three Important Birth Numbers.
:::

*Please read the meaning for number 2 (in [chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)), the "root number" for 11, as well*.

When 1 becomes 11, the *original creative mind* and *leadership* of
number 1 are incorporated into 11 as the Psychic Master, blending 1 into
an experience of double new beginnings and enlightened leadership. 11 is
supreme balance. Balance between light and dark, masculine and feminine,
the seen and unseen, the known and unknown. Thus you as an 11 symbolize
both the seen and unseen, which need to be brought into equilibrium.
However, there is an illusion heaven and earth, visible and invisible,
are separate, and you must bypass this illusion of division by uniting
seemingly separate energies and goals. When you do so, you will stop
feeling a sense of incompletion and division running through your life.

As a "Master Number" you are being asked to master something at a high
level. For the 11 you are mastering listening to your inner voice---the
only true voice connected to your divinity, your soul. Anytime you feel
a sense of separation or division, tune in. This division could appear
from a person or an interfering idea or ignorance. If you refuse to see
*both* sides, listen and understand, you will prevent a rebalancing of
energy from occurring. In all cases of conflict or separation your role
is to find out the source of opposing energy. Then the magical shift
happens when you understand the Law of Opposites. That in order to
experience light you must also know darkness. Then, exquisite harmony
and peace infuse your heart as you listen intently---surrendering to the
light of wisdom within you.

Any nervousness, which comes as a result of 11 ruling light and
electrical currents, can be healed through establishing routine and
order in your life.

The ancient temples of mystery had a pillar on each side of the
entrance, looking very much like the figure 11. These pillars are a
doorway and symbolize an initiation. Your overall divine mission is to
delve into the mysteries and miracles of life---to walk *through* the
two pillars and unite active and passive, emptiness and fullness,
receptivity and action. All becomes *one* within you. When you enter the
Temple of Awareness, you have made a choice to live fully, with total
acceptance of every situation that appears before you as being by your
design, your beckoning---and always for your highest good. No matter how
it appears!

::: land100
[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_70
.pagebreak}![Image](./f0070-01.jpg){#f0070-01}
:::

[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_71 .pagebreak}*"In order to elevate yourself to the
higher calling of a Master Number you must listen intently to your inner
calling which always will reveal your soul's chosen path."*

Anything can be channeled through this opening---a new invention, an
intuitive download, a piece of music or art, a book. Channeling a gift
is the highest expression of this number. The gift is always bringing
forth brand-new information and inspiration---the initial experience of
the unknown, thus making the unknown visible.

It is no surprise then that 11 symbolizes light (the word "light" adds
up to 29/11 using the Pythagorean system).

As an 11 you illuminate the truth. You have a choice to illuminate
negative or positive energy, but you *will* channel energy and bring it
to light. To prepare to channel what is *for your highest good*, it is
initially important for you to discover your "inner teacher."
Reconnecting to your inner voice is another way of describing your
conscious engagement with your spiritual guides. You also receive great
inspiration through symbols, music, art, and sacred geometry. Aligning
to your soul opens up a universe of wisdom that you can access at will,
instantaneously, and then share with others. It is by walking between
light and dark, keeping the balance, standing secure on both feet, like
the 11, that allows you to open up your creative vessel and let the
divine pour through the 11.

You must always choose which endeavors in your life bring unity and
which cause separation. You will need to get off the fence and make a
choice. That choice will enable you to enter the 11 gateway, take that
risk, and live fully in the present moment. This is when you feel whole.
Once the way to unity is recognized, honored, and practiced
continuously, you leave the struggle and division behind. You feel at
peace. It is in the act of surrender that you fulfill your role to be a
Master of Light and Love.

If you don't step through the gateway, explore your inner world---both
the light and the darkness---you will project your fantasies and
neuroses on others instead and eventually sabotage your goals. Life is
filled with paradoxes, so there is no reason to doubt the importance of
every experience as being valid. If you exclude exploring all sides of
an issue you leave out part of the human experience. Your role is to be
unconditional in your tolerance of those people and experiences that
seem different. Then your 11 gateway is totally about freedom and
unconditional love.

[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_72 .pagebreak}In exploring the dark and the light,
the seen and the unseen, nothing escapes you, and you walk the world an
avatar of love. Instead of fighting injustice, you heal. Instead of
resisting oppression and pain, you understand that *all* that happens to
you has been called in by your soul. Nothing happens to us that is not
ultimately for our highest good.

As an 11 you understand there is a veil of illusion---maya---that
appears once we are born on Earth, protecting us from knowing everything
we've experienced and will experience. Otherwise we would be overwhelmed
and not able to function. That veil is lifted for a bit every time we
enter the 11 portal. In the entering of the gateway, light beams through
our third eye and reveals our true divine origin. We become "seers"
enlightened by entering the light. This is the moment-to-moment
enlightenment, the union with love we so yearn for. So, the more you as
an 11 trust and surrender to your intuition, the higher you raise your
vibration. 11 is the Master teacher.

Anyone who crosses your path will be enchanted by your undeniable
charisma. You just change people by the sheer influence of your powerful
aura. For you personally this spiritual essence appears as unexpected
windfalls, seemingly coincidental, that appear in synchronicity with
your goals---guiding you to the light so that you can play the leading
role you are meant to. Surprises and unexpected events are part of your
life. Allow yourself to be guided by this invisible force---as you too
wield an invisible, magical influence on others.

::: group
### MASTER NUMBER 22 {.h3}

If you are born on the 22nd day of any month or have a 22 Life Purpose
Number and/or 22 Destiny Number, you have the qualities of not only root
number 4, but the Master Number 22.
:::

*Please read the meaning for number 4 (in [chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)), the "root number" for 22, as well*.

You are the Master Architect of Peace. You manifest achievement and
build your dreams into reality. You work hard and embody the power of
the Buddha Principle. I refer to 22 as the "Buddha" Number.

Master Number 22 intensifies the single-digit 4, representing work,
discipline, and honesty, which arrives in 22 through peace, intuition,
and cooperation. Thus your work encompasses spiritual self-study,
spiritual self-discipline, and spiritual honesty.

[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_73 .pagebreak}*"11 is supreme balance. Balance
between light and dark, masculine and feminine, the seen and unseen, the
known and unknown."*

As a 22, you are ...

\* Able to download higher divine wisdom into physical reality

\* Designed to build a project/business/idea from the ground up with
lasting results

\* A master at invoking peace and calm in daily life

In order to create peaceful solutions and manifest results with lasting
impact you need to be highly disciplined. At times you might feel like
you are inferior or don't have all the internal tools necessary. This
false belief will propel you to rely too much on outside sources or
people's opinions for approval. Understand that you are here as a Master
Number 22 to rely on your own abilities---which requires tremendous
inner strength. In order to be a master of manifestation you need
patience and strong vigilance to stay "on track."

The root number 4 that 22 reduces to gives you the gifts of planning,
dedication, and order so that you don't veer off into areas that are
irrelevant or even detrimental to your well-being. Without consistent
monitoring of your actions, though, done with full integrity and
honesty, you may get blinded by negative actions of people around you
that will lead to delusion and frustration. You will experience illusion
instead of inner illumination.

Master Numbers ask more of you---they also give you the tools to
accomplish more! So use your ability to *discern* truth from illusion.
Slay the dragons of fear and nebulous energy and replace them with the
magnificent light of truth.

Recognize your spiritual mastery---reflected in how you take
responsibility, in spiritual acceptance of how life shows up for you.
Practice this spiritual responsibility in your daily life, in your
relationships, and to accomplish your goals. Remember that the roles
other people play in your life are for multitude reasons---including
showing you what *not* to do! This is just as valid a lesson as the
person who inspires you as a positive role model. Accepting all
experiences and relationships as valid and useful in some way is the key
to helping you to the inertia to inner change you can encounter. Some
situations or individuals are so challenging that you will make major
shifts that result in life-changing readjustments and end up
[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_74 .pagebreak}wielding a positive impact on you.
Others will refine your sensitivity, propelling you to step into a new
role in uplifting society.

Thus if you refrain from inner growth by avoiding pain, you can miss out
on developing an incredibly profound understanding of peace---of what
creates peace and what keeps us from feeling at peace. The basics
surrounding the question and answer to what constitutes a life of peace
are there for you to unlock in your soul. You know that there is a
necessary process that we as human beings need to experience to create
that inner transformation from ego self to spiritual being, and that
this awakening comes as a result of self-awareness and self-acceptance.
You understand that when we become adults we must move into
self-realization, not rely on others to replace our parents, previous
guidance. In the same way it is important for you not to be caught up in
fads, the latest trends, and keeping up with your friends or neighbors
in an attempt for outside approval. Conformity is the shadow side of
22/4. Being independent and free to create your *own* order based on
your own truth and accepting the consequences of your actions as
feedback from the universe (not judgment) is vital to your peace and
well-being.

When you as a 22 are out of alignment you can succumb to indifference,
being aimless, reckless, apathetic, self-important, frustrated. You may
resent a lack of recognition, be envious of other's successes, and
exaggerate.

22/4 encompasses two of three numbers in the 2-4-8 Manifestation Triad,
and thus it carries great energy---accomplishments made real. Any area
you pursue will allow you to achieve a position of distinction because
you are not afraid of challenges and see them as necessary, even
welcome, stepping-stones to success. Master Numbers carry majesty and
greatness, and your expression of that power comes through your capacity
to manifest by planning great projects which you direct into existence
(rather than manage the intricacies---you must leave the trivial matters
to others). As the "Architect of Peace" Master Number you always want to
be at peace with your work and values so you can also enjoy the benefits
of the power bestowed on you. Guard against using your ambition to
manifest only for personal profit without caring *how* you arrive at
your goals.

::: group
### MASTER NUMBER 33 {.h3}

If you have a 33 Life Purpose Number and/or 33 Destiny Number, you have
the qualities of not only root number 6 but the Master Number 33. (There
is no 33 Day of Birth.)
:::

*Please read the meaning for number 6 (in [Chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)), the "root number" for 33, as well*.

[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_75 .pagebreak}You embody the Selfless Giver and the
Cosmic Guardian. Others look to you as an example. You have to discern
between martyrdom and compassionate service.

As a 33, you are ...

\* Highly sensitive and could be a powerful empath

\* Designed to be a teacher of compassion

\* Concerned for the welfare of the masses

When expressed at its highest vibrational alignment Master Number 33
symbolizes a person who embodies unconditional love. 33 carries all the
qualities of its root number, 6 (see [chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)), yet
is even more sensitive---feeling people's emotions as deeply as their
own. This is the kind of love that says to anyone who crosses your path,
"I accept you and love you no matter what you do or don't do. I will
always continue to love you regardless."

This unconditional love is extended to *you* as well. When the time
comes and you are at the point of transitioning to another dimension,
you will only remember whether you have been of service and loved to the
fullest extent possible. Nothing else will matter more than having led a
life of meaning and a life of love. Service and compassion create our
most profound experiences of love and joy. And 33/6 encompasses the
gamut of this underlying yearning for human beings to serve and love one
another.

In order to tune into the depths of heart-centered connection required
for this level of compassion there are times when you may experience
great doubt or distress, delusion, and disappointment in your life.
There are many responsibilities a 33/6 Master Number person takes on to
understand how to consistently activate the deep empathy of this
powerful vibration. It is said that Jesus died on the cross at age 33,
accepting all the whole human experience as his own, welcoming it all
with great humility, in service to humanity's awakening to love. This is
the ultimate expression of the 33, a love that gives birth to the
highest ideals through the death of the ego.

Note that our spinal column has 33 verterbrae, which act as the backbone
of our human body. Thus 33 takes on both the physical and emotional
expression of our human experience and embodies the chakras.

You may struggle with issues of intimacy and loyalty. Putting yourself
in a loved ones, shoes is integral to your emotional growth. This means
looking in the mirror and reflecting on how your words impact others,
how your actions impress everyone affected. You also can have a tendency
for being a perfectionist---expectations of perfection are contrary to
forgiveness---and you must learn to forgive others for not measuring up,
beginning first with forgiving yourself for being imperfect (a perfectly
natural state to be!).

*"As a 44 you have great magnetism, leadership abilities, powers of
persistence and self-control. These qualities allow you to reach the
highest echelons of power and wealth giving you a great capacity to
serve the world."*

[]{#ch04.xhtml#page_76 .pagebreak}You are here to uplift others through
unconditional loving service and joy, embodying the *empath*,
unpretentious and concerned only with the welfare of all---a teacher of
balance and harmony who leads others by example.

When you as a 33 are out of alignment you can succumb to criticism of
your self and others, pretentiousness, perfectionism, irresponsibility,
setting no clear boundaries, resisting reflection, worry, insensitivity,
anxiousness, rigidity in your beliefs, abuse of power, and using money
to control.

33/6 comprises two of three numbers in the 3-6-9 Creation Triad. You are
extraordinarily intuitive and can use your gifts in artistic and
creative endeavors. With your supreme appreciation of beauty, your sense
of aesthetics are exceptional, and you can master music, artistic line,
color, creative movement, and/or form to the highest degree.

::: group
### MASTER NUMBER 44 {.h3}

If you have a 44 Life Purpose Number and/or 44 Destiny Number, you have
the qualities of not only root number 8, but the Master Number 44.
(There is no 44 Day of Birth.)
:::

*Please read the meaning for number 8 (in [Chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)), the "root number" for 44, as well*.

You embody the Practical Visionary and Ingenious Director, here to
empower others by restoring order and dedication in their life.

As a 44, you are ...

\* A builder and manifestor of group consciousness

\* Designed to create new modalities of greater income and abundance

\* Trusting of the order of the universe

You are very resourceful and able to manifest valuable ideas in service
to others. Your creations are designed to help others rebuild their
lives. Your mental abilities are great, as is your strength of
conviction. 44 exudes []{#ch04.xhtml#page_77 .pagebreak}a powerful
personality, which matches their expansive goals. As a 44 you have great
magnetism, leadership abilities, and powers of persistence and
self-control. These qualities allow you to reach the highest echelons of
power and wealth giving you a great capacity to serve the world.

You are innately practical and strong. Your *big* ideas germinate from
an expansive imagination, which is able to conceive of intricate and
grand visions. This ingeniousness allows you to manage and bring
together many different aspects of power and personalities---thereby
finding seemingly magical solutions to problems others can't solve. You
do this by including them in the process, allowing their ideas to blend
with the ultimate solution, thereby acting as leader, manager, and
magician all at once and bringing complex projects to a harmonious
conclusion. This natural genius for directing also stems from your
innate ability to analyze and reason while applying compassion and
leadership with total confidence and control.

There is a serenity and integrity in you that instantly allows others to
feel secure and grounded. You are just, efficient, strong, and
ethical---having both tact and an incisive intellect that wields
enormous power, as all your energy is poured into making your ideals and
ideas *real*.

You do not shy away from work and are tirelessly engaged with your
responsibilities and projects, reflecting the self-discipline and
tenaciousness required for any great leader or organizer. Like all the
Master Number vibrations 44 also requires high ideals and complete
integrity in order to be of service. Your great desire is to improve
people's lives, their quality of life, and you use your influence,
power, and fortune to manifest all levels of improvements and elevation
in your community.

When you as a Master Number 44 are out of alignment you become
inconsiderate, overworked, and overstressed. You use money to control
others, expect others to manifest your good ideas, have no personal
discipline, are critical behind the scenes and envious of others'
success, resist responsibility, and are dominated by your own ambitions.

As a 44 you use discipline, humility, perseverance, and total dedication
to stay on your soul's chosen path. Often your satisfaction for having
completed a goal brings the greatest fulfillment---you know that you
have prepared for this moment, this life, and the satisfaction of
completion is superior to any other reward you may receive.

## []{#ch05.xhtml#page_82 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 5]{.f3} {#ch05.xhtml#ch05 .h2n}

## DOUBLE-DIGIT NUMBERS 10--98 {.h2t}

[N]{.dropcap}[OW WE WILL DISCOVER THE MEANINGS FOR DOUBLE-DIGIT NUMBERS
10 THROUGH 98.]{.f3}

::: group
### NUMBERS 10--19 {.h3b}

#### **NUMBER 10** {.h4}

*If you are born on the 10^th^ or 28^th^ day of any month or have a 10,
28, 37, or 46 Life Purpose Number or Destiny Number---or 55, 64, 73, 82,
91, 109 (etc.) Destiny Number---you internalize the qualities of number
10*.
:::

10 is the vibration of "Instant Manifestation." This means you can
manifest ideas, thoughts, goals, and emotions easily and often
instantly. The in 10 adds an element of divine protection. Your words
also have a great impact on others. The strong implementation gifts of
this frequency carry a big responsibility---since your thoughts and
feelings *will* manifest whether they are positive or negative. So be
sure to see your life from a "glass half full" perspective as often as
possible. 10 is made up of 1 and 0---the straight line and
curve/circle---the building blocks of sacred geometry and the universe,
giving you direct access to cosmic wisdom. (Our computer code is made up
of 1s and 0s and indicates the expansive impact that the number 10
wields.) Dedicate your life to creating love and light in all ways, and
you will manifest magical outcomes.

[]{#ch05.xhtml#page_83 .pagebreak}The shadow side of number 10 is
expressed when you are out of alignment. Watch for these clues: You are

awareness are being neglected.

within when seeking a solution. When you focus on expanding your
spiritual and intuitive education you reap success and experience
happiness.

The shadow side of number 12 is expressed when you are out of alignment.
Watch for these clues: You feel like you are a victim (or are
victimizing others), sacrificing your life to the point where you've
compromised your mission or values to be in servitude to another person
or cause, or you've given up your sovereignty, are a doormat, or are

As a 37 you are sensitive and private. You tend to have good friendships
throughout your life. This vibration can also emphasize love and
romance. Partnerships in general are good for you, in both business and
your personal life. You have a magnetic relationship with the
public---especially in the arts. You are wise in how you express your
emotions. You are also deeply spiritual. You have a desire to be
prominent and successful in your chosen field so you can express your
feelings and connect others to the divine in themselves.

The shadow side of number 37 is expressed when you are out of alignment.
Watch for these clues: You may be dishonest, deceitful, or manipulative.
You may not trust your intuition and may turn to others for answers.
Guard against emotional conflicts. You can get aggressive.

to learn the truth and will delve into your high intelligence to

The shadow side of number 70 is expressed when you are out of alignment.

instability. Your fluctuating moods may interrupt your intuitive flow.
You may worry too much. Guard against living pretentiously.

[]{#ch06.xhtml}

## []{#ch06.xhtml#page_120 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 6]{.f3} {#ch06.xhtml#ch06 .h2n}

## THE LETTERS IN YOUR NAME: A--Z {.h2t}

[J]{.dropcap}[UST LIKE EVERY NUMBER CARRIES A UNIQUE MESSAGE, EACH
LETTER IN THE ALPHABET RESONATES TO A SPECIFIC MEANING.]{.f3} The
alphabet conveys sacred symbolism. It is a wonderful tool to access
another part of a person's soul contract and give a deeper, spiritual
meaning of words. Use this chapter as a key to discover how language,
names, and words impact you all day long. You'll be amazed at the
profound impact the numerology of letters has on your life.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_121 .pagebreak}Your current name and birth name are
made up of several letters. Some are your initials, some are repeated,
and others appear only once. Letters that begin or end a name carry
extra weight, as does the middle letter of a name, if the name has an
odd number of letters. (Discover the meaning of a letter's placement and
repeated letters in [chapter 11](#ch11.xhtml#ch11).)

You'll notice that all twenty-six letters look different. This is your
first clue that they impact you differently! As you discover the meaning
behind each letter, you'll see certain words that begin with that letter
in capitals. Pay attention to words and names that activate each letter
for even more insights.

*Pay particular attention to the letters that correspond to your
initials, the first vowel in each of your separate names, any doubled
letter that is side by side (like aNNa has two Ns next to each other,
and JiLL two Ls side by side), or letters that are repeated. These will
carry extra emphasis in your life (more in [chapter
11](#ch11.xhtml#ch11))*.

Let's delve into the secret meaning of each letter of the alphabet!

[A]{.f1}/[1]{.f2}

::: group
#### **A = 1** {.h4}

A is balanced on two feet and shows initiative, Action, Activation, and
leadership. A likes to take charge!
:::

A has a line in the middle that balances the spiritual and physical,
higher and lower realms.

A reaches up to one point of arrival---A is Ambitious. An "A" in a
student report card in the U.S. means the highest or the best.

A must decide quickly or else it will be overly Analytical.

A is the first letter of the alphabet and represents the Air we
breathe---the first breath we take when we are born. Say "Ah" and it
sounds like a breath. Thus A also is highly engaged and creative,
confident and active. The word "A" means "one," as in "A" house, "A"
picture.

A needs to curb its enthusiasm if it turns negative. This can be
expressed as being overly ambitious, self-important, egotistical, bossy,
blunt, or jealous.

A is completely made up of straight lines, which gives focus, clarity,
direction, directness, and awareness.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} A [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} A
Activates Accomplishments and Acknowledges that Anything is possible!**

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_122 .pagebreak}[B]{.f1}/[2]{.f2}

::: group
#### **B = 2** {.h4}

B looks like two rooms that make up a home. These rooms are closed, so
it Births something sacred and secret.
:::

As the second letter of the alphabet, B represents the number 2---two
sides of the coin. Balance.

B has a middle line that divides the top and bottom "rooms." This
delineates the spiritual from the physical world, bringing an
understanding of both, yet also keeping them separate.

B governs the word Body, the physical "home" of our soul.

B is a visual representation of two Breasts---the mother's Bosom
designed to nurse the Baby. "Baby" has two Bs and requires Breast milk
to Build its Body.

To "Be" verbalizes the letter "B." Thus B symbolizes a body in balance
(feminine and masculine), with a brain, temporarily housing your
soul---and "to Be" is a Bringer of Beauty.

B needs a good home, is loving by nature, makes a caring companion, and
thrives in partnership. B dislikes jarring sounds and noise and is
deeply moved by music.

As an enclosed letter, B can hold secrets but needs to guard against
secrecy, moodiness, being lazy, codependent relationships,
oversensitivity, and needing to please.

B is made up of a straight line, representing the spine---energy and
inspiration coming down from Source---and two curves, cradling those
inspirations and ideas, holding them close to the chest (Breast) to
provide security so these seeds of inspiration Begin a new journey. B
can handle more than one activity at a time.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} B [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} B
Births and Breathes life into Being, Balancing the Best in everyone.**

[C]{.f1}/[3]{.f2}

::: group
#### **C = 3** {.h4}

C is a Circle that is open, Cradling Creativity and yearning to share it
through Communication.
:::

C sits on a "rocker" and is Changeable and flexible.

C sounds like "see" and is open to the right (the future)---thus C can
"see" into the future.

As the third letter of the alphabet, C represents the number 3 and the
Triad of Creation.

C must share with their voice, writing, music, art, singing. C has a
great facility and fluid sense of sound, words, color.

C is shaped like a half moon and shines the light of Clarity. Cs love to
[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_123 .pagebreak}shine and are the happiest when
uplifting others. Cs may hesitate to be visible, so the light must be
shined on them.

Turn C on its side and it looks like a smile---Cs love to bring joy and
smiles.

As a smiling mouth, C symbolizes your voice and music.

C is artistic and not interested in mundane jobs. Rather, C wants to
feel enjoyment in everything and is aligned with playfulness, creative
exploration, and "seeing" the beauty before it is made real---in the
abstract Concepts. C should leave managerial matters to others.

C wants to share their heart and emotions, allowing their feelings,
words, art, and music to flow unimpeded by barriers.

C can be critical of self and others and, may share too much, get
offtrack or gossip, Close up their gifts of expression and then become
intolerant of joy, dissipate their energy, and get too serious.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} C [IS WHEN ... C]{.f3}
Communicates Childlike joy and Connects us to Cosmic Creation through
the Creative process.**

[D]{.f1}/[4]{.f2}

::: group
#### **D = 4** {.h4}

D comes from the Greek "Delta" and means Door.
:::

D is a closed "room" and looks most like a square, symbol of number 4.

D is rooted in the physical experience---using Discipline to make the
Divine a visible Design. Thus D governs architecture---"Domus" in Latin
means "home," and D is Domestic by nature.

D loves the home and is Dependable, Dedicated to family and country,
strong, Defined, and a good Delegator, Decision maker, Defender, and
Director---with a great Desire to open the Door to the Divine.

D is connected to Doing and Discipline and holds Dominion over Death and
the Divine.

D can be too Disciplined and set limits on growth and expansion.

D likes to work and is reliable and good at completing projects but
needs to guard against Dedicating too much energy to work and no play.

D is Direct and honest---representing 4, D likes to get a "square" deal.

D is made up of a straight line, bringing the divine down, and is fully
enclosed by a C curve---creating a secure foundation for making the
Divine manifest.

D is great at seeing the Details but is not a "seer" like C or S. It
needs proof and visible evidence---see it to believe it. Ds are
methodical, patient, and best left to grow and work at their own pace.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} D [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} D
Develops a Divine Design to manifest its Destiny with Discipline.**
