[E]{.f1}/[5]{.f2}

::: group
#### **E = 5** {.h4}

E is open, like the number 5, and faces to the right---the future.
:::

E has a line in the middle, which balances the spiritual and physical
worlds.

E is Energy. (N is the fourteenth letter, and 14 reduces to 5. Both E
and N are representative of Energy and appear often in names.) E
Explores the five senses and is open to change

E is Extroverted, talkative, Expressive, Emotional, and likes to speak
and sing.

E loves to Experience all of life, including the mystical---the seen and
unseen.

When E is doubled in a word as "ee," it Expands the Expressive nature of
the word while also activating the five senses---such as in Feel, Deep,
See, Seer, Speech, Seeker, Teeth, Sleep, Freedom.

E is made up of only straight lines, giving clarity, focus, and
awareness.

E can be impatient, restless, and too changeable. E can overexplore and
get tied to the sensual pleasures. Too much self-indulgence can create
poor health.

E looks forward and is progressive, living to express and explore future
joys, rarely looking back. E likes the new (all letters in the word
"NEW" resonate to the root number 5)

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF E IS WHEN ...]{.f3} E is
Excited to Explore and Embrace all Experiences and trusts in Eternal
Expansion.**

[F]{.f1}/[6]{.f2}

::: group
#### **F = 6** {.h4}

F Faces Forward into the Future

F is a straight-line letter, Focused and Firm---depicting a direct line
from heaven down to Earth with two arms stretching forward in service to
others.
:::

F likes to take Fundamental responsibility for Family, Friends, and the
Future and is a parental vibration.

F is loyal, compassionate, artistic, forgiving, and caring and needs
harmony, beauty, and music in its environment.

F can be nurturing but may take the "mothering" to the point of
"smothering."

F needs to Feel calm and Free in order not to take on burdens; otherwise
confusion results. Guard against wanting control, meddling, and being
Fanatical or dismissive of others.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_126 .pagebreak}F Feels deeply and wants to Feel
appreciated. Their sense of Family extends to their community. F has
strong views. One of their greatest joys is to help or mentor others so
they can express their emotional confidence.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} F [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} F
expresses Loving Forgiveness and Feels Fulfilled when extending Freedom
to Family and Friends.**

[G]{.f1}/[7]{.f2}

::: group
#### **G = 7** {.h4}

G is a visual representation of a spiral and symbolizes a Galaxy.
:::

G sits on a rocker, so it can change easily.

G is expressive like the C and open to the left, but more internal and
quiet. G is not as verbally active as the C.

G symbolizes the Grace and Gratitude of a Great force and spiritual
Greatness, as in God/Goddess energy, a specialist or Guru, and Galactic
awareness and Genius.

As a spiral, G epitomizes constant Growth.

G, like P (both 7 root numbers), strives for perfection and wants to
find solutions to secrets to unveil the hidden meanings of things. The
ability to "Spiral" their thoughts and imagination allows Gs to
understand people's underlying motives, penetrating to the origins of
human behavior and actions.

G is wise, clairvoyant, and determined. G loves music and its ability to
heal. G is discerning and very selective. G is very sensitive to sounds
and needs peace and quiet. Being in contact with nature is important to
G's emotional equilibrium. G prefers mental exercise to physical
exercise.

Gs can be Guarded and loners and afraid of intimacy. G is not happy in
big crowds. G has to guard against aloofness and criticism.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} G [IS WHEN]{.f3} ... G
Guides others to experience Galactic expansion and God consciousness
through Gratitude and Goodness.**

[H]{.f1}/[8]{.f2}

::: group
#### **H = 8** {.h4}

H is a symbol of a window, looking above and looking below. Homes and
Hotels have windows---H is a window the soul. Thus as an H your vision
must encompass the wholeness of life and include all experiences.
:::

H is a made up of straight lines---two vertical lines representing
opposites and one Horizontal line representing the balance of light and
dark. H has great clarity and focus once it sees clearly. The view for H
can be happy or sad, light or dark, and embracing all visions as part of
the totality of our Human experience is critical for H.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_127 .pagebreak}In order to see clearly H has to look
above and below---the eighth letter also represents infinity. H Heals
with Honesty and by seeing beyond the Horizon.

H begins and ends the word Health. Good health is very important for H
to stay coordinated and balanced. Exercise imbues H with strength and
long life. H can work well under pressure.

H must be very discerning about how to spend precious time; there may be
a tendency to squander all Hard-earned progress through the openings at
the top and bottom of the letter and dissipate energy. H can be selfish,
intolerant, demanding, suspicious, and too cautious with money.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} H [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} H is
a window to the soul, bringing people Home to themselves by leading them
beyond the Horizon.**

[I]{.f1}/[9]{.f2}

::: group
#### **I = 9** {.h4}

I is a straight vertical line from the heavens to Earth, representing
Intelligence and Inspiration.
:::

Exhibiting only one straight line makes I very focused and singular.

"I" is the word for referring to yourself, as in "I am---the
Indvidual---and looks like the number 1. I feels Important!

I brings Insights and great Interest in both Intuitive and Intellectual
solutions.

I brings an Immunity from distraction (depending on other letters and
numbers in the person's overall soul code).

I Invokes Ideas, which are Infused with an Infinite sense of
possibility.

I represents Income, and the prefix "in" can add Intensification.

I is highly creative and impressionable and needs to feel deeply---music
and the arts are important tools, helping I feel encouraged to express
itself clearly and fluidly.

As the ninth letter, I has a knowing and wisdom to grasp the abstract
while being a humanitarian.

I needs to guard against Intolerance, moodiness, self-centeredness,
Ignorance, being too Intense, and arrogance

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} I [IS WHEN]{.f3} ... I

[J]{.f1}/[10 & 1]{.f2}

::: group
#### **J = 10 AND 1** {.h4}

J looks like a hook and faces to the left, using its excellent memory to
hook others into ideas and stories and knowledge.
:::

J takes inspiration from above and brings it down, and the curve allows
a repurposing of information for any occasion or goal.

J is unique and forges its own path as a leader; thus it does not want
to be told what to do.

J is daring and Jumps into situations. Since J sits on a rocker at the
bottom, it needs to use care and not rush into things.

As a 10/1, J is ambitious and highly creative in accomplishing goals.

J has excellent Judgment and makes a good Juror, due to its strong sense
of Justice.

J can be clever, a "Joker," witty, and humorous and is often deeply
spiritual or religious.

Jesus, John, Jeremiah, Joseph, Jakob, Judith---many great Bible figures
were master storytellers, with a "hook" to pull you into the narrative
and message.

J must guard against Jealousy, dishonesty, not completing what it
begins, an inflated sense of self, materialism, bluntness, and being
dictatorial.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} J [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} J
turns a Judgmental attitude into an understanding of divine
Justice---"as you sow, so shall you reap"---guiding others to a place of
Joy.**

[K]{.f1}/[11 & 2]{.f2}

::: group
#### **K = 11 AND 2** {.h4}

K is the eleventh letter of the alphabet, representing a Key to the
unknown.
:::

K is represented by a vertical line that reaches from heaven to Earth
and then branches out to the right---the future---with a sideways V,
symbolizing two open arms reaching upwards for spiritual insights and
downwards for grounding those insights into physical reality.

K at the bottom has both feet firmly planted.

K has a distinct middle point that separates two Vs pointing upwards and
downwards. Thus K reaches far and wide for inspiration, a picture of the
Master Intuitive of the 11.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_129 .pagebreak}K yearns to master how to leave lower
vibrational energy behind by reaching a point where upwards movement
towards higher vibrational energy is undeniable.

K represents the Kundalini energy that moves up and down the spine and
chakras and distributes vibration throughout the body and aura.

K needs a Kingdom in which to explore its powerful psychic intuitive
gifts and learn to shine its light. K has a Knowing that extends from
the Kinesthetic to unlocking Keys to universal truth and wisdom. The
need to Know is great with K!

K needs to connect with others. K also benefits from a good
partner---personal and/or professional.

K is highly sensitive. Since number 11 rules light and electrical
currents, K needs to keep nerves calm---which is best done by deep
breathing and daily exercise. K symbolizes motion through focused
Kinetic energy.

K can be easily hurt due to its extra sensitivity. Guard against
intolerance and dishonesty, deception, emotional reaction, and inner
tension. Nervousness can be healed through routine and order.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} K [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} K
Knows the Key to all Knowledge is contained within, accessed in an
instant by trusting in a feeling of "Knowing."**

[L]{.f1}/[12 & 3]{.f2}

::: group
#### **L = 12 AND 3** {.h4}

L is Love and Light. The two straight lines are a powerful 90° angle of
divine Love pouring from Source and shining the Light of knowledge and
wisdom.
:::

L sits firmly on a straight baseline and is balanced and grounded. Thus
even though L resonates to a root number 3, it is not as scattered and
changeable as the C, which sits on a curved line.

L yearns to be educated and is wise, Loving, and romantic---devoted to
Loved ones. L is sociable, friendly, Likes to Laugh and usually exhibits
a happy disposition.

L Likes turning on Lamps and curling up on the couch with a book---a
natural homebody.

L is very creative yet, due to being a purely straight-line Letter, is
not as flexible or spontaneous as the C.

L governs Law, so L has a good Legal sense and a natural understanding
of universal and human Laws. L easily understands people's underlying
motives and has good first impressions.

L has a voice that can carry and enjoys speaking, especially about Love
and what it has Learned---though L needs to refrain from gossip.

L has a strong Libido and Lust (though guard against Lechery) and a
beautiful sense of the Lyrical.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_130 .pagebreak}L may get overly emotional or
negative and find fault with everyone and everything. L also can be
indecisive---as the two lines of L reach in two directions and L can
understand the value for both choices or issues. L can feel victimized
or be the victimizer.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} L [IS WHEN]{.f3} ... L
follows the natural Laws of Life by uplifting with Love and Light**

[M]{.f1}/[13 & 4]{.f2}

::: group
#### **M = 13 AND 4** {.h4}

M, the thirteenth letter represents the Middle of the twenty-six-letter
alphabet.
:::

M is made of straight lines---an image standing on two feet with a
Middle V adding balance and receptivity and a willingness to listen to
Messages.

M has both Movement and stability, has an excellent Memory, and governs
the Mother principle, Water, and Mountains.

M is a good Manager and has a Mind that is organized and focused (since
13 reduces to 4) as well as streak of genius. M can deal with Major
situations and decisions.

M is pronounced with the lips completely closed---the only letter to do
so. Thus M represents silence, secrets, and the depths of the ocean that
are totally devoid of sound. In German is there is a saying, "Still
waters are deep," and M carries a profound depth and wisdom. M is
aligned with Meditation.

M likes to Mother and is a natural Mentor and giver of good advice. M
can have good business instincts and is aligned with Money and
Millionaire.

M is not afraid to work hard and tends to be organized and practical. M
pays great attention to details and can also go off on brilliant
tangents. M likes to use its hands, as a Musician or artist or through
Massage or a Mechanical vocation. M is patient and Moves at its own
speed.

M needs to guard against being boxed in or exhibiting coldness towards
others. M can be temperamental and moody, ignore unresolved emotional
issues, not show their love to others (even though they love deeply), be
careless, and have an inability to relax.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} M [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} M
Masters life by taking the Middle ground and Moving to the Music of
Mysticism and Magic.**

[N]{.f1}/[14 & 5]{.f2}

::: group
#### **N = 14 AND 5** {.h4}

N begins the second half of the alphabet and thus represents a pivot
point and new beginning.
:::

Like the number 5, which is open to the left and right, N is open to the
top and bottom---welcoming all experiences and wanting to explore.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_131 .pagebreak}N looks the same when turned 180° and
stands balanced at the bottom.

N is a completely straight-line letter and has Vs opening diagonally
towards heaven and Earth, exhibiting an openness to receive spiritual
and material insights. N embraces versatility, is not afraid of change,
likes to travel and be with people, and is Nimble on its feet.

Turning the N clockwise 90° to the right or counterclockwise to left
results in a Z, showing intuitive abilities that may be hidden. (Z is
made up of two interconnected 7s, representing powerful intuitive
gifts.)

N carries goodness and has healing abilities. Being connected to the
number 14 also imbues N with abilities in media-related endeavors and a
yearning to communicate a message.

N loves to move and is imaginative and ambitious. However, N needs to be
careful not to be busy for the sake of feeling alive. Unnecessary
distractions can take N offtrack, keeping N from finishing projects. N
also may be attracted to risky behavior or be stubborn and like to
argue.

N is like an antenna, picking up ideas from anywhere---Notice "aNteNNa"
has three Ns.

**The highest vibrational expression of N is when ... N is the eye of
the Needle, pulling through the thread of life to sew a New story, an
invitation to only experience the Now.**

[O]{.f1}/[15 & 6]{.f2}

::: group
#### **O = 15 AND 6** {.h4}

O is the image of a circle, representing the unifying cosmos and
everything in it, the eye and the zero. O never changes its shape, no
matter how you flip or turn it.
:::

O is a magical letter encompassing the wholeness of human love.

O loves the home, family, beauty, and abundance. As the fifteenth
letter, O symbolizes the "Spiritual Alchemist," uplifting others through
joy.

O also looks like a mouth that is Open. It represents expression,
warmth, sensuality, poise, and security. Love is physically expressed
through an Orgasm, and the feeling of bliss can be an Orgasmic
experience.

O is aligned with business, as it wants harmony and will negotiate to
make a deal.

O has access to all wisdom and can be an Oracle, so it is highly gifted
in many areas.

O can inspire others---negatively or positively. It is all or nothing.

A negative O is moody and Opinionated, may Ostracize others, goes
Overboard emotionally, likes Opposition, is materialistic, suspicious,
possessive, and jealous, and can get despondent.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_132 .pagebreak}Words or names with two side-by-side
Os look like a pair of eyes. Words like "look" and "book" require the
use of the our eyes.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} O [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} O is
Open to Our Original Source, embracing the Opulence of its gifts and
being the Oracle of love and joy.**

[P]{.f1}/[16 & 7]{.f2}

::: group
#### **P = 16 AND 7** {.h4}

P is the image of a Person with a big head at the top. P has a Purpose.

P is made up of a vertical straight line from heaven to Earth and a loop
at the top symbolizing a great mind filled with knowledge and wisdom.
:::

P carries Power. Many Prominent Professional Positions begin with P,
such as President, Pope, Prime Minister, Principal, Physician,
Pharmacist, Psychiatrist, Psychologist, Priest, Preacher, Peace Officer,
Police Person, Prophet, Philosopher, Pilot, Politician.

P is defined by Persevering to bring a Plan or Program to Perfection.

P needs to be completely Present to lead and succeed.

P is a Professional---focusing on Perfection by building a Pyramid and
getting to the Prime Position.

P feels its life is of Paramount importance. It is a highly Private
letter.

P is the sixteenth letter and highly Psychic. It symbolizes the
Pituitary gland, a master gland that controls many highly important
functions, including libido in men and ovulation in women. It regulates
serotonin, which impacts our emotional state and ignites Passion in
love.

P likes to analyze but may overthink as well. A negative P is unfocused,
aloof, and unable to express feelings and can be tactless, domineering,
possessive, intolerant, and deceptive. They carry a perfectionist streak
and are not always the easiest partners.

Like any 7 letter---other being G, P, and Y---P needs rest, Peace, and
quiet time, especially in nature. It enjoys uncovering mysteries and is
interested in the unseen.

P can be a Prophet---seeing and understanding concepts ahead of its
time.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} P [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} P is
a Prophet of Peace, Pointing to the Present as the Portal of Positive
empowerment.**

[Q]{.f1}/[17 & 8]{.f2}

::: group
#### **Q = 17 AND 8** {.h4}

Q is on a Quest.

Q represents a circle with a balancing line at the bottom right.
:::

Q is the seventeenth letter of immortality and needs the balancing line
to ground its tremendous power---keep the balance. Otherwise the Q can
focus too intensely on one Question or direction.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_133 .pagebreak}*"P can be a Prophet---seeing and
understanding concepts ahead of its time."*

Q is a leadership letter as represented by the Queen.

Q holds the same ability to see as the O but elevates the vision to
clairvoyance.

Q symbolizes Quenching a thirst for knowledge---used in order to
manifest.

Q will ask many Questions and always seek to find the highest Quality.

Q connects to Quantum physics and Quantum wisdom, imbuing it with a wide
range of talents. Thus Q has many interests.

Q also exhibits genius and can come off as peculiar.

Q is honest, dependable, charming, practical, mentally Quick, and
physically active. Q can work under pressure and wants to join with a
partner who is accomplished and likes to live a life of opulence.

In the negative, Q can be too strange, unstable mentally, directing its
power into negative areas, greedy, and prone to exaggeration. As a
partner Q may find it challenging to share.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} Q [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} Q is
on a Quest to reveal the unanswered Questions by tapping into the
Quantum nature of the divine.**

[R]{.f1}/[18 & 9]{.f2}

::: group
#### **R = 18 AND 9** {.h4}

R has a vertical line on the left and a Round loop at the top
(representing a big head full of ideas and wisdom) like the letter P,
but R also has a "leg" that Reaches out to the Right into the future and
creates forward momentum.
:::

R Represents the power and wisdom moving forward. R has a wonderful mind
and the ability to retain and Repurpose knowledge.

R is connected to Royalty and Regal leaders. Their thoughts are meant to
Rise above the norm to seek higher understanding and wisdom.

As the eighteenth letter, R has tremendous compassion and tolerance. 18
can sacrifice to bring about brotherhood and sisterhood.

R is also a great teacher---creative, passionate, selfless, loving, and
kind.

R also Resonates to the Root number 9 and is a letter of completion, so
it Represents an initiation into the mysteries, a celebration of life,
and a []{#ch06.xhtml#page_134 .pagebreak}passing of testing situations
to reach higher wisdom. Integrity and a strong search for truth define
this letter.

The Royal nature of the R is so powerful it can either destroy or create
something. R impacts the many, so when put to positive use R will give
without wanting anything in Return, Reflecting the Remarkable Respect,
Radiance, Reliability, and Refinement of this letter.

In the negative expression, R needs to guard against being too
emotional, jealousy, a bad temper, rudeness, a rough demeanor, being
over controlling, and being rebellious.

There is only one other number-9 letter in the alphabet---the letter I.
Like the I, R has an inner knowing, understands the abstract and the
concrete, is a humanitarian who genuinely cares for and likes people,
and is deeply intuitive, impressionable, and highly creative.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} R [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} R
Raises vibrations and honors the Richness and Radiance in everyone,
facilitating Rebirth after Rebirth.**

[S]{.f1}/[19 10 & 1]{.f2}

::: group
#### **S = 19 AND 10 AND 1** {.h4}

S opens to the right (future) on the top and left (past) at the bottom
like the number 5 and represents an openness to engage the Spiritual and
material.
:::

S Symbolizes the image of the Snake, which can wind itself Secretly and
Silently through any Situation (thus can also be deceptive) and gain
power and wisdom.

S also represents the Spinal cord and has great kundalini energy.

As the nineteenth letter, S represents both the 1 of new beginnings and
original ideas and the 9 of higher wisdom, culmination, and endings. S
is also a 10 of instant manifestation and root number 1. So S represents
a broad Spectrum of the human experience, winding its way through life
in a Spiral.

S is Strong, Sensitive, Sexual, Social, Supportive, and fascinated with
Success.

S has a Strong connection to the Sun, Stars, Solar, and Soul Subject
matters.

S is a Symbol of the Spiral Staircase to the Stars and thus indicates
genius, as it sees the Spiritual and physical realms and weaves them
into one.

S consists of two Cs, one facing left and the other right, being very
open to create and communicate---seeing both the past and future to
gauge how to reach SucceSS.

S can indicate changing directions in the middle of a project or plan,
always Searching for a better approach. Thus S needs to guard against
too []{#ch06.xhtml#page_135 .pagebreak}many changes so that it Sticks
with a plan, making Slight course corrections but not discarding the
whole vision. This tendency can make it harder for an S person to plan
ahead.

S represents the Self. It needs to watch being Self-centered and
Selfish. As a 1, S doesn't like to take orders and can be jealous,
blunt, and materialistic.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} S [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} S
uses Superior Sensitivity to Spiral towards Soul-centered Success.**

[T]{.f1}/[20 & 2]{.f2}

::: group
#### **T = 20 AND 2** {.h4}

T is balanced with the horizon at the top, representing heaven, and a
straight line in the middle leading down to Earth.
:::

The horizontal top line can represent either a burden or a tremendous
bounty of wisdom and knowledge being channeled into physical reality. It
is Source descending into matter.

T searches for spiritual and peaceful answers to questions. T weighs all
sides to reach a balanced conclusion.

T likes to Travel and gather Things. T is helpful, supportive, kind, and
organized in its Thinking.

T is a 20 and a 2, representing two sides, duality, and a high
sensitivity to Touch. T likes harmony and will strive to please.
Beautiful music moves them to the core and keeps Ts in balance
emotionally.

T can carry other people's issues on their strong spiritual
shoulders---represented by the horizontal line.

T likes to be on the Throne and is a Tolerant leader of peace.

T can also represent a "t" cross and must be careful not to sacrifice
for others so as not to Tap out energetically and fail to complete their
own mission. T can be impatient and have a Temper. T can get too caught
up in the details and might get easily frustrated when others make
mistakes.

Since Ts are so balanced, they might at times find it difficult to make
a decision.

T is a peace maker and peace keeper---a diplomat who does not like
conflict. T is Tactful but must also balance sharing the Truth even if
it is at the expense of Temporary disharmony---to Trust that peace will
be restored. Being Timid and suppressing anger at the expense of
speaking up in order to maintain a false sense of peace is not
recommended for a T, as the internal disharmony will need resolving to
keep the balance.

T does well when in a partnership, though it needs to maintain a private
sanctuary to maintain its sense of peace and equilibrium.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_136 .pagebreak}**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION
OF]{.f3} T [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} T is a Teacher of peace, Taking Time to
reveal the Truth and using its Talents to Transform Trauma through
Tenderness.**

[U]{.f1}/[21 & 3]{.f2}

::: group
#### **U = 21 AND 3** {.h4}

U represents a cup holding the wisdom of the Universe.

U is open to the spiritual insights from above and can hold that wisdom
securely.
:::

U has two sides or arms reaching up vertically to receive---yet they can
also act as opposites and represent the duality of nature. The prefix
"Un" Undoes the meaning of a word by introducing its opposite
nature---such as do/Undo, grateful/Ungrateful, or
conventional/Unconventional.

U has high sides holding the container, able to collect ideas and habits
and paradigms---creating impenetrable boundaries on either side and a
more conservative approach to life.

U resonates to 21, the vibration of truth that defines our twenty-first
century.

U will speak up and share the truth with strong projection and
magnetism. This is also because 21 reduces to 3, the vibration of the
voice, so U has a beautiful voice.

U carries itself regally and has the ability to be the executive.

U is very determined and can be quite musical.

U needs to guard against Using its intelligent tongue sarcastically or
to antagonize others, or Using words negatively to win or for aggressive
purposes. Us must always maintain control and not tip the bottom curve
of the U off-balance and cause it to Unravel.

Us are emotional and intense and can have a nervous energy.

Us are usually Unconventional and Unique and know how to handle
Upheaval.

Us love delving into the mysteries of the Universe and have an Uncanny
intellect.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} U [IS WHEN]{.f3} ... U
shares Universal laws by Unmasking Untruths and leading others into
their Unique capacity for Unconditional love.**

[V]{.f1}/[22 & 4]{.f2}

::: group
#### **V = 22 AND 4** {.h4}

V represents two arms completely open, stretching diagonally to the
spiritual realms.

V resonates to 22, the Master Number of Peace and the Master Builder.
:::

V likes to claim Victory and knows how to work to accomplish its
goals---either alone or with others. V has a good sense of business and
management.

V does not have a middle line separating the spiritual from the physical
realms, and the bottom of V is not balanced, so it is important for V to
[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_137 .pagebreak}study spiritual, metaphysical
modalities and practice some kind of meditation to stay balanced and
grounded.

I call 22 the "Buddha" number, making the V a peaceful, strong, and
determined leader. V is a completely straight-line letter and carries
great focus and clarity as well as awareness.

V can easily Visualize when the intention resonates with V's Soul
Blueprint and mission. With patience and a methodical approach, V can
accomplish anything.

V symbolizes a Vortex of energy, indicating a tremendous source of
manifestation power.

V likes Vitality mixed with Velocity and can live a life that is fast
paced---so V needs to get outdoors and exercise to stay balanced.

V needs to guard against being suspicious and selfish and feeling like a
Victim. A negative V may take a major risk and lose a lot in the
process.

**T[HE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} V [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} V
Volunteers to be Vulnerable, inspiring Virtue in others while teaching
the power of positive Visualization as a path to Victory.**

[W]{.f1}/[23 & 5]{.f2}

::: group
#### **W = 23 AND 5** {.h4}

W is Wide open to the top (spiritual) and bottom (physical).

W resonates to the number 23, symbolizing the Royal Star of the Lion,
giving this letter great strength and a mysterious power.
:::

W is an upside-down M. It represents a person stretching out two
arms---and also looks like a Mountain range as does M. Where M shows two
mountains and one valley, W shows one mountain and two valleys. Thus W
goes deeply into the unconscious aspects to gather the resources in
order to climb the mountain of Wisdom. W can stand apart as mystical and
Wondrous.

W is also a 5 and thus magnetically attracts crowds and people. W knows
how to persuade and is a good letter for business, since W has the Will
to accomplish goals and Will get them done.

W needs to work at a mission where there is adventure, change, and much
activity---W does not do well in monotonous situations. W likes to think
quickly and has a knack for coming up with new ideas and new inventions.

The word "NEW" represents all three letters in the alphabet that
resonate to the number 5!

W is sensual (five senses) and loves deeply. W is generous and shares
with those it loves.

W in the negative can be impatient, cut corners, and cause
instability (not going into the valleys before climbing the mountain).
The up-and-down nature of W means there is a fluctuation of energy, in
which hasty actions might be regretted at a later time. W needs to Watch
Worry.

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_138 .pagebreak}Wealth is attracted to W, while
health must be taken care of. Walking is Wonderful.

W represents the Woman and the Womb of Creation---and is a powerful
letter of Winning and Wisdom, representing an unbeatable strength that
allows W to transfer power to others. It is a very magnetic letter and
can accomplish rapid success.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} W [IS WHEN]{.f3} ... W
has the Will to flow with the Winds of change and Walk into each
adventure with a Winning attitude and a Willingness to Wonder.**

[X]{.f1}/[24 & 6]{.f2}

::: group
#### **X = 24 AND 6** {.h4}

X is open on all sides and can be vulnerable.

X either exhibits a spiritual, high vibration or can be materialistic
and attracted to lower energies.
:::

X can have a bipolar-like or double personality.

X may "cross out" or put an X on progress and growth.

Or X may rush too fast into a situation and unwittingly push the delete
button.

X represents the number 24 and single-digit 6 of human love. X can bring
love into a situation but needs to guard against confusing sex with
loving intimacy. Love and sex are both related to the 6 vibration, which
has an X in the word "six". So, due to the openness of the X, it can be
amazingly open and ecstatic or it can be led astray by its sexual
desires.

XXX denotes a high sexual content of lower vibrational force.

A positive X has a wonderful strong intention to uplift humankind
through love, wisdom, intellectual knowledge, and inner strength.

A negative X can attract challenging karma and lead a life of turmoil.
It will seek pleasure at all costs and turn to the dark side for power
and answers. The word "hex" can apply to the negative applications of
this letter.

All 6 letters have deep emotions and have a need to be appreciated. Thus
X has a deep underlying need to help others, is artistic, holds strong,
passionate views, and makes a wonderful teacher and counselor.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} X [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} X is
eXcited to serve humanity by opening all channels in service to love.**

[Y]{.f1}/[25 & 7]{.f2}

::: group
#### **Y = 25 AND 7** {.h4}

Y represents a fork in the road.

Y is the symbol of a decision and a person who is at a crossroads. A big
question is---which of two paths do I choose? Y introduces many choices
that need to be intuitively investigated.
:::

[]{#ch06.xhtml#page_139 .pagebreak}Y reaches to the heavens for answers.
As a 25 letter, Y is very psychic. So it must use its intuitive gifts to
listen and hear the answers it will inevitably seek to make choices.

Decisions will be the main theme in a Y person's life. They will
encompass going left or right, up or down, diving deeply or skimming the
surface, warm or cold, past or future.

Y must always choose the spiritual path.

As a letter made up only of straight lines, Y is very focused and clear.

Y resonates to the root number 7 and Yearns to know the mysteries of
life.

Y needs rest, quiet, nature, and peaceful surroundings.

Y's ability to listen will be especially important when quick decisions
need to be made---that is when Y must "trust their gut" for guidance.

A negative Y will feel moody, restless, intolerant of others,
overactive, and touchy. Y can be critical and quite self-centered, which
can lead to a fanatical approach to life.

Y looks like a dowsing rod and represents dowsing for gold, Yearning for
the golden nugget of truth.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} Y [IS WHEN ...]{.f3} Y
sees both the Yin and Yang in You and Yearns to feel Youthful with a
Young attitude---saying a big Yes to life.**

[Z]{.f1}/[26 & 8]{.f2}

::: group
#### **Z = 26 AND 8** {.h4}

Z is the final letter of the Western alphabet, representing the Zenith.

Z is made up of two 7s that are joined as one horizontal line connected
by two horizontal lines---the upper symbolizing heaven and the lower
Earth. Thus Z can channel powerful wisdom between planes of existence.
:::

Z looks like a lightning bolt, signifying an electrical aspect to the
sudden insights this letter attracts.

Z is an N turned on its side and resembles an antenna. It can scan the
skies for ideas and manifest them into physical reality.

Z represents numbers 26 and 8---the number of infinite strength,
overcoming obstacles, leadership. As an 8 letter, Z can attract
abundance.

Z works well under pressure and has a great desire for achievement and
recognition. There is no limit (8) to what they can and will do to
manifest a successful outcome.

In the negative, Z may exaggerate and has a hard time sharing, so can be
challenging as a partner. If it abuses its natural power resources, it
can easily loose what it has gained. Z must always lead with integrity
and honorable intentions.

**[THE HIGHEST VIBRATIONAL EXPRESSION OF]{.f3} Z [IS WHEN]{.f3} ... Z
strives for the Zenith, embodying the powerful Zero-point---and a life
of Zen.**

[]{#ch07.xhtml}

## []{#ch07.xhtml#page_140 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 7]{.f3} {#ch07.xhtml#ch07 .h2n}

## YOUR ASTROLOGY NUMBERS' CODE {.h2t}

[N]{.dropcap}[UMEROLOGY DESCRIBES THE ENERGY OF THE PLANET EARTH]{.f3}.
The numbers you see---the numbers in your Soul Blueprint, the numbers in
your name, and the numbers of your current cycles ([chapter
8](#ch08.xhtml#ch08))---are a description of your soul and your future
timelines. Just like you, the Earth and all beings emit vibrations that
are translatable as numbers.

The celestial bodies---our stars and planets---carry frequencies as
well. When we apply numerology to the position of the stars and planets
at the time of our birth and beyond, it expands our understanding of who
we are as divine beings that, after all, originated from the stars! Like
the numbers that appear in your Soul Blueprint, the numbers in your
astrology birth chart are specifically aligned to your cosmic code and
cosmic origins.

[]{#ch07.xhtml#page_141 .pagebreak}Astrology is the study of the
movements and positions of celestial bodies and their specific influence
and impact on us individually and collectively. It is usually seen as
separate from numerology. And yes, you can divine a person's soul code
with either science. However, you will uncover more layers and deeper
understanding when you utilize *both*.

Astro-numerology is a powerful modality---one that cannot be adequately
addressed in one chapter alone. However, this chapter will help you
discover how your birth planets and rising sign resonate to specific
degree numbers---and how those combinations impact you and your life.
Since we are discovering your soul Birth Code, we must also look at the
code in your stars at birth ...

To explore astro-numerology in greater depth, check out this free online
Master Class:
[TaniaGabrielle.com/numbers](http://TaniaGabrielle.com/numbers).

::: group
### ANATOMY OF AN ASTROLOGY BIRTH CHART {.h3}

Here is an example of Oprah Winfrey's astrology birth chart---look at
all the degree numbers! The bold numbers inside the circle (within the
twelve "pie slices") are the degree numbers of the Sun and planets at
the moment []{#ch07.xhtml#page_142 .pagebreak}of Oprah's birth. The bold
numbers in the wheel on the outer rim are the degree numbers that begin
each of Oprah's twelve houses (you must know your exact birth time and
birth place to get the twelve houses).
:::

As you can see, in astrology numbers are everywhere and thus form an
integral picture of your Soul Blueprint.

::: group
::: land100
![Image](./f0141-01.jpg){#f0141-01}
:::

**Oprah Winfrey**

[NATAL CHART]{.f3}

[JANUARY 29, 1954]{.f3}

[7:50:00 PM CST]{.f3}

[KOSCIUSKO, MISSISSIPPI]{.f3}

[TROPICAL PLACADIUS TRUE NODE]{.f3}
:::

::: group
### HOW TO READ THE NUMBERS IN YOUR ASTROLOGY CHART {.h3}

If you know your exact birth time and place, you can construct a chart
with the twelve houses, where the beginning of each house resonates to a
specific degree number.
:::

If you already have your astrology birth chart, go grab it now. I also
recommend you follow the instructions below, so you can access the PDF
that lists your important astrology degree numbers. If you do not have
your natal birth chart, follow these instructions:

::: group
#### **GO TO [ASTRO.COM](http://ASTRO.COM)** {.h4}

1\. Click on My Astro (top right).

2\. Click on Create a horoscope immediately, as a Guest User.
:::

3\. Enter your birth information. *If you don't know your birth time,
enter 12:00 p.m*. Then click Continue.

4\. Under Horoscope Chart Drawings, click on Chart Drawing, Ascendant.

5\. A page with your astrology birth chart will appear.

6\. Click on Additional Tables (PDF).

7\. This is the PDF we will use to access the degree numbers in your
astrology birth chart.

Now let's look at the numbers in your astrology birth chart. (Even if
you don't know your exact time, you'll still be able to see most of the
important degree numbers in your birth planets---but you will not see
the degree numbers for your twelve houses.)

In the Planet Positions table on the next page you will see several
columns. There is only *one* column that is important to us---the
"Longitude" column. I have highlighted the area in this column that
shows exactly where the degree numbers are that you need to pay
attention to. Notice how in each case, it is the first number on the
left that has a degree symbol (°). This is the *only* number you need to
pay attention to.

What this table is showing are the exact degrees of the planets at the
moment you were born.

::: group

+-------------+--------------------------------------------------------+

::: land100
[]{#ch07.xhtml#page_144
.pagebreak}![Image](./f0144-01.jpg){#f0144-01}
:::

[]{#ch07.xhtml#page_145 .pagebreak}*"When we apply numerology to the
position of the stars and planets at the time of our birth and beyond,
it expands our understanding of who we are as divine beings that, after
all, originated from the stars!"*

If you do not know your exact birth time and place, then pay attention
to the Sun and all other planets, with the exception of the Moon. The
Moon changes one degree every two hours, so an exact birth time is
absolutely necessary to know your Moon degree number.

In our example, this person has a Sun at 6°. If you know your astrology
symbols, you'll see the Aries icon next to the Sun. For the purpose of
this book we will not be discussing Sun signs, only the degree numbers,
to give you a snapshot of the numerology formula of your astrology Birth
Code.

Go down the longitude column of the planet table and highlight or write
out all the numbers you see---so, for the Sun, Moon (if you have your
exact birth time), Mercury, Venus, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Uranus,
Neptune, Pluto, the True Node (skip the Mean Node), and Chiron. This
will give you a set of twelve numbers (eleven if you don't count the
Moon).

Pay particular attention to the numbers of the Sun and personal
planets---Moon, Mercury, Venus, and Mars. But *all* the numbers
contribute another layer of information about you and your Soul
Blueprint.

Read a description of each of the numbers that appear in this column for
more insights into your soul code. Then apply each number to each
planet.

shown [here](#ch07.xhtml#page_143) are the essential meanings of the sun
and planets in the order they appear in the table.

Now combine the numbers with each planet. Go to [chapters
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03), [4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04), and [5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05)
to check the meaning for each degree number and align it with the
meaning of the planet.

In our example, the Sun resonates to 6°, and means that this person's
identity is known to be warm, giving, in service and someone who takes
on responsibilities. His or her creative life force resonates to love.

Venus is aligned to 20°, revealing that this person places a high value
on cooperation, harmony, and uniting opposites. Creatively, this person
is balanced and imaginative. Money is an equal give and take, and in
general an awakening will take place in love, money, and values.

Neptune vibrates to 4°, unveiling an imagination that is easily
manifested and a compassion that is honest and real, while psychic gifts
may []{#ch07.xhtml#page_146 .pagebreak}be used for specific areas of
life---there's a mystery or enigma around how this person loves and uses
his or her intuitive gifts.

*"When you follow the numbers, you'll be shown a deeper picture
revealing a magic and mystery that otherwise would have been missed
altogether."*

Now let's apply these same numbers to the houses. You'll see the
"Houses" table to the right of the "Planet" table. (If you do not know
your exact birth time, you will not be able to check these degree
numbers. The ones that show up in your PDF are not correct.)

What you'll notice is that the first six numbers repeat again. So just
write down the first six degree numbers. In our examples those are 28°,
12°, 0°, 6°, and 23°.

Look up the meaning of each degree number in [chapters
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03), [4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04), and [5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05).
Each of these planetary or house degree numbers adds a layer of
information to your Soul Blueprint.

If you notice that *any* of your Three Important Birth Numbers is also
reflected in your astrology birth chart, pay attention! This
cross-correlation is powerful and points out an intensification of that
number.

For any double-digit degree number, also check the corresponding
single-digit root number.

If you notice a particular emphasis on one (or more) of the three
numerology triads ([chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)), make a note of that.
It is another layer of distinction for you that points out a vibrational
alignment emphasizing the Mind, Manifestation, or Creation.

::: group
#### []{#ch07.xhtml#page_147 .pagebreak}**REPEATED DEGREE NUMBERS** {.h4a}

Pay particular attention to:

\* Numbers that appear more than once---an intensification.

*In our example, the number* ***20*** *appears twice*.

*The number* ***7*** *appears twice*.

\* Single-digits that appear more than once---an intensification.

*In our example the numbers there are two 20s and one 29, all of which
reduce to the root number* ***2***, *which is an intensification of the
number 2*.

*There is also one* ***24*** *and one* ***6***, *an intensification of
the number* ***6***.

*In addition to the two* ***7s*** *we see one* ***25***, *an
intensification of the number* ***7***.
:::

You are now beginning to make connections that are profound. Numbers
"speak" to each other, and your astrology birth chart is widening the
scope of who you are at soul level. This awareness will help you feel
more at ease and secure in yourself---even reveal hidden gifts you
didn't know you had!

So often we can cut ourselves short by placing limits on our perception
of our potential. Your potential is aligned to be expressed in a
*limitless* way! When you follow the numbers, you'll be shown a deeper
picture, revealing a magic and mystery that otherwise would have been
missed altogether. Acknowledging who you are at soul level, unveiling
the unique beauty that is you, is the greatest gift you can give---to
yourself and others.

Live your life *without restrictions*. Dispose of self-judgment or
others' opinions of who you are. Rather, turn to the glory that is
you---revealed in your true soul code. You are here on Earth temporarily
experiencing your soul in a new, infinitely wonderful way. Your soul
code is a reminder of your divinity. There is only one way to
God---through self-awareness.

## []{#ch08.xhtml#page_150 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 8]{.f3} {#ch08.xhtml#ch08 .h2n}

## PERSONAL YEAR, MONTH, AND DAY AND YOUR POWER CYCLES {.h2t}

[N]{.dropcap}[OW THAT YOU HAVE A GOOD PERSPECTIVE ON YOUR SOUL
BLUEPRINT, IT'S TIME TO MOVE INTO PRESENT TIME!]{.f3} Your birthday
started a continuous series of Personal Cycles that measure and describe
the active energies influencing your life---energies you can fully take
advantage of! By knowing the meaning and timing of your personal year,
month, and day vibrations, you have a powerful tool to take your life
from good to great.

In this chapter you'll discover how to calculate your cycles. You'll
also be able to see which of your Personal Years, Days, and Months are
Power Cycles. These will []{#ch08.xhtml#page_151 .pagebreak}intensify
the energy and attract experiences and opportunities that lead to even
greater growth and overall advancement.

::: group
### THE THREE IMPORTANT NUMBERS IN YOUR PERSONAL CYCLES {.h3}

Your current and future cycles comprise:
:::

1\. Your **Personal Year---**the vibration you are experiencing from one
birthday to the next birthday

2\. Your **Personal Month**---each calendar month carries a specific
personal vibration for you

3\. Your **Personal Day**---every day carries a specific personal
vibration for you

Your Personal Cycles are an invitation to consciously participate in
creating your reality in the most optimal way possible. Once you get
into the rhythm of your yearly, monthly, and daily cycles, you hold the
keys to the natural ebb and flow of your life in full alignment with
your Soul Blueprint.

::: group
### HOW TO CALCULATE YOUR PERSONAL YEARS {.h3}

Let's begin with your Personal Year vibration. Some numerologists start
*everyone's* Personal Year on January 1. However, I have found with
reading thousands of clients that the shift we feel on New Year's Day is
related to the *Universal Year* Number changing, not our individual
Personal Year. You see, there are Universal Cycles, which impact
everyone collectively, and then your Personal Cycles, which are totally
unique to you. When the Universal Year number shifts every January 1, we
all feel the change. But your Personal Year begins on your birthday, not
on January 1.
:::

Astrology, too, focuses on the shift on your birthday. It is always on
your birthday that your solar-return astrology chart is created (when
the Sun returns to the exact position that it occupied at the moment of
your birth), to give you the energetic forecast of your next year---not
on January 1.

When you consider that the day you were born began your life, gave you
your Life Purpose Number (which was your first Personal Year on Earth!),
then it makes total sense to begin your next vibrational cycle on your
birthday every year. Besides, that's the day your age changes too!

Your Personal Year begins in the month of your birthday. You change your
age and your Personal Year on your birthday, not on January 1. So for a
birthday in June, your Personal Year (and your age) begins in June of
one year and runs until May the following year.

[]{#ch08.xhtml#page_152 .pagebreak}This means that within one calendar
year, a person born during any month except January would experience
*two* different Personal Year numbers:

1\. One carried over from the previous calendar year *until* their
birthday.

2\. One *from* their birthday month onwards.

Your current Personal Year is derived by adding the digits of your day
of birth and month of birth to the current calendar year and reducing to
a single digit. Every new Personal Year begins the month that you were
born in. Your next Personal Year number will be one digit lower unless
you're currently in a 9 Personal Year, in which case your next Personal
Year will be 1.

Let's look at some examples.

+---------+---------+-------------+---------+-------------+---------+
| **[IF   |         | **[AND THE  | **[YOUR |             | **[AND  |
| YOU     |         | YEAR        | P       |             | IT      |
| WERE    |         | IS]{.f3}**  | ERSONAL |             | RUNS]   |
| BORN]   |         |             | YEAR    |             | {.f3}** |
| {.f3}** |         |             | IS]     |             |         |
|         |         |             | {.f3}** |             |         |
+=========+=========+=============+=========+=============+=========+
| may     | 23      | 2019        |         |             | may     |
|         |         |             |         |             | 2019    |
+---------+---------+-------------+---------+-------------+---------+
| 5 +     | 2 + 3   | 2 + 0 + 1 + | 22      | 2 + 2 =     | april   |
|         |         | 9 =         |         | **4**       | 2020    |
+---------+---------+-------------+---------+-------------+---------+

+---------+---------+-------------+---------+-------------+---------+
| **[IF   |         | **[AND THE  | **[YOUR |             | **[AND  |
| YOU     |         | YEAR        | P       |             | IT      |
| WERE    |         | IS]{.f3}**  | ERSONAL |             | RUNS]   |
| BORN]   |         |             | YEAR    |             | {.f3}** |
| {.f3}** |         |             | IS]     |             |         |
|         |         |             | {.f3}** |             |         |
+=========+=========+=============+=========+=============+=========+
| october | 15      | 2019        |         | 1 + 9 = 10  | october |
|         |         |             |         |             | 2019    |
+---------+---------+-------------+---------+-------------+---------+
| 1 + 0 + | 1 + 5   | 2 + 0 + 1 + | 19      | 1 + 0 =     | se      |
|         |         | 9 =         |         | **1**       | ptember |
|         |         |             |         |             | 2020    |
+---------+---------+-------------+---------+-------------+---------+

Your previous Personal Year number, which is active before your month of
birth in any given calendar year, is one digit lower than the current
year's (unless the current year's is a 1, in which case the previous
year's was a 9.)

Once you calculate your current yearly cycle, you can look back at
previous personal years and forward to coming personal year cycles to
gauge how these cycles have impacted you in the past and will impact you
moving forward.

::: group
### HOW TO CALCULATE YOUR PERSONAL MONTHS {.h3}

Your Personal Months change at the beginning of each month. To find your
Personal Month number, add the number of the month in question to your
single-digit Personal Year number.
:::

[]{#ch08.xhtml#page_153 .pagebreak}*"Once you get into the rhythm of
your yearly, monthly, and daily cycles, you hold the keys to the natural
ebb and flow of your life in full alignment with your Soul Blueprint."*

In the example above, the person born on May 23 calculated a 4 Personal
Year in 2019. That means that her months are:

+---------------------------+-------------+------+--------------------+
| **[PERSONAL YEAR          | **[MO       | **[  |                    |

|                           |             | ONAL |                    |
|                           |             | M    |                    |
|                           |             | ONTH |                    |
|                           |             | NU   |                    |

Note: September is the ninth month. Thus in September every year, your
Personal Month number is the same as your Personal Year number. This is
because adding 9 to any number and reducing the total sum to a single
digit results in the same number that you originally added to 9.

[]{#ch08.xhtml#page_154 .pagebreak}In the other example shown
[here](#ch08.xhtml#page_152), the person born on October 15 calculated a
1 Personal Year in 2019, beginning a brand-new nine-year cycle. That
means that her months are:

::: group
### HOW TO CALCULATE YOUR PERSONAL DAYS {.h3}

Take the Personal Month Number in question and add it to the day in
question.
:::

Personal Month \_\_ + Day = \_\_ Personal Day

For example, to find the Personal Day on **May 6, 2019,** for the person
born on May 23:

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+
| **[PERSONAL MONTH      | **[DAY OF THE      | **[PERSONAL DAY        |
| NUMBER]{.f3}**         | MONTH]{.f3}**      | NUMBER]{.f3}**         |
+========================+====================+========================+
| 9 +                    | 6                  | = 15 (1 + 5) = 6       |
+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+

Read the descriptions for 4, the Personal Year Number; 9, the Personal
Month Number; and 6, the Personal Day Number, in the Personal Cycles in
[chapter 9](#ch09.xhtml#ch09).

[]{#ch08.xhtml#page_155 .pagebreak}To find this person's Personal Day
for **September 29, 2019:**

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+
| **[PERSONAL MONTH      | **[DAY OF THE      | **[PERSONAL DAY        |
| NUMBER]{.f3}**         | MONTH]{.f3}**      | NUMBER]{.f3}**         |
+========================+====================+========================+
| 4 +                    | 29 (2 + 9)         | = 15 (1 + 5) = **6**   |
+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+

Read the descriptions for 4 and 6 Personal Cycles in [chapter
9](#ch09.xhtml#ch09).

To find this person's Personal Day for **February 14, 2020**:

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+
| **[PERSONAL MONTH      | **[DAY OF THE      | **[PERSONAL DAY        |
| NUMBER]{.f3}**         | MONTH]{.f3}**      | NUMBER]{.f3}**         |
+========================+====================+========================+
| 6 +                    | 14 (1 + 4)         | = 11 (1 + 1) = **2**   |
+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+

Read the descriptions for 4, 6, and 2 Personal Cycles in [chapter
9](#ch09.xhtml#ch09).

As previously calculated, the person born on October 15 will enter a
**1** Personal Year in October 2019, beginning a brand new 9-year cycle!

To find the Personal Month for **October 7, 2019:**

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+
| **[PERSONAL MONTH      | **[DAY OF THE      | **[PERSONAL DAY        |

+========================+====================+========================+

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+

Read the descriptions for 1, 2, and 9 Personal Cycles in [chapter
9](#ch09.xhtml#ch09).

To find the Personal Month for **August 26, 2020**:

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+

+------------------------+--------------------+------------------------+

Read the descriptions for 1, 9, and 8 Personal Cycles in [chapter

Read the descriptions for 1 and 4 Personal Cycles in [chapter
9](#ch09.xhtml#ch09).

::: group
### []{#ch08.xhtml#page_156 .pagebreak}YOUR POWER CYCLES {.h3}

There are certain Personal Years, Months, and Days that activate one of
your Three Important Birth Numbers. When this happens you will feel an
intensification of energy. You'll experience profound growth and more
opportunities. These are your Power Cycles, and their enhancement
happens *any time a current Personal Cycle number aligns with one of the
numbers in your Soul Blueprint*.
:::

For example, if your Three Important Birth Numbers are 3, 7, and 4 (Day
of Birth, Life Purpose, and Destiny), you want to note any Personal
Year, Month, or Day that *also* resonates to 3, 7, or 4. So, if you are
experiencing a 4 Personal Year, Month, or Day, you are activating your 4
Destiny Number. Make a note of these upcoming Power Cycles! Knowing
about them will help you navigate your life with confidence and ease.
You'll be able to leverage the profound vibrational alignment that takes
place each and every time.

Keep in mind, you have several Power Cycle Personal Days each and every
month---no matter whether you are in a Power Cycle Personal Month and
Year or not! So you are never without this surge of energy.

You have some Days and Months when two of your Three Important Birth
Numbers are activated. This happens when a Personal Year and a Personal
Day both align with one of your Three Important Birth Numbers at the
same time. Or it can be a Personal Month and Personal Day.

Once in a while, if your Personal Year and Personal Month both activate
one of your Three Important Birth Numbers, you will have *triple
intensification* Power Cycle days! That is when the Personal Year,
Personal Month, and Personal Day *all* resonate to one of the Three
Important Numbers in your Birth Blueprint.

Take advantage of any Power Cycle activation. It is a green light from
the universe to your soul, letting you know---all systems go! Whatever
you experience during these Year, Month, or Day Power Cycles, it is
designed to up your game, lift you higher, and put you in greater touch
with the Light of God---your Spiritual Source.

Now let's discover the meaning of your Personal
Cycles\![]{#ch08.xhtml#page_157 .pagebreak}

[]{#ch09.xhtml}

## []{#ch09.xhtml#page_158 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 9]{.f3} {#ch09.xhtml#ch09 .h2n}

## THE MEANING OF YOUR PERSONAL CYCLES {.h2t}

[N]{.dropcap}[OW THAT YOU KNOW HOW TO CALCULATE YOUR PERSONAL
YEARS,]{.f3} [MONTHS, AND DAYS]{.f3} as well as decipher when your Power
Cycles are, it's time to give all the numbers meaning! You will discover
how each number vibration, from 1 through 9, is activated. Use the
interpretation for each number for all your cycles---year, month, and
day.

::: group
### []{#ch09.xhtml#page_159 .pagebreak}9-YEAR CYCLES {.h3}

Every nine years you begin a new 9-year cycle, from Personal Year 1
through 9. Any time your 9-year cycle comes to an end (you are in a 9
Personal Year) or begins again (you are in a 1 Personal Year), you will
feel a major shift in your life. You are releasing old paradigms and
ways of being, people, and beliefs to make room for a rebirth.
:::

This "shift" also happens to a lesser degree when you transition from a
9 Personal Month to a 1 Personal Month, and even from a 9 Personal Day
to a 1 Personal Day.

As a reminder, your current and future cycles comprise:

1\. Your **Personal Year**---the vibration you are experiencing from one
birthday to the next birthday

2\. Your **Personal Month**---each calendar month carries a specific
personal vibration for you

3\. Your **Personal Day**---every day carries a specific personal
vibration for you

Whenever a Personal Day, Month, or Year is the same as one ofyour Three
Important Birth Numbers, the impact will intensify.

::: group
### 1 PERSONAL YEAR/MONTH/DAY {.h3}

**Keywords:** New Beginnings, Action, Change, New Goals

Learning new modalities, fresh energy, completely letting go of beliefs,
things, people, and investments that are not supporting you, boldness,
courage, opportunity, rebirth---you are at a crossroads.
:::

Shadow side: guard against stubborn resistance to change, not focusing
on and planning your future.

\* You are experiencing a new beginning in some or all areas of your
life.

\* Seed new original ideas.

\* 1 cycles initiate, so put your ideas and ambitions into action.

\* You are rebranding your life and thinking about yourself and your
plans in refreshing new ways.

\* This is an intense period of awakening.

\* Your confidence is growing and making room for you to open up and
explore bold new directions.

\* Pay meticulous attention to new opportunities.

\* Sudden change shifts you to the core.

\* Fearlessly embrace and proclaim what makes you unique.

\* Create and invent.

::: land100
[]{#ch09.xhtml#page_160
.pagebreak}![Image](./f0160-01.jpg){#f0160-01}
:::

::: group
### []{#ch09.xhtml#page_161 .pagebreak}2 PERSONAL YEAR/MONTH/DAY {.h3}

**Keywords:** Cooperation, New Partnerships (personal and business),
Balance, Patience, Peace

Relationships, diplomacy, slow down, meticulous attention to details,
correct timing, trust that your goals are being taken care of,
listening, intuition, germination of seeds planted during last cycle.
:::

Shadow side: guard against impatience, division, feeling insecure about
making decisions.

\* Your 2 cycle is bringing you into equilibrium---you must balance
light and dark and embrace all of life.

\* Listen to your inner voice for spiritual insights.

\* You are deeply sensitive to everyone and everything.

\* Trust in the correct timing of events, and be patient.

\* Allow your heart to decide for you.

\* Seek relationships that create balance in your life.

\* Communicate your message with compassion and sensitivity.

\* Take time for serenity---honor your sweetness and beauty.

\* Embrace your inner psychic!

::: group
### 3 PERSONAL YEAR/MONTH/DAY {.h3}

**Keywords:** Creative Self-Expression, Being Social, Sharing Feelings,
Pleasure, Connections
:::

Circle of friends, express your inner voice, relax about having fun,
enjoyment of the arts, find what makes you happy, travel, action,
optimism, unexpected events (3 sits on a rocker).

Shadow side: guard against emotional drama, distractions, moodiness.

\* Your creativity is being channeled through many sources and expresses

\* Take great joy in finding what fulfills you to the core of your
being.

\* Your imagination has no bounds!

\* Staying positive attracts many opportunities.

\* Opportunities are seized with bold action.

brothers.

\* What moves you to tears? Follow that thread ...

::: group
