[]{#ch10.xhtml}

## []{#ch10.xhtml#page_168 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 10]{.f3} {#ch10.xhtml#ch10 .h2n}

## ADDRESS NUMBERS {.h2t}

[A]{.dropcap}[S YOU CONTINUE READING THIS BOOK ON THE SECRET MEANING OF
NUMBERS]{.f3} you'll start noticing the numbers in your daily life more
and more. For example, each of the pages in this book is numbered! In
[chapters 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03), [4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04), and
[5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05) you discovered the detailed meanings of all
single-digit and double-digit numbers. These three chapters are your
ultimate guide to the numbers in your daily life, including messages you
receive when you randomly open a page of any book.

[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_169 .pagebreak}Other more permanent prominent
numbers in your life are your address number, your phone number(s), the
number of children you have, even numbers you are drawn to. Look at each
number and read about it in [chapters 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03) to
[5](#ch05.xhtml#ch05); it will tell you something about yourself in each
particular context.

There is so much more to understand about your life that is revealed day
to day in letters and numbers.

::: group
### DAILY SYMBOLS IN YOUR LIFE---YOUR DIRECT LINE TO SOURCE {.h3}

Let's say you ask a question, or there has been something on your mind
and you reach for a favorite book and open to shown
[here](#ch04.xhtml#page_78). That page number carries a message for you.
Even if you did not have a question in mind, you are receiving a message
from Spirit. The universe *loves* using numbers to communicate with your
soul, because numbers are so easy to find everywhere and, as you can
see---easy to understand. So, paying attention to the number messages
that come up for you several times a day allows you to connect with
Source all the time.
:::

Or let's say you look at the time and notice it's 1:09 p.m., for
example. Look at the overall message 1 + 0 + 9 = 10, which reduces to 1.
So this is a fresh, new-beginnings message for you. One that favors
honoring your originality and the energy surge that accompanies
furthering your idea, goal, or approach. Then you check *each* of the
individual numbers that make up the whole, in this case numbers 1, 0,
and 9, for an additional layer of meaning.

::: group
### ADDRESS VIBRATIONS {.h3}

Just as every person emits a special code, each address carries a
specific vibration. There are three important items you need to know
about your address number:
:::

\* Is it an overall fortunate vibration?

\* If yes, does the vibration resonate with one of your Three Important
Birth Numbers?

\* If not, what remedy can you use to introduce a secondary positive
influence?

Address numbers have different effects on your life, so it is important
to understand how your address affects you, whether it is your personal
address or business address. This knowledge alone will have a major
effect on your daily life. You'll be able to know which addresses keep
you in the flow, with minimal challenging interference and
distractions---and just as importantly, which do not.

::: group
#### []{#ch10.xhtml#page_170 .pagebreak}**HOW TO CALCULATE ANY ADDRESS** {.h4}

In any address that impacts your life, only the number is important to
you. You do not need to calculate the street name. The only instance
where a letter will be considered as part of the calculation process is
when a letter appears in your actual address number, such as 555 Cedar
St., **#9H.**
:::

Let's look at variations of addresses you may encounter in your life:
First write down the number of your address.

1\. For a simple street address, without an apartment number, simply
write down the number.

If you live at 4816 Main St., write down **4816**.

Add all the numbers until you can bring the total down to a single-digit
"root" number:

**4816** = 4 + 8 + 1 + 6 = **19**

**19** = 1 + 9 = **10**

**10** = 1 + 0 = **1**

The address number for this property is 1.

2\. If you live in an apartment or condo, you must calculate both the
street number of your whole building *and* the unit number of your condo
separately. Your building number is of lesser importance than the unit
number---since only the unit number is unique to you. The unit number is
your personal address vibration.

For 4816 Main St., \#**25:**

**25** = 2 + 5 = **7**

The address number for this unit is 7. We already know that 4816 Main
St. adds up to a "root" number of 1. But **7**, the unit number, *has
the greatest influence on the inhabitant(s)*. Number **1** for 4816 Main
St. has a secondary impact.

3\. For addresses with letters, you must add the numeric value for the
letter *with* and *without the equivalent number value of the letter*.

An address of 32 Apple Dr. #8B would be added:

8 + B = 8 + 2 = 10

10 = 1 + 0 = 1

Without the Letter B this address *also* vibrates to number 8. So this
condo unit activates both the numbers 1 and 8. It is important to
calculate *both* versions---with and without the letter---whenever a
[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_171 .pagebreak}number and letter are present. *Thus,
look at the number as a standalone vibration and the total of the number
and letter*.

::: land100
![Image](./f0171-01.jpg){#f0171-01}
:::

::: group
#### **HOW YOUR ADDRESS ALIGNS WITH YOUR BIRTH CODE** {.h4}

Look at all the single-digits that make up your Three Important Birth
Numbers ([chapters 1](#ch01.xhtml#ch01) and [2](#ch02.xhtml#ch02)).
:::

Figure out which of the three triads they resonate to ([chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)).

If *one* of your Three Important Birth Numbers is activated by your
single-digit address number, your address number will resonate with you.
However, you still need to check whether your address activates a
"challenging" vibration. Even if it resonates with you, it may attract
challenges if it is not connected to abundance.

::: group
### MEANING OF YOUR ADDRESS {.h3}

*Remember, as long as one of your Three Important Birth Numbers
resonates with the single-digit of your address, you are compatible with
the address*.
:::

::: group
#### **1 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* Optimism, achievement, and manifesting new ideas.

\* If you're looking for a fresh start, a number 1 address gives you the
confidence and strength.
:::

\* Good for those who are self-employed or want to live alone and/or
work alone.

\* Favors activation and determination, not a laid-back lifestyle.

\* 1 addresses do not like any clutter. 1 thrives on clarity and
cleanliness.

\* A 1 address is good for people who are naturally independent---though
favors partners who are interdependent and respect each others personal
freedom and boundaries.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **5**, and **7**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **8**, and **9**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **2**, **4**, and **6**.

::: group
#### []{#ch10.xhtml#page_172 .pagebreak}**2 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **2 addresses** favor partnerships and love (please see exceptions in
next section).

\* 2 addresses foster harmony and balance.
:::

\* 2 is more laid-back and not as connected to manifesting financial
abundance than other numbers.

\* Putting career first is not as easy---relating with compassion and
consideration are the major themes.

\* You can feel more emotional and codependent in a 2 address.

\* Favors meditation and diplomacy in a compassionate, nurturing
environment.

\* Getting caught up in other people's lives and feelings is something
to be aware of.

\* 2 addresses are wonderful for sharing, settling down with a family,
and having roommates.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **2**, **4**, and **8**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **6**, and **9**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **5**, and **7**.

*\*\* Avoid addresses that initially add up to 11, 29, 38, or 47.
Addresses that add up to 2 or 20 are good*.

::: group
#### **3 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **3 addresses** are perfect for the creative, free-spirited person.

\* 3 homes attract movement, activity, emotional expression, and change.
:::

\* 3 can scatter energy and does not plan for the future, so this
address is less likely to attract financial abundance.

\* 3 homes foster communication and social engagement.

\* 3 addresses attract optimism and fun and are great for parties and
social gatherings.

\* 3 addresses activate your imagination.

\* In a 3 address, being clean and tidy is not a priority.

\* 3 invites sharing and emotional self-expression---not practical,
serious endeavors.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **6**, and **9**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **2**, and **5**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **4**, **7**, and **8**.

*\*\* Avoid addresses that initially add up to ***12***, ***39***, or
***48***. Addresses that add up to ***3***, ***21***, or ***30*** are
good*.

[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_173 .pagebreak}*"The universe loves using numbers to
communicate with your soul, because numbers are so easy to find
everywhere, and, as you can see---easy to understand."*

::: group
#### **4 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **4 addresses** bring a sense of order, stability, and long-term
residents.

\* 4 addresses foster slow and steady progress and protection.
:::

\* 4 is the number of diligent work, so this space won't be as relaxing
as others.

\* 4 addresses do not support freedom or a flowing sense of ease.

\* 4 addresses are more serious than fun.

\* A 4 address is not very aligned with generating financial abundance.

\* In a 4 house you'll need to be patient and know that manifestation
will take effort.

\* A 4 address is good for study, work, security, and stability.
Structure, order, and discipline influence this address.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **2**, **6**, and **7**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **4**, **5**, **8**,
and **9**.

*\*\* 4 addresses in general are best avoided, since they make it more
challenging to attract abundance*.

[NOTE:]{.f3} *Any person with a ***4*** or ***8*** Day of Birth or
***4*** or ***8*** Life Purpose Number should not live in a 4 address.
(This rule does not apply if your Destiny Number reduces to ***4*** or
***8***.)*

::: group
#### **5 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **5 addresses** are very active energetically, inviting exploration
and risk, not peace and quiet.

\* A 5 home favors communication, media, and connection with people.

\* Traveling, adventure, pleasure, and freedom are magnified in a 5
address.
:::

[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_174 .pagebreak}\* Any excessive behavior or
addiction is amplified in a 5 home.

\* 5 addresses favor variety and don't tend to be permanent residences.

\* Amplifies fearlessness and progressive ideas---living life to the
fullest.

\* Your curiosity is piqued, and new exciting experiences are welcomed.

\* People come and go in 5 addresses---they have a sense of
unpredictability.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **5**, and **7**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **3** and **9**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **2**, **4**, **6**, and
**8**.

::: group
#### **6 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **6 addresses** radiate with warmth, cheer, beauty, and compassion.

\* A 6 address is a wonderful family home and favors love and abundance.
:::

\* Your creativity and inspiration are magnified at a 6 address.

\* People of all ages can reside here and feel nurtured and cared for.

\* 6 addresses invoke strong responsibilities, so keep the balance with
self-care in order not to get drained energetically.

\* A 6 address favors running a home business and any endeavors related
to providing a service.

\* The focus is on acceptance, trust, and building strong family bonds.

\* A 6 address can be a beautiful sanctuary for the heart and soul.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **6**, and **9**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **2**, **4**, and **8**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **5**, and **7**.

::: group
#### **7 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **7 addresses** are peaceful, meditative spiritual and favor personal
development.

\* Favors learning, studying philosophy, esoteric subjects and all
education.

\* This is a very private, quiet address---a refuge. Noise must be kept
to a minimum to not disturb the peace.
:::

\* At times, sudden events bring deep transformation.

\* 7 addresses are more suited for the single person, not families or
couples.

\* Solitude, contemplation, intellectual pursuits, intense devotion, and
a connection to nature are favored.

[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_175 .pagebreak}\* This address is not recommended
for manifesting financial abundance.

\* Escape everyday stresses in this retreat home---favors writers,
healers, spiritual seekers.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **5**, and **7**.

**Good** for Birth Code Number **4**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **2**, **3**, **6**, **8**,
and **9**.

*\*\* Avoid addresses that initially add up to 16, 25, 34, or 43.
Addresses that add up to 7 are good, if you don't mind that this
property won't be a major abundance attractor*.

::: group
#### **8 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **8 addresses** favor leadership, power, success, and a strong focus
on manifesting money.

\* Favors running a home business, but not necessarily family life.

\* Helps you to be recognized for your mission, expertise, career.
:::

\* 8 addresses must exude elegance with quality furniture and luxury
items.

\* 8 addresses do not encourage social events or casual visitors.

\* Favors manifesting financial abundance, organization, endurance,
overcoming obstacles, and management.

\* This address is about prestige and power.

\* Keep a balance on spiritual and physical fulfillment.

**Great** for Birth Code Number **2**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **5**, and **6**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **4**, **7**, **8**,
and **9**.

\*\* [NOTE:]{.f3} *Any person with a ***4*** or ***8*** *Day of Birth*
or ***4*** or ***8*** *Life Purpose Number* should not live in a 4
address. (This rule does not apply if your Destiny Number reduces to
***4*** or ***8***.)*

\*\* *Avoid addresses that initially add up to 26, 35, or 44. Addresses
that add up to ***8*** or ***17*** are good*.

::: group
#### **9 ADDRESSES/UNIT NUMBERS:** {.h4}

\* **9 addresses** favor spiritual leadership, empathy, unconditional
love, teaching, and family.

\* Favors settling down long term, completion of goals, and love.

\* Supports interaction with extended family and friends.
:::

\* 9 addresses exude warmth, tolerance, compassion, and acceptance of
all.

\* 9 addresses favor creativity and inspirational pursuits.

\* In a 9 space you want to make the world a better place and give
something back.

\* Supports abundance generation and spiritual growth.

\* Living here will put the focus on letting go, seeking higher wisdom,
forgiveness, and giving.

**Great** for Birth Code Numbers **3**, **6**, and **9**.

**Good** for Birth Code Numbers **1**, **2**, and **5**.

**Not recommended** for Birth Code Numbers **4**, **7**, and **8**.

*\*\* Avoid addresses that initially add up to 18. Addresses that add up
to ***9***, ***27***, or ***36*** are good*.

*For more detailed information on address numbers, check out the
Abundance Accelerator online training program at
[taniagabrielle.com/abundance](http://taniagabrielle.com/abundance)*.

[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_176 .pagebreak}*"Address numbers have different
effects on your life, so it is important to understand how your address
affects you, whether it is your personal address or business address."*

::: group
### REMEDIES FOR CHALLENGING ADDRESS NUMBERS (AND HOW TO ALIGN THESE TO YOUR SOUL BIRTH CODE) {.h3}

If an address number is either challenging or not in harmony with one of
your birth numbers, there is an easy remedy to diminish a challenging
address and infuse it with a secondary positive vibration.
:::

Place a number inside the front door---anywhere on the door, but it must
be *inside the main door* of the residence or office---thus facing into
the home.

This number is added to the single-digit address number.

Make sure the new digit double-digit and single-digit address number
resonates with one of the Three Important Numbers in your Birth Code.

Make sure the number is positive and is not listed in the "Avoid"
section.

For example, if you live in a 12 home (which is in the "Avoid" section
[]{#ch10.xhtml#page_177 .pagebreak}under 3 addresses), you want to add
the root number 3 (12 = 1 + 2 = 3) to a single-digit for which the new
sum reduces to a number that supports you.

Let's say you would like to add a secondary positive vibration that
reduces to 6. Add a 3 to the existing 3 (3 + 3 = 6). **Place a 3 inside
the front door** to your home or office or condo and start benefitting
from the fortunate secondary influence of a 6 address in your life.

Keep in mind, the dominant address vibration will still be 12 (which
reduces to 3). However, now you have diluted the influence of this
challenging address number by placing a 3 inside the front door, thus
creating a *new* secondary positive influence of number 6.

[]{#ch11.xhtml}

## []{#ch11.xhtml#page_178 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 11]{.f3} {#ch11.xhtml#ch11 .h2n}

## REPEATED NUMBERS AND LETTERS: A MAGNIFICATION IN YOUR LIFE {.h2t}

[A]{.dropcap}[NY DOUBLE LETTER IN A NAME OR DOUBLE NUMBER IN A BIRTHDAY
OR CURRENT CYCLE MAGNIFIES THE ENERGY]{.f3}, creating an intensity that
needs to have a way to resolve. This is a good thing---a call to action
to step up in your area of expertise or area of learning. Either way,
you are expanding your influence on your life.

Your birth name and current name (which can often differ from your
birth-certificate name) may carry additional unique qualities. Let's
look now at intensifications---the impact of numbers or letters that are
repeated---a powerful magnification of a lesson and message.

::: group
### []{#ch11.xhtml#page_179 .pagebreak}DOUBLE LETTERS, INITIALS, LETTER INTENSIFICATIONS {.h3}

Intensifications in names come in three forms:
:::

1\. Letters that are doubled within a single name.

2\. Initials in which the same letter is repeated.

3\. A higher than average occurrence of a specific letter in our name.

If you are born with an intensification in your birth name, it has a
lifelong impact. If it occurs in a current name that you have chosen,
the impact lasts while you use that name.

1\. A double letter appears when you have *two consecutive letters
within one name that are the same*. For example my last name,
"Gabrielle," has a double L. The name "Mado**nn**a" has a double N,
"Brad Pi**tt**" has a double T, "Eckhart To**ll**e" has a double L,
"D**ee**pak Chopra" has a double E, "E**mm**a Thompson" has a double M,
and "Joh**nn**y De**pp**" has both a double N and a double P.

2\. Another way that a letter can carry a deep impact on your life is
when *any of the letters in your initials are repeated*. Examples of
this are **H**ay **H**ouse and **H**oward **H**ughes (HH) (HH),
**W**ayne **W**. Dyer (WWD), **D**aniel **D**ay-Lewis (DDL), **S**teven
**S**pielberg and **S**usan **S**arandon (SS), **C**alvin **C**oolidge
(CC), **R**onald **R**eagan and **R**obert **R**edford (RR), and
**M**arilyn **M**onroe (MM).

3\. The final way a letter carries a deeper impact is when it appears
*more often than average* in your *birth* name. If you have more than
the average of letters in any group, that is an intensification.

Here is the average number of times each letter family appears in a
given birth-certificate name:

+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [A, J,      | [NUMBER 1          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF THREE       |
| S]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIMES.]{.f3}                      |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [B, K,      | [NUMBER 2          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF ONE         |
| T]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIME.]{.f3}                       |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [C, L,      | [NUMBER 3          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF ONE         |
| U]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIME.]{.f3}                       |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [D, M,      | [NUMBER 4          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF ONE         |
| V]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIME.]{.f3}                       |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [E, N,      | [NUMBER 5          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF THREE       |
| W]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIMES.]{.f3}                      |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [F, O,      | [NUMBER 6          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF ONE         |
| X]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIME.]{.f3}                       |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [G, P,      | [NUMBER 7          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF ZERO        |
| Y]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIMES.]{.f3}                      |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [H, Q,      | [NUMBER 8          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF ZERO TO ONE |
| Z]{.f3}     | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIME.]{.f3}                       |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+
| [I, R]{.f3} | [NUMBER 9          | [APPEAR AN AVERAGE OF THREE       |
|             | LETTERS]{.f3}      | TIMES.]{.f3}                      |
+-------------+--------------------+-----------------------------------+

::: group
#### []{#ch11.xhtml#page_180 .pagebreak}**EXAMPLE:** {.h4}

Oprah Winfrey has both a birth name and current name that have more than
an average of amount of number 7 letters:
:::

Her current name, O**p**rah Winfre**y**, has one P and one Y---for a
total of two (zero to one is average in the G, P, Y category).

Her birth name, O**p**rah **G**ail Winfre**y**, has a G, P, and Y---for
a total of three! In fact, her birth name reflects all three letters in
this G, P, Y number 7 category!

1\. Write down your name given at birth.

2\. For each of the nine categories, write down how many times a letter
from that category appears in your birth-certificate name.

3\. If the number is higher than average, read the section for that
letter below.

4\. If you have a missing letter in a category (like you don't have any
F, O, or X in your birth name, so are missing the category resonating to
number 6), read the following section on "Missing Letters" in this
chapter.

::: group
### MEANING OF DOUBLE LETTERS, INITIALS AND INTENSIFICATIONS {.h3}

*Be sure to read the meaning of each individual letter you are affected
by in [chapter 6](#ch06.xhtml#ch06) as well to get an in-depth
understanding of that letter's influence on your life*.
:::

::: group
#### **A, J, S (NUMBER 1)** {.h4}

You must stay active! Your mind is filled with ideas, and movement to
fulfill your goals is vital for your well-being. When you feel
stimulated by a project you can go for it with boundless energy
reserves. You know how to start but not necessarily how to complete
(unless you have other prominent letters or initials that signify
completion). You can make decisions quickly---and if you don't, you will
feel out of sorts. You have the courage to stand up for yourself and are
very independent. Leadership fits you like a glove. When you can express
your highly innovative and original ideas, you are most happy. Guard
against self-centeredness, arrogance, single-mindedness to the point of
excluding others, and aggression.
:::

::: group
#### **B, K, T (NUMBER 2)** {.h4}

You know how to cooperate and often provide a soothing peaceful presence
for others. You are highly sensitive (which can easily get your feelings
hurt). For this reason you want to be accepted and liked by others and
[]{#ch11.xhtml#page_181 .pagebreak}may go beyond your comfort zone to
please. Practice not taking criticism personally and focusing on the
facts, not your worries or fears. Receiving emotional reassurance, even
through human touch (a hug, the holding of your hand), imbues you with
joy and confidence. You may need a partner to feel comfortable moving
forward, unless you have a strong presence of number 1 or 8 letters in
your birth name. You can adapt easily to people and change.
:::

::: group
#### **C, L, U (NUMBER 3)** {.h4}

You are very artistic and must have a way to express yourself
creatively. Explore all there is to explore regarding writing, music,
dance, or art. You crave creating something with your life that brings
beauty and joy and uplifts others in some way. You tend to be romantic.
Guard against distractions and spending time on frivolous things. You
may have a tendency to scatter your creative energy by focusing on too
many endeavors. Your natural sweet nature and childlike qualities may at
times turn into childishness---this is when you act irresponsibly and
don't stick to your daily routines and goals. You like to talk or
write---it's your way of sharing feelings. Watch overspending without
regard to a set budget.
:::

::: group
#### **D, M, V (NUMBER 4)** {.h4}

You actually enjoy work and have tremendous self-discipline. People can
rely on you to deliver. Manifestation and implementation are your gifts.
Having a plan, schedule, or routine suits you well. You tend to
overprepare so as not to loose control---including spending an
inordinate amount of time getting ready for a social occasion. Try not
to get to caught up in the details. Also guard against rigidness. Having
an achievement or goal to focus on will allow you not to get stuck in a
rut, as you might lock yourself into a relationship or career that is no
longer elevating your life. Keep your life flowing and be open to new
ideas and different ways of seeing things. Family is important to you.
:::

::: group
#### **E, N, W (NUMBER 5)** {.h4}

Change and adapting to new conditions is natural for you. You are fun
loving and need your freedom above all else. You enjoy traveling and
being in the media spotlight. If you don't have a project to focus on,
you can get restless and be prone to irritability. You are very sensual
and need an outlet for your natural sensuality. Guard against
multitasking and losing the original thread of your daily or overall
goal. When you feel passionate []{#ch11.xhtml#page_182 .pagebreak}about
something---whether it is a product or performance---you know how to
"sell" it to anyone no matter what your profession is. Be sure to
exercise so you can release some of your restless energy. You have an
innate sense of humor---use it to see the humor in all of life.
:::

:::

::: group
#### []{#ch11.xhtml#page_183 .pagebreak}**F, O, X (NUMBER 6)** {.h4}

You are devoted to family and love to nurture others. You are highly
sensitive to energy and aesthetics and feel best when your environment
is beautiful and the relationships in your life are all harmonious.
Disharmony will distract you from your mission to love and uplift with
grace and gratitude. Being of service is a natural for you; however, you
must guard against giving too much at the expense of your own
well-being. Having a secure, lovely home is vital to your
happiness---you love to decorate and make everything beautiful. Be
careful about taking control to the point of meddling in other people's
lives.
:::

::: group
#### **G, P, Y (NUMBER 7)** {.h4}

This intensification enhances your ability to analyze and research
subjects with great depth and beyond any boundaries. Your concentration
goes a long way in allowing you to understand and retain knowledge.
Practicing some kind of meditation is important for your well-being. You
may get too "into your head"---the abstract entices you yet needs to be
balanced with heart-centered feelings---trust your intuition! You like
to ask a lot of questions (which may irritate others) and need alone
time to process your tangential discoveries. Guard against isolating
yourself and coming off as a "know-it-all." Due to your highly sensitive
nature, any enhanced substances (drugs, alcohol) are not recommended.
Your highly distinct body of work has the potential to transform people.
:::

::: group
#### **H, Q, Z (NUMBER 8)** {.h4}

You are highly motivated to accomplish a body of work that brings you
influence and financial security. You have a very strong will, and your
powerful aura has a major impact on people when you walk into a room.
Guard against overpowering others and coming off as authoritarian, or
being impatient and judgmental with those who are slower to understand.
You desire to make a change in the world---be sure to pay attention to
changing yourself as well. You do best when in a leadership position and
can leave behind a lasting legacy. You desire quality and will strive to
secure the highest possible outcome. Overcoming obstacles strengthens
your resolve to succeed.
:::

[]{#ch11.xhtml#page_184 .pagebreak}*"If you are born with an
intensification in your birth name, it has a lifelong impact. If it
occurs in a current name that you have chosen, the impact lasts while
you use that name."*

::: group
#### **I, R (NUMBER 9)** {.h4}

You love to serve from a place of unconditional love and wisdom.
Clearing old cobwebs---past patterns of behavior and outdated
paradigms---is your specialty. You reach beyond personal love---and
activate universal compassion. Forgiveness is one of the keys to your
inner peace and happiness. You are a humanitarian, sharing resources and
being of service for a higher purpose. Guard against wanting to "save
the world" and helping others at the expense of dissipating your own
energy and resources. You have an innate artistic nature and must have a
way to create and use your powerful imagination.
:::

### MISSING LETTERS {.h3}

In [chapter 2](#ch02.xhtml#ch02) you learned how to assign each letter
in your given birth name to a number. Did you happen to notice if there
was any number from 1 to 9 that was missing? Most people do not have all
nine numbers represented in their birth name. If you notice one or more
numbers that are not represented, check out the meaning of your missing
number below.
:::

First, turn to your birth name again. Assign each letter to the
corresponding number.

[PYTHAGOREAN SYSTEM]{.f3}

::: land100
![Image](./f0184-01.jpg){#f0184-01}
:::

[]{#ch11.xhtml#page_185 .pagebreak}If you are missing a number, discover
the effect it may have on your life---and how you have been given a
wonderful opportunity for growth in this area! Also, keep in mind, if
one of the numbers missing in your name is prominent in your Birth Code
(Day of Birth or Life Purpose Number), the impact is greatly lessened or
even completely negated.

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 1** {.h4}

Missing the 1 vibration is unusual and indicates you can be more
interested in others' welfare than in yourself. You will be prompted to
assert yourself, be courageous, be more independent, and make your own
decisions. You have a naturally lovely nature and must stand your ground
when around strong-willed people.
:::

Don't waste any energy on what others may think of you. Be
self-confident and promote yourself. Trust in your ability to make good
judgments. Have the courage to act on your strong convictions.

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 2** {.h4}

Missing the 2 vibration indicates you must practice cooperating with
others as you refine your listening skills. Being tactful and caring and
exhibiting the utmost patience are often required in order to come to a
resolution or be able to proceed. You may need to stay in the background
and learn to be part of a team. Be sensitive to other people's emotional
states and needs.
:::

You will find yourself in situations where patience, peace of mind,
conflict resolution, and attention to details are required in order to
achieve your goals.

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 3** {.h4}

Missing the 3 vibration can indicate your lack of experience with fun
and spontaneous creativity. Lightening up and seeing the humor in life
will allow your inner child to express your innate joy and passion. You
truly yearn to freely express your happiness in all that you say and do,
so use your imagination without placing any boundaries! Focus on staying
positive---you are here to explore how to play. Do things "just for the
fun of it."
:::

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 4** {.h4}

Missing the 4 vibration means you need to establish a methodical and
disciplined approach to your life. Structure is vital to your success.
Otherwise you will feel like you are drifting, and results will be
fleeting and few. If you []{#ch11.xhtml#page_186 .pagebreak}focus and
use discipline you will be able to master your gifts at the highest
levels. Apply yourself through diligent work. A combination of
concentration and order will enable you to express and foster your
natural talents.
:::

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 5** {.h4}

Missing the 5 vibration is seldom found in Western names, since letters
E and/or N are usually present. You may have a dislike of crowds and a
desire to be left alone. Learn to embrace change. Adapting to new
circumstances will be important in your life. Guard against being rigid
and inflexible. Trust and have faith. You will learn a great deal
through experience and embracing freedom. Communicating your thoughts
and feelings needs to be practiced.
:::

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 6** {.h4}

Missing the number 6 may mean committing to long-term relationships is
more challenging. You need to learn to show your true emotions. You may
need to take on extra family responsibilities, which broaden your
understanding of responsibility and nurturing. You may feel isolated and
lonely yet not understand why. Instead of being guarded in your
relationships, open up your heart, and you will discover the magic of
feeling deep compassion and love.
:::

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 7** {.h4}

Missing the 7 vibration means you may not naturally want to look more
deeply at issues or understand the "why" and "hows" of life. Your
interest in underlying motives and reasons or asking questions to get
more information is not as strong. You may be less cautious than others
and less prone to analyze. One of your lessons is to have faith and to
trust. At times you may not to trust yourself and others. You are here
to rediscover the power of your immortal soul and to trust that Source
is your home.
:::

::: group
#### **MISSING NUMBER 8** {.h4}

Missing the 8 vibration means you are highly independent. The number 8
can, surprisingly, be missing even in the names of highly successful
people. No 8s can signify less strain about finances in the long run and
more support coming from others who will step in and help you achieve
your goals. Or you may just not make financial abundance and power a
major focus in your life. You are less likely to want to take a leading
role.
:::

::: group
#### []{#ch11.xhtml#page_187 .pagebreak}**MISSING NUMBER 9** {.h4}

Missing the 9 is rare and means you are learning about human nature and
may be asked to feel more compassion, tolerance, and understanding for
others. Experiences will ask you to expand your heart-center and connect
and engage emotionally. You have great potential to influence your own
destiny and the destiny of others once you stop withholding energy to
help people.
:::

::: group
### SHAPE OF LETTERS---STRAIGHT, CURVED, OR COMBINATION? {.h3}

Each letter in the alphabet forms an image. This image is drawn with
either straight lines, curved lines, or a combination of both. Most
people have two or three initials---the first letters of their names. As
you know, every letter is also a number with a powerful symbolic
meaning. But what about the shape of the first letters of your name? The
image of your initials reveals even more about your disposition and
approach to life.
:::

Now we will delve deeper into the sacred geometry of letter images,
since they reveal hidden information about the quality of every
letter---and how it affects your life.

**The first letter of each of your names is always capitalized. This
brings extra attention, and thus the impact and influence on your life
is enhanced as well.**

Are the first letters of your names both curved and straight? For
example, the letters B, G, J, and R have both curves *and* straight
lines.

Or are all the letters straight lined only, such as M, T, A, and Y?

Or do you have capital letters that are all curved, like the letters S,
O, and C?

::: group
#### **15 STRAIGHT-LINE LETTERS** {.h4}

[AEFHIKLMNTVWXYZ]{.big1}

Straight-lined initials give you an intense ability to *focus on your
goals*.
:::

Many accomplished athletes have this combination. Having only
straight-line initials means you are more stubborn and
rigid---single-mindedly focused on your goals. You like to be perfect.
You have the discipline and drive to accomplish any task you set your
mind on.

::: group
#### []{#ch11.xhtml#page_188 .pagebreak}**4 CURVED-LINE LETTERS** {.h4}

[COSQ]{.big1}

Shows flexibility and openness. You are multitalented. However, you can
get distracted more easily. You are highly creative and must have a
consistent outlet for self-expression.
:::

::: group
#### **7 COMBINATION CURVED AND STRAIGHT-LINE LETTERS** {.h4}

[BDGJPRU]{.big1}

Combination letters bring balance, flexibility, and focus---all in one
package.
:::

These letters give you the ability to see all sides. Many politicians
have this combination so they can appease a broader group of followers
and get elected. For the same reasons, high-profile Hollywood stars and
musicians benefit from this combination as well.

::: group
### DIFFERENCE BETWEEN YOUR BIRTH AND CURRENT NAME {.h3}

In [chapter 2](#ch02.xhtml#ch02) you discovered how to calculate your
birth-certificate name and arrive at your Destiny Number. You cannot
change this number---it is your Birth Code. Just as you can't change
your birthday, birth time, or birth place.
:::

(If you are adopted and your birth name is officially changed on your
birth certificate *before* 6 months of age, you will take on your new
adopted name as your Destiny Number.)

Whereas you only have one birth name, current names can change a few
times in the course of a lifetime, sometimes through marriage and other
times through choice. Many people have more than one current name---they
use a middle initial in some areas (like bank accounts or credit cards)
and not others, or they have a nickname that is used with friends and
family and another name professionally. (Remember, any time you change a
letter, add a letter, or subtract a letter your whole name frequency
changes---it is a matter of math.)

Current names are a unique, separate branch of numerology. They are
calculated using a very complex set of rules and a completely different
numerology alphabet---the Chaldean system. The impact of your current
name on your life is completely different as well. It does not describe
you in any way; however, your current name number does show how easy or
[]{#ch11.xhtml#page_189 .pagebreak}challenging it is for you to fulfill
your birth promise. There is not enough space in this book to cover the
intricate rules on how to check and change current name vibrations.
Discover all there is to know about current names, including how to
create fortunate names for personal and business use, in Discover the
"Secret Power of Your Name." Go here to learn more:
[taniagabrielle.com/name](http://taniagabrielle.com/name).

::: group
### DNA NUMEROLOGY CODES IN FAMILIES {.h3}

Once you begin playing with and paying attention to numbers, you may
notice how certain numbers appear more frequently in your life---and in
the codes for the people closest to you. This is no coincidence! All
energy aligns to similar vibrational frequencies.
:::

You can notice this often in families. There may be one number that many
family members share. Or a "family of numbers" appears over and over
again, like 3-6-9 or 2-4-8 or 1-5-7. This is a spiritual DNA numerology
code that links families to each other. I have seen each parent share a
different number with their child---for example the child has an 11/2
and 6, and one parent shares the 11/2 and the other the 6, forging a
connection. Sometimes certain children align more closely to one parent,
and you can see that in their Birth Code.

You'll notice how you will share certain numbers with your close friends
or colleagues.

[]{#ch12.xhtml}

## []{#ch12.xhtml#page_190 .pagebreak}[CHAPTER 12]{.f3} {#ch12.xhtml#ch12 .h2n}

## 11:11 AND OTHER NUMBER SEQUENCES {.h2t}

[M]{.dropcap}[ANY PEOPLE REPEATEDLY SEE]{.f3} **11:11** [AT UNEXPECTED
TIMES.]{.f3} Or notice patterns such as **3030** or **5566** and
sequences like **1-2-3-4** and **3-6-9**. Every number that appears in
your life is a nudge to listen---Source is engaging with you! Universal
language is expressed through symbols and numbers, so you are constantly
receiving messages from Spirit.

Take note of any sequences when you happen to see them. Once you pay
attention at the moment they catch your eye, you'll notice that codes
engage with you all day long! In our digital age the presence of numbers
opens the door to continual communication with the divine.

Let's discover how to interpret number sequences---so you can start
receiving messages from Spirit!

::: group
### []{#ch12.xhtml#page_191 .pagebreak}PATTERNS AND SEQUENCES: CREATING MOMENTUM {.h3}

*The meaning of patterns, such as 3030 or 5566, and sequences, such as
1-2-3-4 or 3-6-9*.
:::

Whenever you notice a pattern or sequence, the universe is sending you a
message. Patterns exist in nature, in geometry, in music. You can't help
but pay attention to a rhythmic pattern, color code, or number's
sequence---your mind is being elevated and your soul inspired to listen.

In [chapters 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03) and [4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04) you
discovered the meaning of each individual digit from 1 through 9 and the
Master Numbers (11, 22, 33, etc.). Keeping the meanings of these numbers
handy, let's look at a few common sequences and patterns that will help
you decipher future sightings with ease.

::: group
#### **CONSECUTIVE NUMBERS SEQUENCES** {.h4}

Whenever you see a consecutive numbers sequence, such as 1--2--3--4 or
2--4--6--8 or 9--8--7, *momentum* is generated. Momentum is a powerful
call to action. Movement creates direction---thus a sequence is always
moving somewhere.
:::

Any sequence can be continued, sometimes in both directions! So, when
you notice a sequence, you are being called to **follow through** on an
idea, insight, project, or conversation---whatever has been appearing in
your life at the moment that you see the sequence needs your passionate
devotion and supreme attention.

When the number sequence **rises upwards**, as in 4--7--10--13, you are
gathering steam, lifting into a higher vibration, getting *energized*.
Looking at the first and last number in the particular sequence
**4**--7--10--**13**, notice that the sequential pattern is created as
the numbers rise up by a count of 3---symbolizing creativity,
self-expression, and joy. Look even closer and notice the first and last
numbers in this pattern---4 and 13. Number 13 can be reduced to a "root
number" of 4 (13 = 1 + 3 = 4). So the number 4 figures at the beginning
*and* end of this 4--7--10--13 sequence, and that means an
intensification of the number 4 must also be taken into account.

4 stands for getting organized, making a step-by-step plan, implementing
a more disciplined approach, and thinking outside the box---while
maintaining boundaries. In this case the *rising* nature of the sequence
inspires you to take your **creative self-expression** and apply it to
an endeavor that makes you **happy** while making sure you **follow
through with a plan of action that brings security and stability.** This
will enable your life to *rise up* to a higher level of well-being. As a
result, a greater fulfillment naturally propels your goals and energizes
you.

::: f0008-01.jpg|f0012-01.jpg|f0070-01.jpg|f0084-01.jpg|f0124-01.jpg|f0143-02.jpg|f0143-06.jpg|f0143-11.jpg|f0143-25.jpg|f0143-26.jpg|f0143-27.jpg|f0143-28.jpg|f0143-33.jpg|f0143-35.jpg|f0143-37.jpg|f0148-01.jpg|f0160-01.jpg|f0166-01.jpg|f0182-01.jpg|f0192-01.jpg|f0208-01.jpg|f0208-02.jpg|f0208-03.jpg|f0208-04.jpg
[]{#ch12.xhtml#page_192
.pagebreak}![Image](./f0192-01.jpg){#f0192-01}
:::

[]{#ch12.xhtml#page_193 .pagebreak}When the number sequences **go
downwards**, as in 27--25--23, you are pivoting in a new direction and
changing course in some way as a result of letting go of a past idea,
behavior, or decision. So pay attention to insights, synchronicities,
and clues on how you are to proceed next. A downward motion indicates
the energy is slowing down to help you gain wisdom about what has
transpired. This "relaxing" of energy allows you to take a moment to
breathe and reflect so you can make an inspired, informed decision on
how to proceed. A falling sequence is a call to review and
release---readying you vibrationally so you are energized for the next
lift off!

This is very similar energy to when a planet is retrograding in
astrology. Once you know the meaning of the number or planet that is in
a "reflect and review" motion, you can recognize, assimilate, and apply
it into your life with greater ease and grace.

In the example 27--25--23, the numbers are falling by a value of 2. Make
note of this whenever there is a pattern. Number 2 adds an important
message to the story line, of bringing something into balance,
communicating with another, and creating harmony and peace through
cooperation, sensitivity, and kindness.

All sequences indicate movement in a very clear direction. Make sure
that you assimilate and interpret ...

1\. The meanings of the individual numbers

2\. The value number of the sequence (is it going up or down by 1, 2, 3,
etc.?)

3\. The upwards or downwards direction message

If the numbers rise or fall without a discernable pattern, such as
5--7--11, note the direction of the sequence (rising or falling) and
read the specific meanings of the numbers involved.

::: group
#### **SEQUENCES THAT MOVE IN BOTH DIRECTIONS** {.h4}

Occasionally you will see a sequence that is composed of an up **and** a
down numerical pattern.
:::

For example, 5, 2, 8, 3, 11, 4.

In this case there is a 5-8-11 pattern merged with a 2-3-4 pattern.
Since both individual sequences are moving upwards, this would still be
considered mainly a rising sequence with some additional downward
"release and review" energy added.

::: group
#### []{#ch12.xhtml#page_194 .pagebreak}**REPEATED NUMBER PATTERNS** {.h4}

Whether one single number repeats two or more times (such as 555, 77,
660, 3388) or the repeated numbers are embedded around or within other
numbers (as in 3**77**2, **88**4, 1**99**80), repeated number patterns
create an *intensification* of a specific number. Its corresponding
meaning is always enhanced and very significant to you.
:::

Intensifications are clearly designed to grab your attention through
repetition! Anything you experience more than once has a greater
likelihood to stick.

When you notice a repetition of any number, first look up what the
meaning of that number is. If the pattern is defined but just one
number, such as in 555, 88, or 220, then look up the meaning of the
digit, and you'll get a clear message of how one area in your life is
being intensified. (Remember that 0 is not a value; however, 0 will
enhance any sequence or pattern.)

If you notice a repetition of the number 555, for example, it is an
indication of change, a possible unexpected turn of events, a quick
decision, and an invitation to take that risk, be more adventurous, and
explore greater freedom and independence. On the other hand, seeing
multiples of 8, such as 88, places a strong emphasis on gaining more
courage, stepping into leadership, focusing on manifesting abundance,
paying attention to financial flow, overcoming obstacles, or manifesting
your vision.

When you see an intensification of a number while it is embedded with
one or more other numbers, look at the meaning of the repeated number
first. Then check the meaning of all other numbers (that are not doubled
up) to add an additional layer of understanding.

Going back to our 555 example: If the pattern is changed to 5554, then
the overall freedom and adventure experience is the most important, with
an added message that in claiming independence and taking a risk, you
will ultimately also experience security, plus the process may require
greater and more meticulous attention to detail.

In another example, the difference in changing 88 to 2880 means your
financial abundance or big vision is expanded through one-on-one
communication, relationships, and creating more balance in some area in
your life.

As you begin "speaking the language" of the single digits ([chapter
3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)) and the double-digit Master Numbers ([chapter
4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04)), you'll discover a wonderful new modality, a
language of the soul. Decisions will be easier, insights instantaneous,
and inspiration accessible at any time. Interpreting the symbolic
language of the universe will open vaults of wisdom---answers will be
there, at your service, at all times of day and night!

::: group
#### []{#ch12.xhtml#page_195 .pagebreak}**NUMEROLOGY TRIAD SEQUENCES** {.h4}

Any combination of **1**-**5**-**7**, as in 571 or 715, including with
and without 0, such as 1750, will activate the meaning of the 1-5-7 Mind
Triad (see [chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)).
:::

Any combination of **2**-**4**-**8**, as in 482 or 824, including with
and without 0, such as 8042, will activate the meaning of the 2-4-8
Manifestation Triad (see [chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)).

Any combination of **3**-**6**-**9**, as in 693 or 936, including with
and without 0, such as 6309, will activate the meaning of the 3-6-9
Creativity Triad (see [chapter 3](#ch03.xhtml#ch03)).

::: group
### 11:11---ENTER THROUGH THE PORTAL OF TIMELESSNESS {.h3}

Most likely you've experienced seeing 11:11 on a digital clock.
Something happens in that moment---like waking up from a deep sleep,
seeing 11:11 stops you in your tracks, even for a split second, and you
feel suspended somehow. Waking from a dream can leave you feeling
bewildered ... as if you are in between two worlds, hovering. Something
is crystal clear, vividly alive for just a moment.
:::

When the double 11:11 portal appears, you may feel suspended in time---a
wondrous floating sensation of momentary timelessness. It's a connection
that is undeniable, and hard to describe, because it transcends our
human mind---it feels otherworldly. Anytime you step through a door into
another room or building or garden, you enter a new zone---literally or
symbolically your space has changed. Stepping over any *threshold*
translates into an internal *shift*.

And so it is upon witnessing the 11:11.

At the moment 11:11 appears, *you cross a threshold* and forge a
connection.

As you learned in [chapter 4](#ch04.xhtml#ch04), the number 11 is a
gateway aligning your heart with the love of God. So, anytime you
experience the 11:11, it is an open invitation from the universe, your
spiritual guides, the angelic realms, to listen up and tune in, because
a divine message---however small---is asking for your attention!

The momentary suspension when you see 11:11 hovers in "no time" (a
reminder that you are never separate from God). You feel in that instant
at **one** with the universe. There is no past, no future. All you know
is the present moment---all else is unknown---*and not important*. This
is the major gift of 11:11---that the past and future are no longer on
your mind and of interest anymore. You are set free to experience life
the way it is meant to be experienced, without worry and without
projection. True living only happens right now.

[]{#ch12.xhtml#page_196 .pagebreak}*"In our digital age the presence of
numbers opens the door to continual communication with the divine."*

You are ultimate stillness and ultimate motion at once. You are yin and
yang---everything and nothing---the ultimate expression of the 11 portal
experience.

Anytime you are witness to 11:11, it is a spiritual wake-up call to
embrace the unexpected. All inspiration comes from this unknown
space---an infinite void of pure, pulsating potential. Creation is born
in this void. Worry does not exist here---as worry is a projection of
past experiences (the known) into the present (the unknown). So 11:11
beckons you to wake up to now---where fear is nonexistent.

*The illusion of separation from divine Source ends the moment you trust
in its eternal presence in your life*.

One thing is certain: It's not possible to go back once you've crossed
the threshold. Like life or death, once you cross into another realm of
existence, your experience cannot be erased or reversed. In the same
way, the insights and illuminations, small and large, that you receive
upon seeing 11:11 leave a lasting internal awakening.

::: group
#### **11:11---GATEWAY OF LIGHT** {.h4}

The letter values of the word "light" add up to 29, which reduces to 11
(29 = 2 + 9 = 11). 11 is the number of light; 11:11 magnifies the light
of truth in your life.
:::

*When you see 11:11, light is illuminating an issue in your life,
shining the light in darkness, enlightening you with inspiration ... In
order to walk through the two pillars, you must leave everything
behind---all preconceived ideas, beliefs, suppositions, expectations,
worries, fears, the past---and embrace the only constant: eternal life
and timelessness*.

As you fully immerse your energy into now, many doors will start to
open. As you realize you are never alone, your confidence soars. You
accept your true divine origin. You feel invincible. Because you are!
You have reconnected with our true self at soul level.

There is no greater serenity. No greater joy!

All pain, sorrow, confusion, envy, anger, hatred, fear, and jealousy is
transmuted when you surrender to the 11:11 present-moment experience.

[]{#ch12.xhtml#page_197 .pagebreak}In the human experience we need
contrast to appreciate the diversity of life. Contrast allows us to
recognize and discern what we want. We need to experience loneliness to
appreciate oneness, sadness to appreciate joy, dark to recognize light,
war to choose peace, aggression to feel the gift of kindness. 11:11
reminds you: The only thing that matters is that you are connected to
**all** of life as an expression of divinity itself. There is no
judgment in this place of love. No good or bad. There is just life
itself ... the passion for living fully.

Even as others may still judge you (and you them), you are set free of
personalizing their issues with you when you live in this eternal
space---and you will not take their judgments to heart. Your heart is
now cleansed, as you begin to realize that judgment is only a projection
born of ignorance---a lack of understanding. No one can cross the
threshold with you; no one has walked in your shoes.

*11:11 reminds you that you are an eternal flame, and to yourself only
shall you be true. Let others be. Love them, forgive them, be kind to
them---but you focus only on how you can rise to any occasion. A life of
rising is a life lived fully and exquisitely*.

::: group
#### **11:11---A CALL TO ACTIVATE ABUNDANCE** {.h4}

Engaging consistently with your internal light (through your living soul
code and your guides) is how you access and *activate abundance*.
:::

If you are self-conscious and not actually fully present, you're only
half aware---pretending to be fully there. Yes, you can function---you
can answer, you can respond---but you are not fully tuned into your
heart and soul through *intentional listening*.

When you open up completely, with no strings attached---stepping through
the 11 gateway by risking everything to be fully present---**you unlock
the secret key of abundance**.

Abundance manifestation cannot be separated from the rest of your life.
Many find this concept challenging ... *What you do and feel and say
every day is how you do and say and feel about everything else*. 11:11
invites you to play like a child would, to explore and enjoy the act of
creating your life every moment of your day. To live in prosperity, with
joyful anticipation, the internal and external must align. Your feelings
and intentions must be in sync---be *one* and the same. This is the key
to money manifestation. Clear all your resistance and emotional debris,
and you create room for the universe to bring you abundant gifts.

Abundance follows your *energy*.

[]{#ch12.xhtml#page_198 .pagebreak}If you don't feel in balance with
money, in harmony with financial flow, you cannot easily generate it.
Inner fulfillment enriches you on all levels.

In this beautiful space fear is magically absent. You can't get attached
to the past or worry about future outcomes when you are totally engaged
with what's in front of you. 11:11 is a reminder of your constant
connection to Source.

All the abundance you could ever imagine already exists. The universe is
*expanding* constantly. There is no lack of good fortune and prosperity.
Reset your inner palate to vibrate at a highly positive frequency and
watch your natural, childlike passion create magical outcomes.

::: group
#### **DECODING 11:11---CREATING CONSCIOUS MANIFESTATION** {.h4}

A mathematical view of 11:11 reveals more about this profound spiritual
activation:
:::

**11:11 = 2 + 2 = 4**

2 is the number of balance, peace, connection, tenderness, sensitivity,
and awareness. 2 represents loving communication with another. It can be
two people, or you and an entity, or an intimate conversation as you
listen to guidance from your inner voice, your intuition. In its highest
expression, 2 facilitates communication with the divine realms.

2 + 2 represents the lines of communication between you and the
universe. The first 2 is you listening to your intuition, and the second
2 is you experiencing a connection with Spirit.

Adding the single-digits of 11:11 results in the number 4 (1 + 1 + 1 + 1
= 4). 4 is the symbol of making your ideas real---manifestation into
physical reality. Thus embedded in every 11:11 experience is the urge to
*make your inspirations manifest*. You are consciously applying the
subtle message (received in a moment of timeless suspension) ... into
action.

Think of it another way. When you are engaged in an activity that
fulfills you to the core, time flies, right? You're in love with what
you are creating or doing, and it's as if time doesn't exist at all.
Now, imagine if you could bring that quality to your everyday life. When
you live every moment with conscious awareness, no matter how mundane it
may seem to you at the time, and you engage fully with the task at hand
or the person you are talking to, then division and separation end. You
stop feeling divided, torn, and incomplete.

11:11 says to you: The universe has your back! The force is with you!
Take charge of this moment!

::: group
#### []{#ch12.xhtml#page_199 .pagebreak}**11:11 MEDITATION** {.h4}

Trusting your hunches is inspiration, being one with Spirit. Inspiration
means "in spirit."
:::

In these fast-paced and hectic times, the volume of information we need
to navigate day in and day out is astonishing. We are inundated with
news, sounds, interruptions, endless to-do lists and distractions---an
overload of stimuli overwhelming our nervous systems. Being too
stimulated can get you out of sync, exhausted, and unfocused, and then
it's easy to get ungrounded, untethered, and imbalanced. You'll know
right away, because you start to take things *personally*. Emotional
overwhelm results in partaking in unnecessary drama, as you separate
from Source only to feel alone, unsupported, and unloved.

When you find yourself in this state, invoke the 11:11 code.

\* Visualize the 11:11 on a big screen in front of you (choose a serene
color). or write 11:11 down on a piece of paper.

\* Inhale deep, long breaths for a few minutes while visualizing the
11:11 code.

\* Enter the 11:11 portal.

Now set the following intentions:

1\. I am open to embracing the unexpected and seeing opportunity
everywhere.

2\. I am totally present.

3\. I completely trust that everything occurring in my life is always
for my highest good and the highest good of others.

Feel free to visualize and set your intention while listening to
beautiful music. (I recommend classical music, as its beauty and
complexity naturally take you into heavenly spheres.) Bask your heart
and soul in your vision as you enter through the timeless 11:11 portal.

Now you are *one* with the universe. You can *play*!

Connect this way with Spirit anytime, anywhere.

11:11 is a tool, helping you create an *instantaneous moment of
illumination*.

Walk through the 11:11 gateway with no agenda ... only a pure intention
to embrace joy. *Now you are receptive to divine inspiration and can
fill your cup until it runneth over!*

When you open up to endless possibilities---risking all to be
present---you unlock the secret to abundance and bliss.

You're now in manifestation mode!

Now go and manifest money, miracles and magic!

Keep aligning with Source through your soul code, listen for intuitive
prompts, and always be guided by love.

## []{#author.xhtml#page_203 .pagebreak}ABOUT THE AUTHOR {#author.xhtml#author .h2d}

Wealth astro-numerologist and psychic Tania Gabrielle introduced the
merging of two ancient divination arts---astrology and numerology---to
the Western world. Renowned as a gifted channel, Tania unlocks the codes
in the stars, names, and numbers to facilitate wealth and well-being. In
decoding each person's birth promise and forecast map, Tania guides her
clients to claim their true destiny and divine mission. Her primary
focus is on teaching spiritual principles that manifest practical,
real-life results.

Tania has been featured and quoted in the *New York Times*, the *Los
Angeles Times, USA Today, Entertainment Weekly, ESPN Magazine, Essence
Magazine*, [ESPN.com](http://ESPN.com), [Yahoo.com](http://Yahoo.com),
and *US Magazine*. She has appeared as an expert in two
documentaries---*Quantum Communication* and *The Voice*. Tania is also a
gifted classical composer, with her music performed worldwide in the
most prestigious concert halls by Grammy Award--winning artists.

As founder and creator of Numerology Academy, the first online
certification course in astro-numerology, Tania continues to guide
thousands of students around the globe who, in turn, help others to
create extraordinary lives.

Visit her at **[TaniaGabrielle.com](http://TaniaGabrielle.com)**.
